	I2-Se-Kiat	(26)
[1]	Tng saN-chap8--ni5, si3-geh8 chhoe-gou7, goa2 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 e5 ho5-piN, siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan; hit-si5 thiN khui, goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 iN7-siong7.  2). Ti7 hit-geh8 e5 chhoe-gou7, chiu7-si7 Iok-nga2-kun ong5 siu7-liah8 e5 te7-gou7 ni5,  3). ti7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7, Ka-pa-lou2 e5 ho5-piN, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 tiau5-ti5 lim5-kau3 Pou3-se e5 kiaN2, che3-si I2-se-kiat; ti7-hia Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7.  4). Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3, li2 khoaN3, u7 kong5-hong tui3 pak-hng lai5, u7 toa7 phian3 hun5, u7 iam7-iam7-sih e5 he2, i e5 chiu-ui5 u7 kng, tui3 hit tiong-kan e5 he2-lai7 hoat-chhut chhin-chhiuN7 hou2-phek e5 sek-ti3.  5). Koh tui3 hit tiong-kan chhut-hian7 si3 e5 oah8-mih8 e5 heng5-siong7.  In e5 khoan2-sit si7 an2-ni; u7 lang5 e5 heng5-siong7.  6). Tak8-e5 u7 si3 e5 bin7, tak8-e5 u7 si3 ki sit8.  7). In e5 kha si7 tit8-tit8, kha-jiah-toe2 chhin-chhiuN7 gu5-a2 e5 kha-toe5; long2 chhan3-lan7 chhin-chhiuN7 boa5-kng e5 tang5 e5 chhiah-bak8.  8). Ti7 in si3-bin7 e5 sit8-e7 koh u7 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chit e5 si3 e5 oah8-mih8-e5 bin7 kap sit8 chiu7-si7 an2-ni;  9). in e5 sit8 long2 saN-lian5-chiap; kiaN5 e5 si5, seng-khu m7-bian2 oat8, long2 tit8-tit8 chin3-cheng5 khi3.  10). Lun7-kau3 in e5 bin7 e5 heng5-siong7, in u7 lang5 e5 bin7; in si3-e5 ti7 chiaN3-peng5 u7 sai e5 bin7, in si3-e5 ti7 to3-peng5 u7 gu5 e5 bin7; in si3-e5 ia7 u7 eng-chiau2 e5 bin7.  11). In e5 bin7 si7 an2-ni; in e5 sit8 tui3 teng2-bin7 thi2-khui; chit-e5 hit-e5 nng7 e5 sit8 saN-lian5, koh u7 nng7 e5 sit8 kham3 seng-khu.  12). In tak8-e5 tit8-tit8 kiaN5 chin3-cheng5; sin5 beh khi3 toh-loh8, in chiu7 khi3 hia; kiaN5 e5 si5, seng-khu m7-bian2 oat8.  13). Lun7-kau3 oah8-mih8 e5 khoan2-sit, in e5 heng5-siong7 chhin-chhiuN7 toh8 e5 he2-thoaN3, koh chhin-chhiuN7 he2-pe2 e5 heng5-siong7, khi2-khi2 loh8-loh8 ti7 oah8-mih8 e5 tiong-kan; he2 chin kng, tui3 he2-tiong hoat-chhut sih-na3.  14). Hiah e5 oah8-mih8 chau2-khi3 chau2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3 teh sih.  15). Goa2 teh khoaN3 oah8-mih8 e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, u7 chhia-lun5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, ti7 oah8-mih8 e5 piN-a2, chiau3 i e5 si3-bin7.  16). Chhia-lun5 kap in e5 choe3-hoat e5 khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 ng5 e5 gek8 e5 sek-ti3; si3 e5 lun5 e5 heng5-siong7 siang7 chit8-khoan2; in e5 khoan2-sit kap choe3-hoat si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lun5-tiong u7 lun5.  17). Lun5 kiaN5 e5 si5, si3-bin7 long2 oe7 kiaN5--tit; kiaN5 e5 si5 m7-bian2 oat8.  18). Lun7-kau3 chhia-lun5 e5 khoan5 si7 chin-koaiN5 thang kiaN; si3 e5 lun5 e5 khoan5 u7 bak8-chiu moa2-moa2.  19). Oah8-mih8 kiaN5 e5 si5, lun5 ia7 ti7 in e5 sin-piN teh kiaN5; oah8-mih8 ku2-khi2 li7-khui toe7 e5 si5, lun5 ia7 ku2-khi2.  20). Sin5 sou2 beh khi3 e5 sou2-chai7, in ia7 khi3; sin5 na7 khi3 ti7-hia, lun5 ia7 ti7 in e5 sin-piN ku2-khi2; in-ui7 oah8-mih8 e5 sin5 ti7 lun5 e5 lai7-bin7.  21). Hiah-e5 na7 kiaN5, chiah-e5 ia7 kiaN5, hiah-e5 na7 theng5, chiah-e5 ia7 theng5; hiah-e5 na7 ku2-khi2 li7-khui toe7 e5 si5, lun5 ia7 ti7 in e5 sin-piN ku2-khi2; in-ui7 oah8-mih8 e5 sin5 ti7 lun5 e5 lai7-bin7.  22). Oah8-mih8 e5 thau5-khak e5 teng2-bin7 u7 kiong-chhong e5 heng5-siong7, khoaN3-liau2 chhin-chhiuN7 thang-kiaN e5 chui2-chiN e5 sek-ti3, phou ti7 in e5 thau5-khak e5 teng2-bin7.  23). Ti7 kiong-chhong e5 e7-bin7 in e5 sit8 thi2 tit8-tit8, tai7-ke saN-tui3; koh u7 nng7 ki sit8 kham3 i e5 seng-khu e5 chit-peng5, ia7 koh u7 nng7 ki sit8 kham3 i e5 seng-khu e5 hit-peng5.  24). In kiaN5 e5 si5, goa2 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 sit8 e5 siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 siaN, u7 hoa7-hoa7-jiong2 e5 siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 kun-tui7 e5 siaN; in theng5 e5 si5, sit8 chiu7 pang3--loh8-lai5.  25). Ti7 in thau5-khak-teng2 kiong-chhong e5 teng2-bin7 u7 siaN; in theng5 e5 si5, sit8 chiu7 pang3--loh8-lai5.  26). Ti7 in thau5-khak-teng2 kiong-chhong e5 teng2-bin7 u7 po2-cho7 e5 heng5-siong7, chhin-chhiuN7 lam5-sek e5 po2-chioh8; ti7 po2-cho7 heng5-siong7 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 heng5-siong7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit.  27). Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 tui3 i e5 io e5 heng5-siong7 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 hou2-phek e5 sek-ti3, ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7 chiu-ui5 u7 he2 e5 heng5-siong7; ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 tui3 i e5 io e5 heng5-siong7 e5 e7-bin7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 e5 heng5-siong7 chiu7-ui5 chin-kng.  28). Ti7 loh8-hou7 e5 jit8 hun5-tiong kheng7 e5 heng5-siong7 chaiN2-iuN7, chiu-ui5 e5 kng e5 heng5-siong7 ia7 si7 an2-ni.  Goa2 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih; koh thiaN-kiN3 chit8-ui7 kong2-oe7--e5 e5 siaN.

[2]	I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 khi2-lai5 khia7, Goa2 beh kap li2 kong2-oe7.  2). I tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, sin5 chiu7 jip8 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7, hou7 goa2 khia7--khi2-lai5; goa2 chiu7 thiaN-kiN3 hit-ui7 tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7--e5 e5 siaN.  3). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, Goa2 chhe li2 khi3 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 chok8, kau3 poe7-gek8 e5 pang-kok, in si7 poe7-gek8 Goa2 e5; in kap in e5 liat8-chou2 ui5-keh8 Goa2, tit8-kau3 kin-a2-jit8.  4). Chiah e5 kiaN2 bin7-phe5 kau7, sim ngi7; Goa2 chhe li2 khi3 in hia; li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2.  5). In kiam2-chhai2 thiaN, kiam2-chhai2 m7-thiaN, (in-ui7 in si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke), beh chai ti7 in tiong-kan tek-khak bat u7 sian-ti.  6). Jin5-chu2 ah, sui-jian5 u7 chhau2-chhi3 chit8-le5 ti7 li2 hia, koh li2 tiam3 ti7 giat-a2-thang5 e5 tiong-kan, long2 boh8-tit kiaN in, ia7 boh8-tit kiaN in e5 oe7; in sui-jian5 si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke, iau2-ku2 boh8-tit kiaN in e5 oe7, ia7 boh8-tit in-ui7 in e5 bin7-mau7 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5.  7). In kiam2-chhai2 thiaN, kiam2-chhai2 m7-thiaN, li2 choe3 li2 chiong Goa2 e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2; in-ui7 in si7 kek8-ki5 poe7-gek8 e5.  8). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN Goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7; li2 m7-thang poe7-gek8, chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 poe7-gek8 e5 ke; li2 tioh8 khui-chhui3, chiah8 Goa2 sou2 hou7 li2 e5.  9). Hit-si5 goa2 khoaN3, khoaN3 ah, u7 chit8 ki chhiu2 chhun ng3 goa2 chia lai5; khoaN3 ah, chhiu2-lai7 u7 chit8 kng2 chheh;  10). I chiong hit pun2 hian-khui ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; lai7-goa7 long2 u7 sia2-ji7; hi2 teng2-bin7 sou2 sia2-e5 u7 ai-siong, thou2-khui3, chai-e7 e5 oe7.

[3]	I chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, tioh8 chiah8 li2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5; tioh8 chiah8 hit kng2 chheh, ia7 tioh8 khi3 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 ke kong2-oe7.  2). Tui3 an2-ni goa2 khui-chhui3, I chiu7 hou7 goa2 chiah8 hit-kng2.  3). Koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, chiong chit-kng2, Goa2 sou2 hou7 li2 e5, tioh8 chiah8 ti7 li2 e5 pak-tou2, chhiong-moa2 li2 e5 tng5.  Goa2 chiu7 chiah8 i; chhui3-lai7 chai i e5 tiN chhin-chhiuN7 bit8.
	4). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, khi2-lai5 chiu7-kun7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 ke, ia7 eng7 Goa2 e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2.  5). In-ui7 li2 hong7-chhe m7-si7 khi3 hit e5 kong2-oe7 chhim-o3, gian5-gu2 oh--tit thiaN e5 peh-siN3 hia, chiu7-si7 khi3 I2-sek-liat8 ke;  6). m7-si7 khi3 hiah e5 kong2-oe7 chhim-o3, gian5-gu2 oh--tit thiaN e5 choe7-choe7 kok, in e5 oe7 li2 boe7 hiau2-tit thiaN.  7). Goa2 na7 chhe li2 khi3 in hia, in tek-khak thiaN li2.  Chong2-si7 I2-sek-liat8 ke m7-kheng2 thiaN li2, in-ui7 m7-kheng2 thiaN Goa2; in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke si7 thau5-hiah8 teng7, sim ngi7 e5 lang5.  8). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 hou7 li2 e5 bin7 ngi7, ti2-tek8 in e5 bin7; hou7 li2 e5 thau5-hiah8 teng7, ti2-tek8 in e5 thau5-hiah8.  9). Goa2 hou7 li2 e5 thau5-hiah8 chhin-chhiuN7 soan7-chioh8, pi2 he2-chioh8 khah-teng7; in sui-jian5 si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke, li2 boh8-tit kiaN in, ia7 boh8-tit in-ui7 in e5 bin7-mau7 lai5 kiaN-hiaN5.  10). I koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, Goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, li2 tioh8 eng7 sim seng5-siu7, eng7 hi7-khang thiaN.  11). Li2 tioh8 khi3 chiu7-kun7 pun2-kok siu7-liah8 e5 peh-siN3 hia; in kiam2-chhai2 thiaN, kiam2-chhai2 m7-thiaN; li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2-oe7, ka7 in kong2, Che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2.
	12). Hit-si5 sin5 ku2-khi2 goa2, goa2 chiu7 thiaN-kiN3 ti7 goa2 e5 ka-chiah-au7 u7 toa7 tin2-tang7 hu7-hu7-hau2 e5 siaN, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tui3 I e5 sou2-chai7 hian2-chhut, eng-kai tit-tioh8 o-lo2.  13). Goa2 ia7 thiaN-kiN3 hiah e5 oah8-mih8 e5 sit8 saN-khap8-tioh8 e5 siaN, kap in e5 sin-piN lun5 e5 siaN, chiu7-si7 toa7 tin2-tang7 hu7-hu7-hau2 e5 siaN.  14). Tui3 an2-ni sin5 ku2-khi2 goa2, toa3 goa2 khi3; goa2 khi3 chin kan-khou2, sim-sin5 kek-liat8; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 ti7 goa2 sin-chiuN7 chin u7 lat8.  15). Goa2 chiu7 kau3 The-lek8-a-pit, tiam3 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 ho5-piN siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 hit-ui7, kau3 in sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7; ti7 in tiong-kan che7 chhit-jit8 ku2, tiam3 hia chin gong5-ngiah8.
	16). Ke3 chhit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2, kong2,  17). Jin5-chu2 ah, Goa2 siat-lip8 li2 choe3 I2-sek-liat8 ke siu2-bang7 e5 lang5; sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 thiaN Goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2-kong2--e5, thoe3 Goa2 keng2-kai3 in.  18). Goa2 tui3 phaiN2-lang5 kong2, Li2 tek-khak oe7 si2; na7 li2 bo5 keng2-kai3 i, bo5 eng7 oe7 keng2-kai3 phaiN2-lang5 hou7 i li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7, lai5 kiu3 i e5 siN3-mia7; chiu7 hit e5 phaiN2-lang5 beh si2 ti7 i e5 choe7; chong2-si7 Goa2 beh tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2 tho2 i e5 siN3-mia7.  19). Siat-su2 li2 keng2-kai3 phaiN2-lang5, ia7 i bo5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2 sou2-kiaN5 kap i e5 phaiN2-lou7, chiu7 i beh si2 ti7 i e5 choe7; chong2-si7 li2 u7 kiu3 li2 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7.  20). Koh siat-su2 u7 gi7-lang5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui i e5 gi7 lai5 hoan7-choe7, Goa2 ia7 he7 that-gai7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7 i beh si2; in-ui7 li2 bo5 keng2-kai3 i, chiu7 i beh si2 ti7 i e5 choe7, koh i sou2 u7 kiaN5 e5 gi7 bo5 koh tit-tioh8 ki3-liam7; chong2-si7 Goa2 beh tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2 tho2 i e5 siN3-mia7.  21). Chong2-si7 li2 na7 keng2-kai3 gi7-lang5, hou7 gi7-lang5 bo5 hoan7-choe7, i na7 chin-chiaN3 bo5 hoan7-choe7, chiu7 tek-khak tit-tioh8 oah8, in-ui7 i u7 siu7 keng2-kai3; li2 iah8 kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 ti7-hia he7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7; I tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 khi2-lai5, khi3 piN5-iuN5, Goa2 beh ti7-hia kap li2 kong2-oe7.  23). Tui3 an2-ni, goa2 khi2-lai5, chhut-khi3 kau3 piN5-iuN5; khoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng khia7 ti7-hia, chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 ho5-piN sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 eng5-kng chit8-iuN7; goa2 chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih.  24). Sin5 chiu7 jip8 goa2 e5 lai7-bin7, hou7 goa2 khia7--khi2-lai5; I kap goa2 kong2-oe7; tui3 goa2 kong2, Khi3 ah, li2 tioh8 ka-ki7 koaiN ti7 chhu3-lai7.  25). Jin5-chu2 ah, lang5 beh eng7 soh he7 ti7 li2 e5 sin-khu, ka7 li2 khun2-pak8; ti3-kau3 li2 boe7 chhut-khi3 lai5 kiaN5 ti7 in tiong-kan.  26). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 chih8 liam5 ti7 li2 e5 chiuN7-kiuN, ti3-kau3 li2 e2-kau2, boe7 oe7 choe3 chek-pi7 in e5 lang5; in-ui7 in si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke.  27). Tok8-tok8 kau3 Goa2 kap li2 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Goa2 beh khui li2 e5 chhui3, li2 chiu7 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ai3 thiaN--e5 thiaN, m7 thiaN--e5 ku3 i m7-thiaN; in-ui7 in si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke.

[4]	Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 theh8 chit8 te3 chng, he7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siaN5 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7.  2). Koh ui5-khun3 kong-kek--i, khi2 thou5-tui kong-kek--i, ti7 si3-ui5 an-siat toa7-thui5 kong-kek--i.  3). Koh tioh8 theh8 thih-pan2, he7 ti7 li2 kap siaN5 e5 tiong-kan, chun2-choe3 thih-chhiuN5; li2 e5 bin7 tiaN7-tiaN7 ng3--i, chiu7 siaN5 siu7 ui5-khun3, li2 beh ui5-khun3 i.  Che thang choe3 tiau7-thau5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 ke.
	4). Li2 tioh8 khi to3-peng5 to2-teh, tam-tng I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 choe7; chiau3 li2 khi to3-peng5 to2--teh e5 jit8 joa7-choe7, li2 tam-tng in e5 choe7 ia7 si7 an2-ni.  5). Goa2 chiong in hoan7-choe7 e5 ni5 hou7 li2 eng7 jit8 e5 siau3-giah8 lai5 ti2--i, chiu7-si7 saN-pah kau2-chap8 jit8; li2 chiau3 an2-ni tam-tng I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 choe7-koa3.  6). Li2 i2-keng moa2 chiah e5 jit8, tioh8 koh khi chiaN3-peng5 to2-teh, tam-tng Iu5-tai7 ke e5 choe7-koa3, Goa2 ka7 li2 han7 si3-chap8 jit8, chit8-jit8 ti2 chit8-ni5.  7). Sou2-i2 li2 e5 bin7 tioh8 tiaN7-tiaN7 ng3 siu7 ui5-khun3 e5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, chhiu2-kut lek8 theh-theh, soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek--i.  8). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh eng7 soh he7 ti7 li2 e5 sin-chiuN7; ti3-kau3 li2 boe7-oe7 hoan ke3-peng5, kau3 li2 ui5-khun3 siaN5 e5 jit8 moa2.  9). Li2 tioh8 theh8 sio2-beh8, toa7-beh8, tau7-a2, ang5-tau7, soe2-a2, kap chhou-beh8, toe2 ti7 chit8 e5 khi3-ku7-lai7; ui7-tioh8 pun2-sin eng7--i lai5 choe3-piaN2, chiau3 li2 to2 than2-khi e5 jit8 e5 siau3-giah8, chiu7-si7 saN-pah kau2-chap8 jit8, li2 tioh8 chiah8--i.  10). Li2 sou2 chiah8 e5 sit8-but8, tioh8 chiau3 chhin3-tang7, tak8-jit8 chiah8 ji7-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chiau3-si5 lai5 chiah8.  11). Li2 lim chui2 iah8 tioh8 chiau3 niu5, tak8-jit8 chit8-him e5 lak8-hun7-chit8; chiau3-si5 lai5 lim.  12). Li2 chiah8 chit e5 piaN2, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 toa7-beh8-piaN2 chit8-iuN7; tioh8 eng7 lang5 sou2 pang3 e5 pun3, pek--i ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 Goa2 sou2 koaN2 in kau3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong, iah8 tek-khak an2-ni chiah8 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 piaN2.  14). Goa2 kong2, Ai ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 peng5-sou3 be7-bat bak-tioh8 la5-sam5, tui3 soe3-han3 kau3-taN, be7-bat chiah8 ka-ki7 si2--e5, a2-si7 hou7 ia2-siu3 thiah-lih8--e5; hit e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 bah, iah8 be7-bat jip8 goa2 e5 chhui3.  15). Tui3 an2-ni I tui3 goa2 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 hou7 li2 eng7 gu5-sai2 lai5 thoe3 lang5 e5 pun3; li2 tioh8 chiong li2 e5 piaN2 pek ti7 hit teng2-bin7.  16). I koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 toan7-choat8 in sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 bi2-niu5; in chiah8-piaN2 tioh8 chiau3 chhin3, chun2-chat lai5 chiah8; lim chui2 iah8 tioh8 chiau3 niu5, gong5-ngiah8 lai5 lim.  17). Hou7 in khiam3-kheh piaN2 kap chui2, saN-kap gong5-ngiah8, koh ti7 in e5 choe7-koa3 lai5 siau-biat8.

[5]	Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 kiah8 chit8 ki lai7-kiam3, choe3 li2 e5 thi3-thau5-to, lai5 thi3 li2 e5 thau5-mng5 kap li2 e5 chhui3-chhiu; jian5-au7 eng7 li5-teng2 teng2 i e5 tang7-khin, lai5 pun i.  2). Ui5-khun3 siaN5 e5 jit8 i2-keng moa2, li2 tioh8 chiong saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 ti7 siaN5-lai7 eng7 he2 sio--i; chiong saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 eng7 to phah--i; chiong saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 ia7-soaN3 hou7 hong chhe--khi3; Goa2 iah8 beh puih8 to tui-jip--i.  3). Li2 tioh8 tui3 hi2 tiong-kan theh8 kui2-na7 ki, pak8 ti7 li2 e5 saN-a2-ku.  4). Koh tui3 hi2 tiong-kan theh8 tam7-poh8-a2, hiat ti7 he2-tiong, eng7 he2 sio--i; tui3 hia beh u7 he2 chhut, kau3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke.
	5). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Che si7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2; Goa2 beh an-ti3 i ti7 liat8-pang-tiong, liat8-kok ti7 i e5 si3-ui5.  6). I kiaN5 phaiN2 ui5-keh8 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, pi2 liat8-pang khah siong-tiong7; kan-hoan7 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7 pi2 si3-ui5 e5 liat8-kok khah-chham2; in-ui7 i khi3-sak Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, Goa2 e5 lut8-le7 in iah8 bo5 chun-than3.  7). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: In-ui7 lin2 jiau2-loan7 pi2 lin2 si3-ui5 e5 liat8-pang khah siong-tiong7, bo5 chun-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, bo5 chip-siu2 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, iah8 m7-than3 lin2 si3-ui5 liat8-kok e5 hoat-tou7.  8). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh kong-kek li2, Goa2 beh ti7 lin2 tiong-kan sim2-phoaN3 lin2, hou7 liat8-kok chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3.  9). Koh in-ui7 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, Goa2 beh ti7 li2 tiong-kan kiaN5 Goa2 sou2 be7-bat kiaN5, i2-au7 iah8 bo5 koh an2-ni kiaN5--e5.  10). In-ui7 an2-ni, ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan, lau7-pe7 beh thai5 kiaN2 lai5 chiah8, kiaN2 iah8 beh thai5 lau7-pe7 lai5 chiah8; Goa2 beh ti7 lin2 tiong-kan sim2-phoaN3 lin2.  Goa2 beh chiong li2 sou2 chhun e5 cheng3-lang5, long2 si3-soaN3 in ti7 si3-hng.  11). In-ui7 an2-ni, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, ui7-tioh8 li2 eng7 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8, thang iam3-chian7 e5 su7, phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, Goa2 ia7 beh kiam2-chio2 li2 e5 lang5-giah8; Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu bo5 beh thiaN3-sioh li2, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh lin5-bin2 li2.  12). Li2 saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 beh tui3 un-ek8 lai5 si2, iah8 tui3 ki-hng lai5 siau-biat8 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan; saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 beh ti7 li2 e5 si3-ui5 to2 ti7 to-e7; saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 Goa2 beh si3-soaN3 in ti7 hiah e5 hong; iah8 beh puih8-to tui-jip in.  13). Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 tit-tioh8 chiaN5, Goa2 toa7 siu7-khi3 in e5 beh soah, Goa2 chiu7 siu7 an-ui3; koh Goa2 toa7 siu7-khi3 in-e5 i2-keng chiaN5, chiu7 in thang chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 jiat8-sim lai5 kong2--e5.  14). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 choe3 leng2-cheng7, choe3 leng5-jiok8, ti7 li2 si3-ui5 e5 liat8-pang-tiong; hou7 keng-ke3 e5 lang5 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3.  15). An2-ni, Goa2 beh eng7 siu7-khi3, kap toa7 siu7-khi3, kap giam5-giam5 e5 chek-pi7, ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan sim2-phoaN3 li2; hit-si5 li2 chiu7 ti7 si3-ui5 e5 liat8-pang-tiong, chiaN5-choe3 thang leng5-jiok8, thang ki-chhi3, thang kam3-kai3, thang gong5-ngiah8; che si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  16). Hit-si5 Goa2 eng7 ki-hng oe7 chau5-biat8 lang5 e5 phaiN2-chiN3 sia7 in; chiu7-si7 Goa2 sou2 sia7 lai5 chau5-biat8 lin2--e5; Goa2 iah8 beh ke-thiN lin2 e5 ki-hng, toan7-choat8 lin2 sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 bi2-niu5.  17). Koh beh ki-hng ok-siu3 kau3 lin2 hia, in beh hou7 lin2 e5 kiaN2 si2-liau2-liau2; koh un-ek8 kap thai5 lang5 e5 su7 iah8 beh liu5-heng5 ti7 lin2 hia; Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 lin2; che si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[6]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 bin7 ng3 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN, lai5 tui3 i soan-thoan5, kong2, I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN ah, tioh8 thiaN Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7;  3). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 toa7-soaN, sio2-soaN, chui2-kau, soaN-kok, an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2, Goa2 beh eng7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 lin2, iah8 beh hui2-biat8 lin2 e5 soaN-thau5-toaN5.  4). Lin2 e5 che3-toaN5 tek-khak hong-hoe3, lin2 e5 jit8-thau5 e5 thiau7 beh tu2-tioh8 phah-chhui3; Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 to2 ti7 lin2 ngou2-siong7 e5 bin7-cheng5.  5). Goa2 iah8 beh chiong I2-sek-liat8 chok8 e5 sin-si he7 ti7 in e5 ngou2-siong7 e5 bin7-cheng5; chiong lin2 e5 kut-thau5 si3-koe3 hiat ti7 lin2 e5 toaN5 e5 si3-ui5.  6). Ti7 lin2 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, siaN5 beh pha-hng, soaN-thau5-toaN5 beh hong-hoe3; hou7 lin2 e5 che3-toaN5 pha-hng hong-hoe3, lin2 e5 ngou2-siong7 phah-chhui3 biat8-bo5, lin2 e5 jit8-thau5 e5 thiau7 beh chho3-loh8, lin2 e5 sou2-choe3 long2 hoe3-bo5.  7). Siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 beh to2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan; chiu7 lin2 beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  8). Lin2 si3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-kok e5 si5, Goa2 beh ti7 liat8-pang-tiong sou2 chhun e5 lang5 hou7 i thoat-li7 to-kiam3.  9). Lin2 tiong-kan tit-tioh8 thoat-li7 e5 lang5, beh ti7 in siu7 liah8-khi3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong ki3-liam7 Goa2; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hui2-hoai7 in im5-loan7 li7-khui Goa2 e5 sim, i2-kip8 in loan5-ai3 ngou2-siong7 e5 bak8-chiu; in beh ui7-tioh8 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, lai5 ka-ki7 oan3-hun7.  10). In beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Goa2 kong2 beh kang3 chai-e7 hou7 in, m7-si7 khang-khang e5 oe7.
	11). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 phah-chhiu2 tng3-kha, kong2, Chham2 ah, I2-sek-liat8-ke kiaN5 che it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 phaiN2-tai7; in beh tui3 to-kiam3, tui3 ki-hng, tui3 un-ek8 lai5 si2.  12). Tiam3 ti7 hng7 e5 lang5 beh tui3 un-ek8 lai5 si2; tiam3 ti7 kun7 e5 lang5 beh tui3 to-kiam3 lai5 si2; lau5--teh siu7 ui5-khun3 e5 lang5 beh tui3 ki-hng lai5 si2; an2-ni Goa2 beh it-chin7 chiaN5 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 ti7 in.  13). In siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 to2 ti7 in che3-toaN5 si3-ui5 e5 ngou2-siong7-tiong, chiu7-si7 tak8 e5 koaiN5-soaN, tak8 e5 soaN-teng2, tak8 e5 chhiN-chhiu7 e5 chhiu7-kha, tak8 e5 am7-am7 e5 siong7-chhiu7-kha, chiu7-si7 in hian3 phang-phang e5 che3-su7 hou7 it-chhe3 ngou2-siong7 e5 toe7-hng; hit-si5 lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  14). Goa2 beh chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kong-kek in, hou7 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 pha-hng leng2-cheng7, tui3 khong3-ia2 kau3 Te7-pek-lah8-tha; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[7]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 I2-sek-liat8 toe7 an2-ni kong2, Kiat-kiok8 kau3 lah! chit e5 toe7 e5 si3-keng2, kiat-kiok8 kau3 lah.  3). TaN li2 e5 kiat-kiok8 i2-keng kau3 lah, Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 kau3 ti7 li2, iah8 beh chiau3 li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3 li2; chiau3 li2 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 po3-eng3 li2;  4). Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu bo5 beh po2-sioh li2, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh kho2-lin5 li2; si7 beh chiau3 li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 po3-eng3 li2, li2 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 beh kui ti7 li2 tiong-kan; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	5). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: U7 chai-e7, hui-siong5 e5 chai-e7; khoaN3 ah, beh kau3 lah.  6). Kiat-kiok8 kau3 lah, kiat-kiok8 kau3 lah, khi2-lai5 kong-kek li2; khoaN3 ah, kau3 lah.  7). Keng2-lai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 chai-e7 beh lim5-kau3 li2; si5-ki5 kau3 lah, jit8-chi2 kun7 lah, chiu7-si7 hoa7-hoa7-jiong2, m7-si7 soaN-teng2 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN e5 jit8.  8). Goa2 beh kin2-kin2 piaN3-chhut Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 li2; koh it-chin7 chiaN5 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 ti7 li2, chiau3 li2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3 li2, chiau3 li2 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 po3-eng3 li2.  9). Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu bo5 beh po2-sioh li2, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh kho2-lin5 li2, beh chiau3 li2 e5 sou2 kiaN5 po3-eng3 li2, li2 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 beh kui ti7 li2 tiong-kan; lin2 chiu7 chai phah-lin2--e5 si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  10). KhoaN3 ah, khoaN3 ah, jit8-chi2 i2-keng kau3 lah; sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 chai-e7 i2-keng hoat-chhut; koaiN2-a2 i2-keng khui-hoe, kiau-ngou7 i2-keng puh-ge5.  11). Kiong5-po7 heng-khi2, chiaN5-choe3 heng5-hoat8 phaiN2 e5 koaiN2-a2; in bo5--khi3, in cheng3-lang5 iah8 bo5--khi3, in e5 chai5-po2 ia7 bo5--khi3; in tiong-kan bo5 lang5 tit-tioh8 chun-kui3.  12). Si5-ki5 kau3 lah, jit8-chi2 kun7 lah; boe2 e5 lang5 boh8-tit hoaN-hi2, boe7 e5 lang5 boh8-tit hoan5-lo2; in-ui7 toa7 siu7-khi3 i2-keng kau3 ti7 in cheng3-lang5.  13). Boe7--e5 in sui-jian5 iau2 oah8--teh, ia7 boe7 to3-tng2 kau3 i sou2 boe7--e5; in-ui7 chit e5 iN7-siong7 koan-he7 in cheng3-lang5, long2 boe7 to3-tng2-lai5; iah8 bo5 lang5 oe7 tui3 i e5 phaiN2 sou2-kiaN5 lai5 kian-kou3 i e5 oah8-mia7.  14). In i2-keng pun5 sau3-kak, pi7-pan7 chiau5-pi7; chong2-si7 bo5 lang5 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3; in-ui7 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 lim5-kau3 in cheng3-lang5.  15). Ti7 goa7-bin7 u7 to-kiam3, ti7 lai7-bin7 u7 un-ek8, u7 ki-hng; ti7 chhan5-ia2--e5 beh tui3 to-kiam3 lai5 si2, ti7 siaN5-lai7--e5, ki-hng kap un-ek8 beh thun-biat8--i.  16). Ki5-tiong thoat-li7--e5 beh thoat-li7; tak8-lang5 in-ui7 i e5 choe7-koa3, ti7 soaN--nih chhut pi-ai e5 siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 soaN-kok-tiong e5 ka-chui.  17). Chhiu2 long2 sng, kha-thau5-u nng2 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2.  18). Beh eng7 moa5-pou3 ha5-io, kiaN-hiaN5 beh jia-kham3 i, tak8-lang5 bin7 kian3-siau3, thau5-khak bo5 poaN3-ki mng5.  19). In beh hiat in e5 gun5 ti7 koe-lou7, khoaN3 kim chhin-chhiuN7 u3-oe3 e5 mih8; tng Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7-khi3 e5 jit8, in e5 kim-gun5 boe7-oe7 kiu3 in, boe7-oe7 hou7 in e5 sim ti-chiok, iah8 boe7-oe7 hou7 in e5 pak-tou2 pa2; in-ui7 che u7 poaN3-to2 in ti7 choe7-ok tiong.  20). Lun7-kau3 i chng-thaN7 e5 sui2, si7 I hou7 i tit-tioh8 ui-hong; in chiu7 eng7--i lai5 chng thang oan3-hun7 e5 mih8, thang iam3-chian7 e5 ngou2-siong7; sou2-i2 Goa2 hou7 in khoaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 u3-oe3 e5 mih8.  21). Goa2 beh chiong i kau ti7 goa7-pang lang5 e5 chhiu2, choe3 i sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8; kau-hu3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 phaiN2-lang5, choe3 chhat8-chng; in iah8 beh phah la5-sam5 i.  22). Goa2 beh oat8-tng2 Goa2 e5 bin7 bo5 khoaN3--in; in beh phah la5-sam5 Goa2 ki-bit8 e5 sou2-chai7; kiong5-beng2 e5 chhat8 ia7 beh jip8-khi3 phah la5-sam5.  23). Tioh8 cho7 thih-lian7, in-ui7 chit sou2-chai7 moa2-moa2 lau5-huih e5 choe7, siaN5-lai7 chhiong-moa2 kiong5-po7 e5 su7.  24). Goa2 beh hou7 goa7-pang te7-it phaiN2--e5 lai5 pa3-chiam3 in e5 chhu3-theh8; Goa2 beh hou7 kiong5-po7 e5 lang5 e5 kiau-ngou7 soah; in e5 seng3-sou2 phah la5-sam5.  25). Hui2-biat8 kun7 lah; in beh kiu5 peng5-an, iah8 boe7 tit-tioh8.  26). Beh u7 chai-e7 ke-thiN chai-e7, hong-siaN soa3-chiap hong-siaN; in beh tui3 sian-ti kiu5 iN7-siong7; chong2-si7 che3-si e5 lut8-hoat, tiong2-lo2 e5 ke3-ek8, long2 beh toan7-choat8.  27). Kok-ong5 beh pi-ai, ong5-chhin beh leng2-cheng7, peh-siN3 e5 chhiu2 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  Goa2 beh chiau3 in e5 sou2-kiaN5 khoan2-thai7 in, chiau3 in eng-kai siu7 e5 sim2-phoaN3, lai5 sim2-phoaN3 in; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[8]	Te7 lak8-ni5 lak8-geh8 chhoe-gou7, goa2 che7 ti7 goa2 e5 chhu3-lai7, Iu5-tai7 chiah e5 tiong2-lo2 che7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; ti7-hia Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 kau3 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7.  2). Goa2 koan-khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 u7 heng5-siong7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 e5 khoan2-sit; tui3 i e5 io i2-e7 e5 khoan2-sit u7 he2, tui3 i e5 io i2-chiuN7 e5 kng-kng e5 khoan2-sit, chhin-chhiuN7 hou2-phek e5 sek-ti3.  3). I chhun chhut chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 ki chhiu2 e5 khoan2, khiu2-tiau5 goa2 chit8-kou2 e5 thau5-mng5; sin5 chiu7 chiong goa2 ku2-khi2 kau3 thiN kap toe7 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 iN7-siong7-tiong toa3 goa2 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ng3 pak lai7-iN7 e5 mng5-khau2; ti7-hia u7 tou3-khi7 e5 ngou2-siong7 e5 cho7-ui7, chiu7-si7 kek-tong7 tou3-khi7-e5.  4). KhoaN3 ah, ti7-hia u7 I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 eng5-kng, khoan2-sit kap goa2 ti7 piN5-iuN5 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3--e5 chit8-iuN7.  5). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 kiah8-bak8 ng3 pak-hng e5 lou7 koan-khoaN3; goa2 chiu7 kiah8-bak8 ng3 pak-hng e5 lou7 koan-khoaN3; khoaN3 ah, ti7 che3-toaN5 mng5 e5 pak--si3, ti7 mng5-khau2 u7 chit8-e5 kek-tong7 tou3-khi7 e5 ngou2-siong7.  6). I koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 khoaN3-kiN3 in sou2 choe3--e5 mah? chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 ke ti7-chia sou2 kiaN5 toa7 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, hou7 Goa2 li7-khui Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 hng7-hng7? chong2-si7 li2 beh koh khoaN3, iau2 u7 koh-khah toa7 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  7). I chhoa7 goa2 kau3 iN7 e5 mng5; goa2 koan-khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 chhiuN5-piah u7 chit8-khang.  8). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 iah chhiuN5; goa2 chit8-e7 iah chhiuN5, khoaN3-kiN3 u7 chit8 e5 mng5.  9). I ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 jip8-khi3, khoaN3 in ti7 chi2 lai7-bin7 sou2 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 phaiN2-tai7.  10). Goa2 chiu7 jip8-khi3 khoaN3; khoaN3 ah, ti7 si3-bin7 e5 chhiuN5-piah, ui7 tak8-ho7 oe7 so5 e5 mih8, kap kho2-ouN3 e5 chau2-siu3, kap I2-sek-liat8 ke it-chhe3 e5 ngou2-siong7.  11). Ti7 chiah e5 siong7 e5 bin7-cheng5, u7 I2-sek-liat8 ke chhit-chap8 e5 tiong2-lo2 khia7-teh, Sa-hoan e5 kiaN2 Nga2-sat-ni5-a ia7 khia7 ti7 in tiong-kan; tak8-lang5 chhiu2 theh8 hiuN-lou5, hiuN-ian e5 phang-bi7 chheng3 chiuN7-koaiN5.  12). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 tiong2-lo2, ti7 am3-tiong, ti7 in tak8-lang5 ui7-siong7 e5 pang5-a2-lai7 sou2 kiaN5--e5, li2 khoaN3-kiN3 bo5? in-ui7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 goan2, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng li7-khui chit e5 toe7.  13). I koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 beh koh khoaN3-kiN3 in sou2 kiaN5, iau2 u7 koh-khah toa7 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  14). I chhoa7 goa2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, ng3 pak e5 mng5-khau2; khoaN3 ah, ti7-hia u7 hu7-lu2 che7--teh, ui7-tioh8 Tah-bou5-su thi5-khau3.  15). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 khoaN3-kiN3 bo5? li2 iau2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 pi2 che koh-khah kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  16). I koh chhoa7 goa2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhu3 e5 lai7-iN7; khoaN3 ah, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7-mng5, leng2-long5 kap che3-toaN5 e5 tiong-kan, iok-liok8 u7 ji7-chap8-gou7 lang5, ka-chiah ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7, bin7 ng3-tang; in ia7 ng3-tang pai3 jit8-thau5.  17). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 bo5? Iu5-tai7 ke ti7-chia kiaN5 chit e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, iau2 sng3-choe3 sio2-khoa2 mah? in ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 pian3-kiaN5 kiong5-po7, chai3-saN kek Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3; khoaN3 ah, in kiah8 chhiu7-ki he7 ti7 i e5 phiN7-cheng5.  18). In-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 iah8 beh kiaN5 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3; Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu bo5 beh thiaN3-sioh in, Goa2 ia7 bo5 beh kho2-lin5 in; in sui-jian5 ng3 Goa2 e5 hi7-khang-tiong toa7-siaN kiu5-kio3, Goa2 iu5-goan5 m7-thiaN.

[9]	I ng3 goa2 e5 hi7-khang-tiong, toa7-siaN kio3 kong2, Tioh8 kio3 hiah e5 koan2 chit e5 siaN5 e5 lang5 lai5, tak8-lang5 e5 chhiu2 tioh8 kiah8 biat8 siN3-mia7 e5 ke-si.  2). Hut-jian5 u7 lak8 e5 lang5 tui3 ng3-pak teng2 e5 mng5 hit tiau5 lou7 lai5, tak8-lang5 chhiu2 kiah8 thai5-lang5 e5 ke-si; lai7-tiong u7 chit8-lang5 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN, io--nih kui3 bak8-ou5; in jip8-khi3, khia7 ti7 tang5-toaN5 e5 piN-thau5.  3). I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 eng5-kng, pun2 ti7 ki-lou7-peng e5 teng2-bin7; taN tui3 hia chiuN7--khi3, soa2 kau3 tian7 e5 hou7-teng7, I kio3 hit e5 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN, io--nih kui3 bak8-ou5 e5 lang5 lai5.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2, Pian3-kiaN5 ti7 siaN5-lai7, chiu7-si7 pian3-kiaN5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 tiong-kan; kiN3-na7 ui7-tioh8 siaN5-lai7 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, lai5 thou2-khui3 pun5-haiN7 e5 lang5, chiu7 choe3 ki3-ho7 ti7 i e5 thau5-hiah8.  5). Goa2 e5 hi7-khang-tiong thiaN-kiN3 I tui3 ki5-u5 e5 lang5 kong2, Tioh8 te3 i pian3-kiaN5 thong-siaN5, lai5 thai5-si2 lang5; lin2 e5 bak8-chiu boh8-tit thiaN3-sioh, lin2 iah8 boh8-tit kho2-lin5 in.  6). Tioh8 it-chin7 thai5-si2 lau7-lang5, siau3-lian5 lang5, chai7-sek-lu2, eN-a2, hu7-jin5-lang5; iah8 tioh8 tui3 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 thai5-khi2; tok8-tok8 kiN3-na7 u7 ki3-ho7--e5, boh8-tit kun7-oa2 i.  Tui3 an2-ni, in chiu7 tui3 tian7-cheng5 e5 tiong2-lo2 thai5-khi2.  7). I tui3 in kong2, Tioh8 phah la5-sam5 chit keng tian7, hou7 iN7-lai7 chhiong-moa2 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5; lin2 tioh8 chhut-khi3. In chiu7 chhut-khi3, ti7 siaN5-lai7 thai5-si2 lang5.  8). In khi3 thai5 lang5 e5 si5, chhun goa2 ti7-hia; goa2 chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih, kio3 kong2, HaiN7 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chiong toa7 siu7-khi3 piaN3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kiam2 si7 beh chiong I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chin7 biat8-bo5 mah?  9). I chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke kap Iu5-tai7-ke e5 choe7-koa3 kek8-ki5 tang7; pian3-toe7 u7 lau5-huih e5 su7, moa2-siaN5 u7 oan-ong2; in-ui7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng li7-khui chit e5 toe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 teh khoaN3.  10). Sou2-i2 Goa2 e5 bak5-chiu bo5 beh thiaN3-sioh, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh kho2-lin5 in; beh chiau3 in sou2 kiaN5--e5, po3-eng3 ti7 in e5 thau5-khak-teng2.  11). KhoaN3 ah, hit e5 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN, io--nih kui3 bak8-ou5 e5 lang5, chiong chit e5 su7 he5-hok kong2, Goa2 i2-keng chiau3 Li2 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 kiaN5 lah.

[10]	Goa2 koan-khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 ki-lou7-peng thau5-khak-teng2 kiong-chhong e5 tiong-kan, chhin-chhiuN7 lam5-sek e5 po2-chioh8, chhin-chhiuN7 po2-cho7 e5 heng5-siong7 e5 khoan2-sit.  2). I tui3 hit e5 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN e5 lang5 kong2, Li2 jip8-khi3, ti7 tng2-seh8 e5 lun5 e5 tiong-kan, ki-lou7-peng i2-e7, tui3 ki-lou7-peng e5 tiong-kan theh8 toh8 e5 he2-thoaN3, moa2 nng7 chhiu2, ia7 ti7 siaN5-teng2.  Goa2 chiu7 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 i jip8-khi3.  3). Hit-lang5 jip8-khi3 e5 si5, ki-lou7-peng khia7 ti7 tian7 e5 chiaN3-peng5, hun5 chhiong-moa2 lai7-iN7.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tui3 ki-lou7-peng hia chiuN7--khi3, theng5 ti7 tian7 e5 hou7-teng7 e5 teng2-bin7; tian7 u7 hun5 moa2-moa2; hit e5 iN7 iah8 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng5-kng e5 chhan3-lan7 chhiong-moa2.  5). Ki-lou7-peng e5 sit8 e5 siaN thiaN kau3 goa7-iN7, chhin-chhiuN7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2-oe7 e5 siaN.  6). I hoan-hu3 hit e5 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN e5 lang5 kong2, Tioh8 tui3 tng2-seh8 e5 lun5 e5 tiong-kan, ki-lou7-peng e5 tiong-kan, chhu2 he2; hit-si5 i chiu7 jip8-khi3, khia7 ti7 chit8 e5 lun5 e5 piN-thau5.  7). U7 chit8 e5 ki-lou7-peng tui3 ki-lou7-peng tiong chhun i e5 chhiu2, kau3 ki-lou7-peng tiong-kan e5 he2, theh8 koa2 khi2-lai5, he7 ti7 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN e5 lang5 e5 nng7 ki chhiu2; hit-lang5 ka7 i theh8--lai5, chiu7 chhut-khi3.  8). Ti7 ki-lou7-peng e5 sit8-e7, u7 hian2-chhut lang5 e5 chhiu2 e5 khoan2.  9). Goa2 koh koan-khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 ki-lou7-peng e5 piN--thau5 si3 e5 lun5; chit e5 ki-lou7-peng e5 piN--thau5 u7 chit8 e5 lun5, hit e5 ki-lou7-peng e5 piN--thau5 ia7 u7 chit8 e5 lun5; lun5 e5 khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 ng5 e5 gek8 e5 sek-ti3.  10). Lun7-kau3 in e5 khoan2-sit, si3-e5 long2 siang5 chit8-iuN7 e5 heng5-chong7, chhin-chhiuN7 lun5-tiong u7 lun5.  11). KiaN5 e5 si5, si3-bin7 long2 oe7 kiaN5--tit, kiaN5 e5 si5 m7-bian2 oat8, thau5 ng3 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, in chiu7 te3 i kiaN5; kiaN5 e5 si5 m7-bian2 oat8.  12). In thong sin-khu, in e5 ka-chiah, in e5 chhiu2, in e5 sit8, kap lun5, si3-ui5 u7 bak8-chiu moa2-moa2; chiu7-si7 in si3-e5 sou2 u7 e5 lun5.  13). Lun7-kau3 chiah e5 lun5, goa2 hi7-khang-tiong thiaN-kiN3 kong2, Tng2-seh8--e5.  14). Tak8-e5 u7 si3 e5 bin7, thau5 chit8 e5 bin7 si7 ki-lou7-peng e5 bin7, te7-ji7 e5 bin7 si7 lang5 e5 bin7, te7-saN e5 bin7 si7 sai e5 bin7, te7-si3 e5 bin7 si7 eng e5 bin7.  15). Ki-lou7-peng long2 chiuN7--khi3; che si7 goa2 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 ho5-piN sou2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 e5 oah8-mih8.  16). Ki-lou7-peng kiaN5, lun5 iah8 ti7 piN--thau5 kiaN5; ki-lou7-peng thi2-khui sit8 tui3 toe7 chiuN7--khi3, lun5 ia7 bo5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui in e5 sin-piN.  17). Hiah-e5 theng5, chiah-e5 ia7 theng5; hiah-e5 chiuN7--khi3, chiah-e5 iah8 saN-kap chiuN7--khi3; in-ui7 oah8-mih8 e5 sin5 ti7 in e5 lai7-bin7.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tui3 tian7 e5 hou7-teng7-teng2 chhut-khi3, theng5 ti7 ki-lou7-peng e5 teng2-bin7.  19). Ki-lou7-peng chhut-khi3 e5 si5 chiu7 thi2-khui sit8, ti7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 tui3 toe7 chiuN7--khi3, lun5 iah8 ti7 in e5 sin-piN; theng5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3 tang-mng5 e5 mng5-khau3, ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, u7 I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 eng5-kng.  20). Che si7 goa2 cheng5 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 ho5-piN sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 e7-bin7 e5 oah8-mih8; goa2 chai in si7 ki-lou7-peng.  21). Tak8-e5 u7 si3 e5 bin7, tak8-e5 u7 si3 e5 sit8; in e5 sit8-e7 u7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 e5 heng5-siong7.  22). Lun7-kau3 in e5 bin7 e5 heng5-siong7, chiu7-si7 goa2 cheng5 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 ho5-piN sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 bin7; in e5 khoan2-sit, in e5 sin-the2, long2 an2-ni; long2 tak8-e5 tit8-tit8 kiaN5--khi3.

[11]	Sin5 chiu7 ku2-khi2 goa2, toa3 goa2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhu3, ng3-tang e5 tang-mng5; khoaN3 ah, ti7 mng5 e5 mng5-khau2, u7 ji7-chap8-gou7 lang5; goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 in tiong-kan u7 peh-siN3 e5 kui3-chok8, Ap-sok e5 kiaN2 Nga2-sat-ni5, kap Pi2-na2-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Pi2-lah8-the5.  2). I ka7 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, che chiu7-si7 tou5-bou5 choe7-ok e5 lang5, the5-chhiong3 phaiN2-tai7 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7.  3). In kong2, Khi2-chhu3 e5 ki5 iau2-be7 kau3, chit e5 siaN5 si7 tiaN2, goan2 si7 hit lai7-bin7 e5 bah.  4). Jin5-chu2 ah, in-ui7 an2-ni, li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5; tioh8 soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek in.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sin5 lim5-kau3 goa2, tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 kong2 an2-ni, lin2 e5 sim sou2 siuN7, Goa2 chai lah.  6). Lin2 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7 thai5-si2 choe7-choe7 lang5, hou7 sin-si moa2 koe-lou7.  7). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 sou2 he7 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-lai7 e5 si2-lang5 chiu7-si7 bah; chit e5 siaN5 chiu7-si7 tiaN2; chong2-si7 lin2 beh tui3 hit tiong-kan siu7 toa3-chhut--khi3.  8). Lin2 kiaN to-kiam3, Goa2 beh hou7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 lin2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  9). Goa2 beh tui3 hit tiong-kan chhoa7 lin2 chhut-khi3, kau ti7 goa7-pang lang5 e5 chhiu2; koh beh ti7 lin2 tiong-kan kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3.  10). Lin2 beh to2 ti7 to-e7, Goa2 beh ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kau-kai3 sim2-phoaN3 lin2; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  11). Chit e5 siaN5 bo5 beh choe3 lin2 e5 tiaN2, lin2 iah8 bo5 beh choe3 hit tiong-kan e5 bah; Goa2 beh ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kau-kai3 sim2-phoaN3 lin2.  12). Lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 lin2 bo5 kiaN5 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, iah8 bo5 sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7; chiu7-si7 than3 lin2 si3-ui5 liat8-kok e5 hoat-tou7.  13). Goa2 tu2-a2 teh soan-thoan5 e5 si5, Pi2-na2-nga2 e5 kiaN2 Pi2-lah8-the5 si2--khi3.  Goa2 chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih, toa7-siaN kio3 kong2, HaiN7 ah! Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh chiong I2-sek-liat8 e5 lang5 it-chin7 chau5-biat8 mah?
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  15). Jin5-chu2 ah, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, tui3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7, li2 e5 chhin-lang5, kap I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke, chiu7-si7 tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 chit e5 toe7 si7 hou7 goan2 choe3-giap8--e5.  16). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 sui-jian5 chhian-soa2 in hng7-hng7, ti7 liat8-pang-tiong, si3-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-kok-tiong, Goa2 iau2 beh ti7 in sou2 kau3 e5 kok, chiam7-si5 choe3 in e5 seng3-sou2.  17). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 chiah e5 peh-siN3-tiong chio-chip8 lin2, iah8 beh tui3 lin2 si3-soaN3 kau3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong chu7-chip8 lin2, koh beh chiong I2-sek-liat8 toe7 siuN2-su3 lin2.  18). In beh kau3 hia, iah8 beh tui3 in tiong-kan tu5-khi3 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 thang oan3-hun7 e5 mih8.  19). Goa2 beh hou7 in choan-it e5 sim, iah8 beh chiong sin e5 sin5 he7 ti7 lin2 e5 lai7-bin7; koh beh tui3 in e5 jiok8-the2-tiong tu5-khi3 hit-ho7 chhin-chhiuN7 chioh8 e5 sim, siuN2-su3 in hit-ho7 chhin-chhiuN7 bah e5 sim.  20). Hou7 in sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, chun-siu2 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5--i; in choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 iah8 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3.  21). Chong2-si7 sim than3 kho2-ouN3 thang iam3-chian7--e5 e5 sim hit-ho7 lang5, Goa2 beh chiau3 in sou2 kiaN5--e5 po3-eng3 ti7 in e5 thau5-khak-teng2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	22). Hit-si5 ki-lou7-peng thi2-khui in e5 sit8, hiah e5 lun5 iah8 ti7 in e5 piN-thau5; ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7 u7 I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 eng5-kng.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tui3 siaN5-tiong chiuN7--khi3, hioh ti7 siaN5-goa7 tang--si3 e5 soaN.  24). Sin5 ku2-khi2 goa2, ti7 iN7-siong7-tiong tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 sin5 toa3 goa2 kau3 Ka-lek8-ti2 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 hia; goa2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 iN7-siong7, chiu7 li7-khui goa2 chiuN7--khi3.  25). Goa2 chiu7 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chi2-si7 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 su7, long2 kong2 hou7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 thiaN.

[12]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 khia7-khi2 ti7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke-tiong; in u7 bak8-chiu thang khoaN3, iah8 m7-khoaN3; u7 hi7-khang thang thiaN, iah8 m7-thiaN; in-ui7 in si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke.  3). Sou2-i2, jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 ui7 ka-ki7 pi7-pan7 siu7 chhian-soa2 eng3-iong7 e5 mih8-kiaN7; tng-thau5 peh8-jit8 ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 lai5 chhian-soa2; koh tioh8 tui3 li2 e5 sou2-chai7 tng in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 chhian-soa2 kau3 pat8-ui7; in sui-bong2 si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke, kiam2-chhai2 tui3 an2-ni oe7 siuN7.  4). Li2 tioh8 tng-thau5 peh8-jit8, ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, toa3 li2 e5 mih8 chhut-khi3; chhin-chhiuN7 toa3 siu7 chhian-soa2 eng3-iong7 e5 mih8 chit8-iuN7; kau3 e5-hng, li2 tioh8 ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 ka-ki7 chhut-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 chhut-khi3 chit8-iuN7.  5). Li2 tioh8 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5, tui3 chhiuN5-piah iah-khang, tui3 hit khang toa3 mih8 chhut-khi3.  6). Kau3 jit8 am3, li2 tioh8 ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, pe7 ti7 keng-thau5 chhut-khi3; iah8 tioh8 ta3 li2 e5 bin7, kau3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 toe7; in-ui7 Goa2 eng7 li2 choe3 I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 tiau7-thau5.  7). Goa2 chiu7 chiau3 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 khi3 kiaN5, tng-thau5 peh8-jit8 toa3 goa2 e5 mih8-kiaN7 chhut-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 toa3 siu7 chhian-soa2 eng3-iong7 e5 mih8-kiaN7; jit8 beh am3, goa2 eng7 chhiu2 tui3 chhiuN5 iah khang; jit8 i2-keng am3, chiu7 tng in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 pe7 ti7 keng-thau5 toa3 chhut-khi3.  8). Ke3 cha2-khi2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  9). Jin5-chu2 ah, I2-sek-liat8-ke, chiu7-si7 poe7-gek8 e5 ke, kiam2 m7-bat mng7 li2 kong2, Li2 choe3 sim2-mih8 ah?  10). Li2 tioh8 in3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chit e5 khe2-si7, koan-he7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 kun-ong5, i2-kip8 in tiong-kan I2-sek-liat8 e5 choan5-ke.  11). Li2 tioh8 kong2, Goa2 choe3 lin2 e5 tiau7-thau5; goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 kiaN5, in sou2 tu2-tioh8--e5 ia7 beh an2-ni; in beh siu7-liah8 siu7 chhian-soa2.  12). In tiong-kan e5 kun-ong5 ia7 beh ti7 jit8 am3 e5 si5, pe7 mih8 ti7 keng-thau5 toa3 chhut--khi3; in beh tui3 chhiuN5 iah khang, tui3 hit khang toa3 mih8 chhut--khi3; i beh kham3 i e5 bin7, in-ui7 bak8-chiu bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 toe7.  13). Goa2 beh tiuN Goa2 e5 lo5-bang7 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7, i beh hou7 Goa2 e5 oah8-tauh tauh--tioh8; Goa2 beh toa3 i kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 toe7; i sui-jian5 si2 ti7-hia, ia7 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 toe7.  14). Chiu-ui5 it-chhe3 po2-hou7 i e5, kap i sou2 u7 e5 kun-tui7, Goa2 beh si3-soaN3 in ti7 si3-hng; ia7 beh puih8-to tui-jip in.  15). Goa2 hun-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-pang, si3-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-kok e5 si5, in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  16). Chong2-si7 Goa2 beh lau5 in kui2-na7 lang5, thoat-li7 to-kiam3, ki-hng, un-ek8, hou7 in ti7 sou2 kau3 e5 tak8-kok-tiong, kong2-khi2 in kho2-ouN3 e5 su7; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	17). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 kong2,  18). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah lai5 chiah8 li2 e5 piaN2, tioh8 kiaN-hiaN5 chun2-chat lai5 lim li2 e5 chui2.  19). Li2 tioh8 tui3 chit e5 toe7-hng e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kap I2-sek-liat8 toe7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, an2-ni kong2, In chiah8 piaN2 tioh8 chun2-chat, lim chui2 tioh8 gong5-ngiah8, in-ui7 in tiong-kan khia7-khi2 e5 cheng3-lang5 sou2 kiaN5 kiong5-po7 e5 su7, chit e5 toe7 beh hong-hoe3 sit-loh8 i sou2-u7-e5.  20). U7 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5 beh pha-hng; toe7 ia7 beh hong-hoe3; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	21). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  22). Jin5-chu2 ah, ti7 lin2 I2-sek-liat8 toe7, chaiN2-iuN7 u7 chit-ho7 siok8-gu2 kong2, Si5-jit8 ian5-chhian5, iN7-siong7 long2 bo5 eng3-giam7 ah?  23). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 chit e5 siok8-gu2 soah, I2-sek-liat8 tiong bo5 koh eng7 chit-e5 choe3 siok8-gu2; chong2-si7 li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Si5-jit8 kun7--lah, tak8 e5 iN7-siong7 e5 eng3-giam7 ia7-si7 an2-ni.  24). I2-au7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 tiong-kan, tek-khak bo5 koh u7 hu-ke2 e5 iN7-siong7, sun7 jin5-i3 e5 pok-koa3.  25). In-ui7 Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, Goa2 beh kong2, koh Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, beh eng3-giam7, bo5 koh ian5-chhian5; lin2 chit e5 poe7-gek8 e5 ke ah, Goa2 beh ti7 lin2 oah8-teh e5 jit8 lai5 kong2, lai5 chiaN5--i; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	26). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  27). Jin5-chu2 ah, khoaN3 ah, I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 lang5 kong2, I sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 iN7-siong7, si7 siok8 ti7 choe7-choe7 jit8-au7 e5 su7, sou2 kong2 e5 chham3-gu2, si7 chi2 kek8-hng7 e5 si5-ki5.  28). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 e5 oe7 bo5 chit8-ku3 u7 koh ian5-chhian5, Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, tek-khak chiaN5--i; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[13]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek I2-sek-liat8-tiong hiah-e5 teh soan-thoan5 e5 sian-ti, ka7 hiah-e5 chiau3 i ka-ki7 e5 sim-i3 lai5 soan-thoan5--e5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  3). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Hiah-e5 gong7 e5 sian-ti, in u7 chai-e7 ah, in than3 ka-ki7 e5 sim-sin5 lai5 kiaN5, peng7-bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8-hang7.  4). I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 e5 sian-ti chhin-chhiuN7 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 e5 hou5-li5.  5). Lin2 be7-bat chiuN7-kau3 phoa3-khiah e5 sou2-chai7, iah8 be7-bat ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8-ke ui5 chit8 e5 chhiuN5; thang ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8, chian3-tin7 khia7-oe7-tiau5.  6). In sou2 khoaN3-kiN3--e5 si7 hu-ke2, si7 peh8-chhat8 e5 chiam-pok; in kong2, Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5, ki5-sit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5-iaN2 chhe--in, in iau2 teh ng3-bang7 hit e5 oe7 oe7 eng3-giam7.  7). Lin2 kiam2-m7-si7 khoaN3-kiN3 hu-ke2 e5 iN7-siong7 mah? kiam2-m7-si7 kong2 peh8-chhat8 e5 chiam-pok mah? lin2 kong2, Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5, ki5-sit8 Goa2 bo5 chhe in kong2.
	8). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 sou2 kong2-e5 si7 hu-ke2, sou2 khoaN3--e5 si7 peh8-chhat8; khoaN3 ah, in-ui7 an2-ni Goa2 kap lin2 hoan2-tui3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  9). Goa2 e5 chhiu2 beh kong-kek hiah e5 khoaN3-kiN3 hu-ke2, eng7 peh8-chhat8 chiam-pok e5 sian-ti; in tek-khak bo5 siok8 ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 hoe7-tiong, bo5 ki3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 lang5-mia5-phou7; iah8 boe7 thang chin3-jip8 I2-sek-liat8 toe7; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  10). In-ui7 in iu2-hek8 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Peng5-an, ki5-sit8 bo5-u7 peng5-an; chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 khi2 chhiuN5-piah, in ka7 i chheng2 he-chui2.  11). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 hiah-e5 chheng2 he-chui2 e5 lang5 kong2, ChhiuN5 beh to2-hoai7, beh u7 tiong3-chui2 e5 toa7-hou7; toa7-phauh8 ah, lin2 tioh8 loh8--lai5, koh beh u7 toa7-hong chhe-lih8--i.  12). KhoaN3 ah, chhiuN5 to2 liau2-au7, lang5 kiam2 bo5 beh tui3 lin2 kong2, Lin2 sou2 chheng2 e5 he-chui2, taN ti7 toh-loh8?  13). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh ti7 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, eng7 kong5-hong thiah-lih8--i, ti7 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 beh u7 tiong3-chui2 e5 toa7-hou7, ia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 beh loh8 toa7-phauh8 lai5 hui2-biat8--i.  14). Goa2 beh an2-ni thiah-hui2 lin2 chheng2 he-chui2 e5 chhiuN5, thiah kau3 piN5-toe7; ti3-kau3 chhiuN5-ki lou7-hian7, chhiuN5 beh to2-hoai7; lin2 iah8 beh biat8-bo5 ti7 hit tiong-kan; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  15). Goa2 beh an2-ni chiaN5 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 hit e5 chhiuN5, kap chheng2 he-chui2 e5 lang5; iah8 beh tui3 lin2 kong2, ChhiuN5 bo5--khi3 lah, chheng2 he-chui2 e5 lang5 iah8 bo5--khi3 lah.  16). Che chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 sian-ti, in ki2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lai5 soan-thoan5; ui7-tioh8 i khoaN3-kiN3 peng5-an e5 iN7-siong7, ki5-sit8 bo5-u7 peng5-an; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	17). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 bin7 tit8-tit8 ng3 li2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 hu7-lu2, chiu7-si7 chiau3 i e5 sim-i3 lai5 soan-thoan5--e5;  18). li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek--i, kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chiah e5 hu7-lu2 u7 chai-e7 ah, in ka7 cheng3-lang5 e5 chhiu2-khiau pang5 kho3-tiam7, ka7 tak8 teng2-ho7 sin-chhai5 e5 lang5 choe3 ta3 thau5-khak e5 phe3, lai5 chhiuN2 lang5 e5 sin5-hun5! chong2-bo5 lin2 beh chhiuN2 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 sin5-hun5, ui7 li7-ek ka-ki7 kiu3 oah8 sin5-hun5 mah?  19). Lin2 ui7-tioh8 kui2-na7 pe2 toa7-beh8, kui2-na7 te3 piaN2, ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong siat-tok8 Goa2, tui3 Goa2 hiah e5 ai3 thiaN peh8-chhat8-oe7 e5 peh-siN3, lai5 kong2 peh8-chhat8, hai7-si2 hiah-e5 m7 eng-kai si2 e5 sin5-hun5, iah8 hou7 m7-eng-kai oah8 e5 sin5-hun5 oah8.  20). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 hoan2-tui3 lin2 e5 kho3-tiam7, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 eng7 lai5 chhiuN2 sin5-hun5 hou7 i pe--khi3-e5; Goa2 beh tui3 lin2 e5 chhiu2 thiah--khi2-lai5; Goa2 beh thau2-pang3 hiah e5 sin5-hun5, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 chhiuN2 e5 sin5-hun5, lai5 hou7 in pe--khi3 e5.  21). Goa2 iah8 beh thiah-lih8 lin2 hiah e5 phe3, kiu3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 thoat-li7 lin2 e5 chhiu2, bo5 koh siu7 chhiuN2 ti7 lin2 e5 chhiu2-lai7; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  22). In-ui7 hit ho7 gi7-lang5, Goa2 bo5 hou7 i siong-sim, lin2 eng7 peh8-chhat8 oe7 hou7 i siong-sim; koh lin2 kian-kou3 phaiN2 lang5 e5 chhiu2, hou7 i bo5 oat8-thau5 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2-lou7, lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8.  23). Sou2-i2 lin2 boe7 thang koh khoaN3-kiN3 hu-ke2, iah8 boe7 thang koh chiam-pok.  Goa2 beh kiu3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 thoat-li7 lin2 e5 chhiu2; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[14]	U7 kui2-na7 e5 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiong2-lo2 lai5 goa2 chia, che7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 chiu7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  3). Jin5-chu2 ah, chiah e5 lang5 i2-keng chiong in e5 ngou2-siong7 chiap-lap8 ti7 in e5 sim, koh he7 ti3-kau3 hoan7-choe7 e5 that-gai7 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Goa2 kiam2 beh hou7 i mng7 mah?  4). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 tiong-kan kiN3-na7 chiap-lap8 i e5 ngou2-siong7 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 e5 lang5, koh he7 ti3-kau3 hoan7-choe7 that-gai7 ti7 i ka-ki7 e5 bin7-cheng5, koh lai5 chiu7-kun7 sian-ti--e5, Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 i sou2 kiu5 e5 su7, beh chiau3 i e5 choe7-choe7 ngou2-siong7 lai5 in3-tap i;  5). ti3-kau3 Goa2 thang hou7 I2-sek-liat8-ke sim-lai7 ka-ki7 chek-pi7, in-ui7 in long2 ui7-tioh8 in e5 ngou2-siong7 kap Goa2 chhiN-sou.  6). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 hoe5-thau5, oat8-tng2 li7-khui lin2 e5 ngou2-siong7, oat8-tng2 bin7, boh8-tit than3 lin2 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  7). In-ui7 I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 lang5, a2-si7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong kia3-kha e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, kiN3-na7 kap Goa2 keh-tng7, chiap-lap8 i e5 ngou2-siong7 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, koh he7 ti3-kau3 hoan7-choe7 e5 that-gai7 ti7 i ka-ki7 e5 bin7-cheng5, koh lai5 chiu7-kun7 sian-ti, beh ui7 ka-ki7 e5 su7 lai5 mng7 Goa2--e5, Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh pun2-sin in3-tap i.  8). Goa2 beh ng3 hit-ho7 lang5 piN3-bin7, hou7 i choe3 lang5 e5 kam3-kai3, choe3 oe7-piN3, hou7 lang5 gong5-ngiah8; iah8 beh tui3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong chian2-tu5 i; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  9). Sian-ti na7 be5-hek8 lai5 kong2 chit8 ku3 oe7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa be5-hek8 hit e5 sian-ti; Goa2 iah8 beh chhun-chhiu2 kong-kek i; chiong i tui3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8-tiong tu5-biat8.  10). In beh tam-tng ka-ki7 e5 choe7-koa3, sian-ti e5 choe7-koa3, kap kiu5-mng7 i e5 lang5 e5 choe7-koa3, long2 si7 chit8-iuN7.  11). Thang hou7 I2-sek-liat8-ke bo5 koh kiaN5 be5-lou7 li7-khui Goa2, bo5 koh in-ui7 tak8-iuN7 e5 choe7-koa3 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7; tok8-tok8 beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  13). Jin5-chu2 ah, na7 u7 kok tui3 in e5 poe7-gek8 lai5 tek-choe7 Goa2, Goa2 iah8 chhun-chhiu2 kong-kek i, toan7-choat8 i sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 bi2-niu5, hou7 ki-hng lim5-kau3 i, tui3 in tiong-kan chian2-tu5 lang5 kap cheng-siN,  14). ki5-tiong sui-jian5 u7 Na2-a, Tan7-i2-li2, Iok-pek, chi2 saN-lang5; in chi2-u7 oe7 in-ui7 in e5 gi7 lai5 kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7 na7-tiaN7; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  15). Goa2 na7 hou7 ok-siu3 keng-ke3 hit e5 toe7 lai5 sun2-hoai7, hou7 hit sou2-chai7 hong-hoe3; in-ui7 chiah e5 siu3 e5 ian5-kou3, ti3-kau3 bo5 lang5 tui3 hia keng-ke3,  16). sui-jian5 u7 chi2 saN-lang5 ti7 in tiong-kan, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, in boe7 kiu3 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, chi2-u7 in pun2-sin tit-tioh8 kiu3 na7-tiaN7, toe7-hng iu5-goan5 hong-hoe3.  17). A2-si7 Goa2 hou7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 hit e5 toe7-hng kong2, To-kiam3 ah, li2 tioh8 keng-ke3 hit e5 toe7-hng, ti3-kau3 Goa2 tui3 in tiong-kan chian2-tu5 lang5 kap cheng-siN,  18). sui-jian5 u7 chi2 saN-lang5 ti7 in tiong-kan, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, in boe7 kiu3 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, chi2-u7 in pun2-sin tit-tioh8 kiu3 na7-tiaN7.  19). A2-si7 Goa2 hou7 un-ek8 liu5-heng5 hit e5 toe7-hng, hou7 Goa2 piaN3-chhut biat8 mia7 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, thang tui3 in tiong-kan chian2-tu5 lang5 kap cheng-siN,  20). sui-jian5 u7 Na2-a, Tan7-i2-li2, Iok-pek ti7 in tiong-kan, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 chi2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, in boe7 kiu3 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, chi2-u7 oe7 in-ui7 in e5 gi7 lai5 kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7 na7-tiaN7.  21). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ho5-hong3 Goa2 chiong Goa2 si3-hang7 e5 toa7 chai-e7, chiu7-si7 to-kiam3, ki-hng, ok-siu3, un-ek8, kang3-loh8 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, tui3 hit tiong-kan chian2-tu5 lang5 kap cheng-siN, kiam2-m7-si7 koh-khah boe7 kiu3--tit mah?  22). KhoaN3 ah, beh u7 sou2 chhun e5 lang5 lau5-teh, chiu7-si7 siu7 liah8--chhut-lai5 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, khoaN3 ah, in beh chhut-lai5 kau3 lin2 chia, lin2 beh khoaN3 in e5 sou2 kiaN5 sou2 choe3, chiu7 lin2 lun7-kau3 Goa2 sou2 kang3-loh8 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 chai-e7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 it-chhe3 kang3-loh8 ti7 in teng2-bin7 e5, beh tit-tioh8 an-ui3.  23). Lin2 khoaN3 in sou2 kiaN5 sou2 choe3--e5, beh siu7 an-ui3; chiu7 chai Goa2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 kiaN5--e5, m7-si7 bo5 ian5-kou3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[15]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, phu5-to5-chhiu7 chiu7-si7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 chhiu7-bak8-tiong e5 chit8-ki, i pi2 tak8-ho7 chhiu7 u7 sim2-mih8 khah-iaN5?  3). Kiam2 oe7 thang tui3 i chhu2 chha5-liau7 choe3 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7? a2-si7 thang eng7 i choe3 khit8-a2 lai5 tiau3 sim2-mih8 khi3-ku7 mah?  4). KhoaN3 ah, si7 hiat ti7 he2--nih choe3 he2-chha5, siang-thau5 i2-keng hou7 he2 sio-liau2, tiong-ng iah8 siu7-sio, iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7 ah?  5). KhoaN3 ah, ho2-ho2 e5 si5, siong7-chhiaN2 m7-hap8 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7, ho5-hong3 hou7 he2 sio, i2-keng phaiN2--khi3, iau2 oe7 hap8 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7 ah?  6). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5-lai7 chiah e5 chhiu7-tiong e5 phu5-to5, Goa2 sou2 kau-hu3 ti7 he2-tiong choe3 he2-chha5--e5, Goa2 iah8 beh chiau3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3.  7). Goa2 beh tui3 in piN3-bin7; in tui3 he2-tiong chhut-lai5, chong2-si7 he2 beh sio-biat8 in.  Goa2 tui3 in piN3-bin7 e5 si5, lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  8). Goa2 beh hou7 chit sou2-chai7 hong-hoe3, in-ui7 in kiaN5 tai7-chi3 lai5 hoan7-choe7; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[16]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chai i hiah e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7,  3). kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 an2-ni kong2, Li2 e5 pun2-goan5, li2 e5 chhut-si3, si7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7; A-mou5-li7 lang5 si7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, li2 e5 lau7-bu2 si7 Hek-lang5.  4). Lun7-kau3 li2 chhut-si3 e5 keng2-hong2, tng li2 chhut-si3 e5 jit8 bo5 ka7 li2 tng2-chai5; ia7 bo5 eng7 chui2 ka7 li2 soe2 hou7 li2 chheng-khi3; long2 bo5 ka7 li2 sam2 iam5, iah8 bo5 eng7 pou3 ka7 li2 pau.  5). Bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kou3 li2, ka7 li2 choe3 chiah e5 su7, lin5-bin2 li2; li2 chhut-si3 e5 jit8 hiat ti7 chhan5-ia2, si7 in-ui7 li2 hou7 lang5 iam3-ouN3.  6). Goa2 tui3 li2 hia ke3, khoaN3-kiN3 li2 ko7 ti7 li2 e5 huih-lai7, chiu7 tui3 li2 kong2, Li2 sui-jian5 ti7 li2 e5 huih-tiong, iau2-ku2 thang oah8; Goa2 sit8-chai7 tui3 li2 kong2, Li2 sui-jian5 ti7 li2 e5 huih-tiong, iau2-ku2 thang oah8.  7). Goa2 hou7 li2 tiong2-seng5, chhin-chhiuN7 chhan5--nih sou2 hoat-siN--e5, koh li2 chiam7-chiam7 chiaN5-choe3 toa7-lang5, bin7-mau7 chheng-siu3, lin phong3, thau5-mng5 tng5; chong2-si7 li2 iu5-goan5 chhiah-sin lou7-the2.  8). Goa2 tui3 li2 hia ke3, khoaN3-kiN3 li2; khoaN3 ah, hit-si5 si7 li2 heng-khi2 ai3-cheng5 e5 si5; Goa2 chiu7 eng7 saN-a2-ku kham3 li2, jia li2 e5 thng3-theh-theh; koh tui3 li2 chiu3-choa7, kap li2 kiat-iok; li2 chiu7 siok8 ti7 Goa2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  9). Hit-si5 Goa2 eng7 chui2 soe2 li2, soe2 chheng-khi3 li2 sin-the2 e5 huih, koh eng7 iu5 boah li2.  10). Goa2 hou7 li2 chheng7 siu3-hoe e5 saN, iah8 hou7 li2 chheng7 hai2-kau2 phe5 e5 oe5, iah8 eng7 iu3-toe7-pou3 hou7 li2 ha5-io; koh eng7 tiu5-toan7 choe3-saN hou7 li2 moa.  11). Goa2 eng7 chng-thaN7 e5 mih8 chng-thaN7 li2; eng7 chhiu2-khoan5 koa3 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, eng7 kim-lian7-a2 koa3 ti7 li2 e5 am7-kun2.  12). Goa2 iah8 eng7 khoan5 khoa3 ti7 li2 e5 phiN7; eng7 hi7-kau koa3 ti7 li2 e5 hi7-a2, eng7 sui2 e5 bo7 ti3 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-khak.  13). An2-ni, li2 chiu7 u7 kim-gun5 e5 chng-thaN7; sou2 chheng7--e5 si7 iu3-toe7-pou3, kap tiu5-toan7, kap siu3-hoe e5 saN; sou2 chiah8-e5 si7 iu3-iu3 e5 mi7, phang e5 bit8, kap iu5; li2 iah8 kek8-ki5 sui2, hoat-tat8 kau3 ong5-hou7 e5 chun-kui3.  14). Li2 sui2 e5 mia5-siaN thoan5 ti7 liat8-kok-tiong; si7 tui3 li2 e5 sui2 oan5-choan5, in-ui7 Goa2 u7 eng7 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng hou7 li2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). Tok8-tok8 li2 oa2-kho3 ka-ki7 e5 sui2, koh in-ui7 li2 e5 mia5-siaN, chiu7 kiaN5 im5-loan7; li2 hong3-chhiong3 im5-iok8, hou7 ke3-lou7 lang5 chhut-chai7 i e5 i3-su3 lai5 kiaN5.  16). Koh eng7 li2 e5 saN, chng-thaN7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, ngou2-sek long2 chiau5-pi7; ti7 hit teng2-bin7 kiaN5 im5-loan7; chit ho7 su7 bo5 beh lai5, iah8 bo5 koh u7.  17). Li2 iah8 chhu2 Goa2 sou2 hou7 li2 kim-gun5 sui2 e5 po2-khi3; ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 choe3 lang5 e5 siong7, kap i kiaN5-im5.  18). Koh eng7 li2 siu3-hoe e5 saN ka7 i moa, iah8 eng7 Goa2 e5 ko-iu5, Goa2 e5 hiuN-liau7, pai5 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5.  19). Koh Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 chiah8-mih8, iu3-mi7, kap iu5 kap bit8, Goa2 sou2 eng7 lai5 iuN2-chhi7 li2--e5, li2 chiu7 eng7--i, pai5 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 choe3 phang-bi7, sit8-chai7 u7 an2-ni; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  20). Koh li2 eng7 li2 e5 kiaN2 , li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 ka7 Goa2 siN--e5, lai5 hian3 hou7 in chiah8; li2 kiaN5 chiah e5 im5-loan7, kiam2 si7 sio2-khoa2 su7?  21). li2 keng2-jian5 koh thai5-si2 Goa2 chiah e5 kiaN2 lai5 kau-hu3 i, hou7 in keng-ke3 he2 lai5 kui ti7 i?  22). Li2 kiaN5 chiah-e5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 kap im5-loan7 e5 su7 long2 bo5 siuN7-tioh8 li2 soe3-han3 chhiah-sin lou7-the2, ko7 ti7 li2 huih-tiong e5 jit8.  23). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 u7 chai-e7 ah, u7 chai-e7 ah;  24). li2 kiaN5 che it-chhe3 phaiN2-tai7 i2-au7, koh ui7 ka-ki7 khi2 hoe-lau5, ti7 tak8 tiau5 koe-lou7 khi2 koaiN5-tai5.  25). Li2 ti7 it-chhe3 koe-lou7-khau2 khi2 koaiN5-tai5, hou7 li2 e5 sui2 pian3 choe3 kho2-ouN3--e5; koh kap it-chhe3 ke3-lou7--e5 choe7-choe7 kiaN5 im5-loan7.  26). Li2 iah8 kap li2 keh-piah kok, hong3-chhiong3 cheng5-iok8 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 kiaN5-im5, ke-thiN li2 e5 im5-loan7, jia2 Goa2 siu7-khi3.  27). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 chhun-chhut Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kong-kek li2; kiam2-chio2 li2 eng3-iong7 e5 mih8; koh chiong li2 kau hou7 oan3-hun7 li2 e5 Hui-li7-su7 hiah e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2, hou7 in chhut-chai7 i3-su3 khoan2-thai7 li2; in khoaN3-kiN3 li2 kiaN5 phaiN2, lai5 kian3-siau3.  28). Li2 in-ui7 houN3-sek put-ti-chiok, koh kap A-sut8 lang5 kiaN5-im5; kap in kiaN5-im5 liau2-au7, iu5-goan5 bo5 moa2-i3.  29). Li2 koh ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 kau3 Ka-lek8-ti2 kiaN5 choe7-choe7 im5-loan7, iau2-ku2 bo5 moa2-i3.  30). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 kiaN5 che it-chhe3 e5 su7, si7 pa3-seng3 im5-hu7 e5 sou2 kiaN5, kho2-kian3 li2 e5 sim si7 joa7 loan2-jiok8.  31). In-ui7 li2 ti7 it-chhe3 koe-lou7-khau2 khi2 hoe-lau5, ti7 tak8 tiau5 koe-lou7 khi2 koaiN5-tai5; in-ui7 li2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 pat8 e5 chhiong-ki, m7-tih8 chiN5.  32). Goa7! Li2 chit e5 kiaN5-im5 e5 bou2 ah, beh tih8 pat8-lang5 lai5 thoe3 tiong7-hu!  33). Lang5 si7 eng7 mih8 sang3 chhiong-ki, li2 hoan2-tng2 eng7 mih8 sang3 li2 siong-ho2 e5 lang5, chhiaN2 in tui3 si3-ui5 lai5 kap li2 kiaN5-im5.  34). Li2 e5 kiaN5-im5 kap pat8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 tui3-hoan2; in-ui7 m7-si7 lang5 chhe7 li2 kiaN5-im5, si7 li2 eng7 mih8 sang3 lang5, m7-si7 lang5 sang3 li2; sou2-i2 li2 kap pat8-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 tui3-hoan2.
	35). In-ui7 an2-ni, li2 chit e5 chhiong-ki ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7;  36). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 li2 piaN3-chhut li2 e5 u3-oe3; li2 kap li2 sou2 siong-ho2--e5 thng3-theh-theh kiaN5-im5; koh in-ui7 li2 sou2 pai3 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 ngou2-siong7, koh ui7-tioh8 sou2 lau5 li2 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 huih, chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 hian3 hou7 in--e5;  37). khoaN3 ah, in-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 beh chu7-chip8 li2 it-chhe3 siong-ho2--e5, chiu7-si7 li2 bat kap i ian3-lok8--e5, kap li2 it-chhe3 sou2 thiaN3--e5, li2 it-chhe3 sou2 oan3-hun7-e5, Goa2 beh tui3 si3-ui5 chu7-chip8 lai5 kong-kek li2, iah8 beh tui3 in lou7-chhut li2 e5 thng3-theh, hou7 in khoaN3 li2 e5 thng3-theh.  38). Goa2 iah8 beh sim2-phoaN3 li2, chhin-chhiuN7 sim2-phoaN3 kiaN5-im5 kap thai5-lang5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8-iuN7; Goa2 beh eng7 toa7 siu7-khi3 tou3-khi7, hou7 li2 lau5-huih.  39). Goa2 koh beh chiong li2 kau ti7 in e5 chhiu2, in beh thiah-hui2 li2 e5 hoe-lau5, hui2-hoai7 li2 e5 koaiN5-tai5, thng3 li2 e5 saN, chhiuN2 li2 sui2 e5 po2-khi3; lau5 li2 chhiah-sin lou7-the2.  40). In ia7 beh chhoa7 choe7-choe7 lang5 khi2--lai5 kong-kek li2, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 li2, eng7 to-kiam3 chhak8-thau3 li2.  41). Eng7 he2 sio li2 e5 chhu3-theh8, ti7 choe7-choe7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 sim2-phoaN3 li2; Goa2 tek-khak hou7 li2 bo5 koh kiaN5-im5, iah8 bo5 koh sang3 lang5 mih8.  42). An2-ni, Goa2 ng3 li2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 beh soah, Goa2 e5 tou3-khi7 iah8 beh li7-khui li2; Goa2 beh an-cheng7 bo5 koh siu7-khi3.  43). In-ui7 li2 boe7-ki3-tit li2 soe3-han3 e5 jit8, ti7 che it-chhe3 e5 su7 lai5 kek Goa2; sou2-i2 Goa2 beh chiau3 li2 sou2 kiaN5--e5, po3-eng3 ti7 li2 e5 thau5-khak-teng2; hou7 li2 bo5 koh kiaN5-im5, ke-thiN ti7 li2 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	44). KhoaN3 ah, kiN3-na7 kong2 siok8-gu2--e5, beh eng7 siok8-gu2 thoe2-thak li2, kong2, Lau7-bu2 an2-ni, cha-bou2-kiaN2 ia7 si7 an2-ni.  45). Li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 lin2 lau7-bu2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, iam3-chian7 i e5 tiong7-hu kap kiaN2-ji5; li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 lin2 chi2-be7 e5 chi2-be7, iam3-chian7 in e5 tiong7-hu kap kiaN2-ji5; lin2 lau7-bu2 si7 Hek lang5, lin2 lau7-pe7 si7 A-mou5-li7 lang5.  46). Li2 e5 toa7-chi2 si7 Sat-ma2-li7-a, i kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tiam3 ti7 li2 e5 to3-peng5; li2 e5 sio2-be7 si7 Sou2-to-ma2, i kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tiam3 ti7 li2 e5 chiaN3-peng5.  47). Li2 bo5 oh8 in e5 sou2-kiaN5, iah8 bo5 chiau3 in kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 khi3 choe3; li2 liah8 choe3 sio2-khoa2 su7, li2 it-chhe3 sou2-kiaN5-e5, pi2 in khah-chhau3.  48). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7; li2 e5 sio2-be7 Sou2-to-ma2, kap i cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, be7 u7 kiaN5 li2 kap li2 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7.  49). KhoaN3 ah, li2 e5 sio2-be7 Sou2-to-ma2 e5 choe7 si7 chit-khoan2; i kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, sim-chi3 kiau-ngou7, bi2-niu5 pa2-chiok, hiong2-siu7 an-iat8; long2 bo5 hu5-chou7 khun3-khou2 kap song3-hiong lang5 e5 chhiu2.  50). In chu7-ko, ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, Goa2 khoaN3-liau2 chiu7 chiong in tu5--khi3.  51). Sat-ma2-li7-a sou2 hoan7 e5 choe7 bo5 li2 e5 chit8-poaN3; li2 ke-thiN kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 pi2 in khah-choe7, koh tui3 li2 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, hou7 li2 e5 chi2-be7 hian2-beng5 si7 gi7.  52). Li2 ki3-jian5 toan3-teng7 li2 e5 chi2-be7 choe3-gi7, chiu7 tioh8 tam-tng li2 ka-ki7 e5 leng5-jiok8; in-ui7 li2 sou2 hoan7 e5 choe7 pi2 in khah kho2-ouN3, in chiu7 pi2 li2 khah gi7; li2 i2-keng hou7 li2 e5 chi2-be7 hian2-beng5 si7 gi7, li2 chiu7 tioh8 kian3-siau3, tam-tng ka-ki7 e5 leng5-jiok8.  53). Goa2 beh hou7 in siu7-liah8-e5 to3-tng2--lai5; chiu7-si7 hou7 Sou2-to-ma2 kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 siu7-liah8-e5, Sat-ma2-li7-a kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 siu7-liah8--e5, i2-kip8 in tiong-kan lin2 siu7-liah8--e5, long2 to3-tng2--lai5.  54). Thang hou7 li2 tam-tng ka-ki7 e5 leng5-jiok8, koh tui3 li2 it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5 hou7 in tit-tioh8 an-ui3--e5, lai5 kian3-siau3.  55). Li2 e5 chi2-be7 Sou2-to-ma2, kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, beh to3-lai5 goan5-ui7; Sat-ma2-li7-a, kap i e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, beh to3-lai5 goan5-ui7; li2, kap li2 e5 cheng3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 , iah8 beh to3-lai5 goan5-ui7.  56). Tng li2 kiau-ngou7 e5 jit8, li2 e5 chhui3 bo5 kong2-khi2 li2 e5 sio2-be7 Sou2-to-ma2,  57). hit-si5 li2 e5 phaiN2 iau2-be7 hoat-hian7, A-lan5 chiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, lian5 i si3-ui5 e5 lang5, iau2-be7 leng5-jiok8 li2; Hui-li7-su7 chiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, peng5-sou3 ti7 si3-ui5 biau2-si7 li2--e5, i ia7 be7 u7 leng5-jiok8 li2.  58). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 houN3-im5 kap kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, li2 i2-keng tam-tng lah.  59). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 poe7-iok khoaN3-khin chiu3-choa7, Goa2 beh chiau3 li2 sou2 kiaN5 lai5 khoan2-thai7 li2.  60). Chong2-si7 Goa2 beh tui-liam7 Goa2 ti7 li2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5, kap li2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok; iah8 beh kap li2 siat-lip8 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  61). Tng li2 chiap-lap8 li2 e5 chi2-be7, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 toa7-chi2 kap li2 e5 sio2-be7 e5 si5, li2 beh ki3-tit li2 sou2 kiaN5--e5 lai5 kian3-siau3; Goa2 iah8 beh chiong in hou7 li2 choe3 cha-bou2-kiaN2, tok8-tok8 m7-si7 tui3 li2 e5 iok.  62). Goa2 beh kap li2 siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, li2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  63). kau3 Goa2 sia3-bian2 li2 it-chhe3 sou2 choe3 e5 si5, li2 ki3-tit chiu7 kian3-siau3; koh in-ui7 li2 e5 leng5-jiok8, chiu7 bo5 koh khui-chhui3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[17]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 ke chhut-chhai, siat phi3-ju7;  3). kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, U7 chit8 chiah toa7 eng, sit8-kou2 toa7, sit8-be2 tng5, mng5-chhau2 chat8, u7 ngou2-chhai2-sek, pe kau3 Li7-pa-lun3, chhu2 pek-hiuN-chhiu7 tiong-ki e5 ki-be2.  4). At-chih8 i chin7 be2-liu chiN2 e5 ki, kaN5 kau3 seng-li2-tiuN5, he7 ti7 boe2-boe7 e5 lang5 e5 siaN5.  5). Koh chhu2 hit sou2-chai7 e5 cheng2, chai ti7 pui5-toe7, chhah ti7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 piN-thau5, chhin-chhiuN7 chai liu2-chhiu7.  6). Chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 toa7-chang5, chiaN5-choe3 pha-tin5 ke7-ke7 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7; i e5 ki choan2 ng3 hit chiah eng, kun ti7 i e5 e7-bin7; tui3 an2-ni chiaN5-choe3 phu5-to5-chhiu7, siN ki hoat tin5.  7). Koh u7 chit8 chiah toa7 eng, sit8 toa7, mng5 chat8, khoaN3 ah, chit e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 tui3 chai-cheng3 e5 sou2-chai7 oan i e5 kun ng3 i, hoat i e5 ki ng3 i, ng3-bang7 i koan3-ak.  8). I chai ti7 pui5-toe7, choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 piN-thau5, thang hoat-ki kiat ke2-chi2, chiaN5-choe3 ho2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7.  9). Li2 tioh8 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chit e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 kiam2 oe7 hoat-am7? eng kiam2 boe7 puih8 i e5 kun, tu5 i e5 ke2-chi2, hou7 i kou-ta5 mah? hou7 i iu3 e5 hioh8 long2 kou-ta5, ia7 m7-bian2 eng7 toa7-lat8 kap choe7-choe7 lang5 puih8-chhut i e5 kun.  10). I i2-keng chai-cheng3, kiam2 oe7 hoat-am7 mah? tang-hong chit8-e7 chhe--i, kiam2 boe7 long2 kou-ta5 mah? beh ti7 i hoat-siN e5 sou2-chai7 kou-ta5.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  12). Li2 tioh8 ka7 hit e5 poe7-gek8 e5 ke kong2, Lin2 kiam2 m7-chai chiah-e5 si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3 mah? Li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, liah8 i e5 kun-ong5 kap kui3-chok8, toa3 kau3 i Pa-pi2-lun5 hia.  13). Tui3 ong5-chhin e5 tiong-kan, keng2 chit8-lang5, kap i lip8-iok, kah i chiu3-choa7; koh liah8 kok-lai7 u7 se3-lek8 e5 lang5;  14). beh hou7 kok pi-bi5 boe7-oe7 chu7-kiong5, tok8-tok8 siu2 beng5-iok, chiu7 tit-tioh8 po2-chun5.  15). Chong2-si7 i poe7-poan7; chhe su3-chia2 khi3 Ai-kip8, ai3 in hou7 i be2 kap choe7-choe7 peng; i kiam2 oe7 heng-thong mah? kiaN5 chit ho7 su7 e5 lang5, kiam2 oe7 to5-thoat mah? kiam2 u7 poe7-iok, iau2 chau2 oe7 li7 mah?  16). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 ka-ki7 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 siat-lip8 i choe3-ong5, i keng2-jian5 biau2-si7 chiu3-choa7 e5 oe7, poe7 sou2 lip8 e5 iok; in-ui7 an2-ni, i tek-khak si2 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 sou2 tiam3 e5 sou2-chai7.  17). Tng in khi2 thou5-tui, cho7 tai5, beh biat8-bo5 choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 si5, Hoat-lo2 chhoa7 toa7 tui7 peng, kap choe7-choe7 lang5 lai5; ia7 boe7 ti7 kau-chian3-tiong pang-chan7 i.  18). I poe7-iok lai5 biau2-si7 chiu3-choa7, khoaN3 ah, i i2-keng tau5-hang5, iau2-ku2 choe3-chhut chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 su7, i tek-khak boe7-oe7 to5-thoat.  19). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, i i2-keng khoaN3-khin chi2 Goa2 sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7, poe7-biu7 chi2 Goa2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok; Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 choe7 kui ti7 i e5 thau5-khak.  20). Goa2 beh eng7 Goa2 e5 bang7 pha ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7, i beh hou7 Goa2 e5 oah8-tauh tauh--tioh8; Goa2 beh toa3 i kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5, iah8 beh ti7-hia sim2-mng7 i kan-hoan7 Goa2 e5 choe7.  21). I e5 kun-tui7-tiong to5-chau2--e5, long2 beh to2 ti7 to-e7; sou2 chhun--e5, iah8 beh si3-soaN3 ti7 si3-hng; lin2 chiu7 chai kong2 chit e5 oe7--e5, si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	22). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 iah8 beh chhu2 pek-hiuN-chhiu7 tiong-ki koaiN5 e5 be2-liu, lai5 chai--i; iah8 beh tui3 i chiN2 e5 ki e5 be2-liu, at-chih8 i nng2 e5 ki; chai ti7 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 soaN.  23). Goa2 beh chai i ti7 I2-sek-liat8 koaiN5-toe7 e5 soaN, i chiu7 khui-ki kiat-chi2, chiaN5-choe3 ho2 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7; kok-iuN7 e5 pe-chiau2 beh hioh ti7 i e5 e7-bin7, hioh ti7 i e5 ki e5 im3-ng2-e7.  24). Chhan5-ia2 e5 chhiu7-bak8 long2 beh chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 koaiN5 e5 chhiu7 kang3-ke7, ke7 e5 chhiu7 seng koaiN5, chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7 kou-ta5, kou-ta5 e5 chhiu7 bou7-seng7; Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2 i, ia7 chiaN5 i.

[18]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Lin2 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 toe7 siaN2-su7 eng7 chit e5 siok8-gu2 kong2, Lau7-pe7 chiah8 sng e5 phu5-to5, kiaN2 e5 chhui3-khi2 sng-nng2?  3). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Lin2 ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong bo5 in-iu5 thang koh eng7 chit e5 siok8-gu2.  4). KhoaN3 ah, long2-chong2 e5 sin5-hun5 si7 siok8 ti7 Goa2; chhin-chhiuN7 lau7-pe7 e5 sin5-hun5 siok8 ti7 Goa2, kiaN2 e5 sin5-hun5 ia7 si7 an2-ni; hoan7-choe7 e5 sin5-hun5, i beh si2.  5). Lang5 na7 kong-gi7, kiaN5 kong-peng5 kap gi7-li2,  6). be7-bat chiuN7 soaN-teng2 chiah8 che3-mih8, be7-bat giong2-bong7 I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 ngou2-siong7, be7-bat phah la5-sam5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2, be7-bat chhin-kun7 keng-ki5-lai7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5;  7). be7-bat khui-hu7 lang5, si7 chiong khiam3-che3 e5 lang5 e5 tng3-thau5 heng5 i, be7-bat kiong5-chhiuN2 lang5 e5 mih8, si7 eng7 chiah8-mih8 hou7 iau e5 lang5 chiah8, eng7 i-chiuN5 hou7 thng3-theh e5 lang5 chheng7,  8). be7-bat ka7 chioh-chiN5 e5 lang5 tho2 li7-sek, ia7 bo5 theh8 lai7-chiN5, kiu-chhiu2 bo5 choe3-phaiN2, ti7 liong2-peng5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan chiau3 kong-to7 phoaN3-koat,  9). sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, chip-siu2 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, chiau3 seng5-sit8 kiaN5 tai7-chi3, che si7 gi7-lang5, tek-khak tit-tioh8 oah8; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  10). Siat-su2 i siN chit8 e5 kiaN2, choe3 kiong5-to7, choe3 thai5-lang5-e5, a2-si7 kiaN5 hiah e5 phaiN2 e5 chit8-hang7, bo5 kiaN5 teng2-bin7 sou2 kong2 e5 ho2,  11). hoan2-tng2 chiuN7 soaN-teng2 chiah8 che3-mih8, koh phah la5-sam5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2,  12). khui-hu7 khun3-khou2 kap song3-hiong e5 lang5, kiong5-chhiuN2 lang5 e5 mih8, be7-bat eng7 tng3-thau5 heng5--lang5, giong2-bong7 ngou2-siong7, kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7,  13). ka7 chioh-chiN5 e5 lang5 tho2 li7-sek, theh8 lai7-chiN5; chit e5 lang5 kiam2 oe7 oah8 mah? i tek-khak boe7 oah8; i kiaN5 hiah e5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 tek-khak tioh8 si2; i e5 choe7 beh kui ti7 i.  14). KhoaN3 ah, siat-su2 i siN chit8 e5 kiaN2, khoaN3-kiN3 lau7-pe7 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 choe7, chiu7 kiaN-hiaN5, bo5 an2-ni khi3 kiaN5;  15). be7-bat chiuN7-soaN chiah8 che3-mih8, be7-bat giong2-bong7 I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 ngou2-siong7, be7-bat phah la5-sam5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2;  16). be7-bat khui-hu7 lang5, be7-bat theh8 lang5 e5 tng3-thau5, be7-bat kiong5-chhiuN2 lang5 e5 mih8, si7 eng7 chiah8-mih8 hou7 iau e5 lang5 chiah8, eng7 i-chiuN5 hou7 thng3-theh e5 lang5 chheng7,  17). kiu-chhiu2 bo5 hai7 song3-hiong lang5, bo5 tho2 lai7-chiN5, bo5 theh8 li7-sek, i sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, chip-siu2 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, i chiu7 bo5 in-ui7 lau7-pe7 e5 choe7-koa3 lai5 si2-bo5, tek-khak oe7 oah8.  18). Lun7-kau3 i e5 lau7-pe7, in-ui7 i khi-hu7 lang5 chin siong-tiong7, kiong5-chhiuN2 hiaN-ti7, ti7 pun2-chok8-tiong kiaN5 m7-ho2; khoaN3 ah, i beh in-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7 lai5 si2.  19). Lin2 iau2 teh kong2, KiaN2 chaiN2-iuN7 bo5 tam-tng lau7-pe7 e5 choe7? KiaN2 na7 kiaN5 cheng3-tit8, kap hap8-li2 e5 su7, siu2 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7 lai5 kiaN5--i; i tek-khak oe7 oah8.  20). Hoan7-choe7 e5 sin5-hun5, i beh si2; kiaN2 tek-khak bo5 tam-tng lau7-pe7 e5 choe7, lau7-pe7 ia7 bo5 tam-tng kiaN2 e5 choe7; gi7-lang5 e5 gi7 beh kui ti7 i ka-ki7; phaiN2-lang5 e5 phaiN2, ia7 beh kui ti7 i ka-ki7.  21). PhaiN2-lang5 na7 hoe5-thau5 li7-khui sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-ok, chip-siu2 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7, kiaN5 cheng3-tit8 kap hap8-li2 e5 su7, i tek-khak oe7 oah8, boe7 si2.  22). I sou2 hoan7 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-koa3 bo5 koh ka7 i ki3-tit; ti7 sou2 kiaN5 e5 gi7, i beh oah8.  23). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, PhaiN2-lang5 si2-bo5, kiam2 si7 Goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 mah? Goa2 kiam2-m7-si7 hoaN-hi2 i hoe5-thau5, li7-khui i sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8 mah?  24). Chong2-si7 gi7-lang5 na7 oat8-thau5, li7-khui i e5 gi7, lai5 hoan7-choe7, chiau3 phaiN2-lang5 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, lai5 kiaN5; i kiam2 oe7 oah8 mah? i sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 gi7, long2 bo5 koh siu7 ki3-liam7, i beh ti7 sou2 hoan7 e5 choe7, sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2, si2 ti7 hit tiong-kan.  25). Lin2 iau2 teh kong2, Chu2 e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5; I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN; Goa2 e5 lou7 kiam2 bo5 kong-peng5 mah? kiam2-m7-si7 lin2 e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5 mah?  26). Gi7-lang5 na7 oat8-thau5 li7-khui i e5 gi7, lai5 kiaN5 choe7-ok, ti3-kau3 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni lai5 si2; i chiu7 in-ui7 sou2 kiaN5 e5 choe7-ok lai5 si2.  27). Koh phaiN2-lang5 na7 hoe5-thau5, li7-khui i sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2, lai5 kiaN5 cheng3-tit8 kap hap8-li2 e5 su7; i beh hou7 i e5 sin5-hun5 tit-tioh8 oah8.  28). In-ui7 i u7 siuN7, hoe5-thau5 li7-khui i sou2 hoan7 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-koa3; i tek-khak oah8 bo5 si2.  29). I2-sek-liat8-ke iau2 teh kong2, Chu2 e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5; I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, Goa2 e5 lou7 kiam2 bo5 kong-peng5 mah? kiam2-m7-si7 lin2 e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5 mah?  30). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, Goa2 beh chiau3 lin2 tak8-lang5 sou2 kiaN5--e5 sim2-phoaN3 lin2; lin2 tioh8 hoe5-thau5, li7-khui sou2 hoan7 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-koa3; an2-ni, choe7-koa3 boe7-oe7 hou7 lin2 pai7-bo5.  31). Lin2 tioh8 chiong sou2 hoan7 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-koa3 hiat-kak8 li7-khui lin2; ui7 ka-ki7 chiaN5 chit8 e5 sin e5 sim, kap sin e5 sin5; I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 mih-sai2 tioh8 si2?  32). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lang5 e5 si2, Goa2 bo5 hoaN-hi2 i e5 si2; sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 hoe5-thau5, lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8.

[19]	Li2 tioh8 ui7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 ong5-chhin choe3 ai-ko,  2). kong2, Lin2 lau7-bu2 si7 sim2-mih8? si7 bu2 e5 sai, phak ti7 chiah e5 sai e5 tiong-kan; ti7 soe3 chiah sai e5 tiong-kan, iuN2-chhi7 i e5 kiaN2.  3). Ti7 i e5 kiaN2 e5 tiong-kan, chhi7 chit8-chiah kau3 toa7, hak8-sip8 ka7-mih8 lai5 chiah8-lang5.  4). Liat8-kok thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 ti7 in e5 ham7-khiN liah8-tioh8, eng7 lian7 thoa i kau3 Ai-kip8 toe7.  5). Bu2 e5 sai khoaN3 pun2-sin theng3-hau7 kau3 sit-bang7; chiu7 tui3 i soe3-chiah sai e5 tiong-kan koh chhu2 chit8-chiah, iuN2-chhi7 kau3 toa7.  6). I ti7 chiah e5 sai e5 tiong-kan chau2-lai5 chau2-khi3, chiaN5-choe3 iong2 e5 sai, hak8-sip8 ka7-mih8 lai5 chiah8-lang5.  7). I chai in e5 kiong-tian7, koh hou7 in e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 pha-hng, in-ui7 i hm7-hm7-hau2 e5 siaN, pian3-toe7 kap ki5-tiong sou2-u7--e5 chiu7 hong-hoe3.  8). Tui3 an2-ni si3-ui5 e5 pang-kok tui3 tak8-seng2 lai5 kong-kek i, eng7 bang7 pha ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7; i siu7-liah8 ti7 in e5 ham7-khiN.  9). In ka7 i lian7 ti7 tu5--nih, toa3 kau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 hia; koaiN--i ti7 kian-kou3 e5 sou2-chai7; hou7 i e5 siaN ti7 I2-sek-liat8 soaN bo5 koh thiaN-kiN3.
	10). Lin2 lau7-bu2 cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 phu5-to5-chhiu7, kek8-ki5 bou7-seng7, chai ti7 chui2-piN, in-ui7 chui2 choe7, chiu7 kiat choe7-choe7 ke2-chi2, hoat choe7-choe7 ki.  11). SiN-chhut giam2-ngi7 e5 ki-oaiN7, thang choe3 chiang2-koan5--e5 e5 koaiN2; i ti7 am7-am7 e5 ki-oaiN7-tiong choe3 kek8 koaiN5--e5; in-ui7 koaiN5, chiu7 i e5 oaiN7 e5 tiong-ki theng2-khi2 hou7 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3.  12). Chong2-si7 chit-chang5 phu5-to5-chhiu7, in-ui7 toa7 siu7-khi3, tu2-tioh8 puih8--khi2-lai5, hiat ti7 toe7--nih; tang-hong chhe-ta i e5 ke2-chi2, giam2-ngi7 e5 ki-oaiN7 at-chit8 kou-ta5, hou7 he2 sio-lio--khi3.  13). TaN chai ti7 khong3-ia2 ta-so3 bo5 chui2 e5 toe7.  14). Koh tui3 i ki-oaiN7 e5 koaiN5, u7 he2 hoat-chhut, sio i e5 ke2-chi2; ti3-kau3 i bo5 giam2-ngi7 e5 ki-oaiN7, thang choe3 chiang2-koan5--e5 e5 koaiN2; che si7 thang ai-siong--e5, thang choe3 ai-ko.

[20]	Te7 chhit--ni5, gou7-geh8 chhoe-chap8, u7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiong2-lo2 kui2-na7 lang5, lai5 beh mng7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, che7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  3). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiong2-lo2 kong2, ka7 i kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 lai5 si7 beh mng7 Goa2 mah? Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 chi2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 m7 hou7 li2 mng7.  4). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 beh sim2-mng7 in, sim2-mng7 in mah? li2 tioh8 hou7 in chai in e5 liat8-chou2 hiah e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7;  5). tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tng Goa2 keng2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 jit8, ng3 Nga2-kok ke e5 hou7-e3, kiah8-khi2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 hou7 in bat Goa2, tui3 in kiah8-khi2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  6). Hit-jit8 Goa2 tui3 in kiah8-khi2 chhiu2, beh chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, kau3 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 in sou2 kong2, lau5 ni kap bit8 e5 toe7; hit e5 toe7 ti7 ban7-kok-tiong si7 khah u7 eng5-kng--e5.  7). Goa2 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 tak8-lang5 tioh8 khi3-sak bak8-chiu sou2 hoaN-hi2 hiah e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 tai7; m7-thang in-ui7 Ai-kip8 e5 ngou2-siong7 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  8). Chong2-si7 in poe7-gek8 Goa2, m7-kheng2 thiaN Goa2, m7 pang3-sak in tak8-lang5 bak8-chiu sou2 hoaN-hi2 hiah e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 tai7, m7 li7-khui Ai-kip8 e5 ngou2-siong7; Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 piaN3 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 tui3 in it-chin7 chiaN5 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3.  9). Tok8-tok8 Goa2 in-ui7 Goa2 e5 mia5 e5 ian5-kou3 kiaN5 tai7-chi3, bian2-tit Goa2 e5 mia5 ti7 in sou2 khia7-khi2 liat8-pang-tiong e5 bin7-cheng5 siu7 siat-tok8; Goa2 chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, ti7 liat8-pang-tiong e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 hou7 in bat Goa2.  10). An2-ni, Goa2 chiu7 hou7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, chhoa7 in kau3 khong3-ia2.  11). Chiong Goa2 e5 lut8-le7 siuN2-su3 in, chiong Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7 chi2-si7 in; chiu7-si7 lang5 na7 kiaN5--i beh tui3 i lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8--e5.  12). Koh Goa2 eng7 Goa2 e5 an-hioh-jit8 siuN2-su3 in, thang ti7 Goa2 kap in e5 tiong-kan choe3 cheng3-ku3; hou7 in chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 hou7 in chiaN5-choe3 seng3--e5.  13). Chong2-si7 I2-sek-liat8-ke ti7 khong3-ia2 poe7-gek8 Goa2, bo5 sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, khi3-sak Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, (chiu7-si7 lang5 na7 kiaN5--i, beh tui3 i lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8--e5), toa7-toa7 hoan7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 an-hioh-jit8: Goa2 chiu7 kong2, beh ti7 khong3-ia2 chiong Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 piaN3 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, biat8-bo5 in.  14). Tok8-tok8 Goa2 in-ui7 Goa2 e5 mia5 e5 ian5-kou3 kiaN5 tai7-chi3, bian2-tit Goa2 e5 mia5 siu7 siat-tok8 ti7 liat8-pang lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 e5 liat8-pang.  15). Koh Goa2 ti7 khong3-ia2 tui3 in kiah8-khi2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, kong2, Goa2 bo5 beh chhoa7 in jip8 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 in lau5 ni kap bit8 e5 toe7, hit e5 toe7 ti7 ban7-kok-tiong khah u7 eng5-kng--e5.  16). In-ui7 in iam3-chian7 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, bo5 sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, hoan7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 an-hioh-jit8, in e5 sim i3-hiong3 in e5 ngou2-siong7.  17). Sui-jian5 an2-ni, Goa2 e5 bak8-chiu7 iau2-ku2 si7 sioh in, bo5 hui2-biat8 in, bo5 ti7 khong3-ia2 ka7 in biat8 liau2-liau2.  18). Goa2 ti7 khong3-ia2 tui3 in e5 kiaN2-ji5 kong2, Boh8-tit than3 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 lut8-le7, boh8-tit siu2 in e5 hoat-tou7, iah8 boh8-tit in-ui7 in e5 ngou2-siong7 phah la5-sam7 ka-ki7.  19). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, lin2 tioh8 sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, siu2 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5--i.  20). Koh eng7 Goa2 chiah e5 an-hioh-jit8 choe3-seng3; chiah e5 jit8 ti7 Goa2 kap lin2 e5 tiong-kan choe3 cheng3-ku3, hou7 lin2 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  21). Tok8-tok8 in e5 kiaN2-ji5 poe7-gek8 Goa2, bo5 sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, iah8 bo5 siu2 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5--i, (chiu7-si7 lang5 na7 kiaN5--i, beh tui3 i lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8--e5); in hoan7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 an-hioh-jit8; Goa2 chiu7 kong2, Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 piaN3 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, ti7 khong3-ia2 it-chin7 chiaN5 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 kong-kek i.  22). Sui-jian5 an2-ni, Goa2 iau2-ku2 kiu Goa2 e5 chhiu2, ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 mia5 e5 ian5-kou3 kiaN5 tai7-chi3, bian2-tit Goa2 e5 mia5 siu7 siat-tok8 ti7 liat8-pang lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 e5 liat8-pang.  23). Koh Goa2 ti7 khoan3-ia2, tui3 in kiah8-khi2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, kong2 beh hun-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-kok, si3-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-pang.  24). In-ui7 in bo5 than3 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, iam3-chian7 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, hoan7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 an-hioh-jit8, bak8-chiu i3-hiong3 in lau7-pe7 e5 ngou2-siong7.  25). Koh Goa2 eng7 m7-ho2 e5 lut8-le7, kap boe7-oe7 tui3 i lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8 e5 hoat-tou7, hou7--in.  26).
