In eng7 it-chhe3 e5 thau5-chiuN7-kiaN2 keng-ke3 he2; Goa2 chiu7 ti7 in e5 che3-su7 ka7 in phah la5-sam5, hou7 in hong-hoe3; hou7 in chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	27). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2 oe7, ka7 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 tek-choe7 Goa2, eng7 an2-ni siat-tok8 Goa2.  28). In-ui7 Goa2 chhoa7 in kau3 Goa2 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2 beh siuN2-su3 in e5 toe7; in khoaN3-kiN3 tak8 e5 koaiN5-soaN, tak8-chang5 am7 e5 chhiu7; chiu7 ti7-hia hian3 in hiah e5 che3-su7, hian3 kek Goa2 siu7-khi3 e5 le2-mih8, iah8 ti7-hia sio phang-phang e5 seng-le2, kap koan3-tian7.  29). Goa2 chiu7 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 sou2 chiuN7 hit e5 koaiN5-ui7 si7 sim2-mih8? i e5 mia5 kio3-choe3 Pa-ba5, tit8-kau3 kin-a2-jit8.  30). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 iu5-goan5 chiau3 lin2 liat8-chou2 sou2 kiaN5-e5, phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7 mah? iu5-goan5 than3 in kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 kiaN5-im5 mah?  31). Lin2 hian3 le2-mih8, hou7 lin2 e5 kiaN2 keng-ke3 he2 e5 si5, iu5-goan5 chiong it-chhe3 e5 ngou2-siong7 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7, kau3 kin-a2-jit8 mah? I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, Goa2 kiam2 beh hou7 lin2 mng7 mah? Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 tek-khak m7 hou7 li2 mng7.  32). Lin2 kong2, Goan2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 goa7-pang lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 liat8-kok e5 chong-chok8, khi3 hok8-sai7 chha5-e5, chioh8-e5; lin2 hoat-khi2 chit-ho7 sim-i3, toan3-toan3 boe7 chiaN5.  33). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 beh eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, kap chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2-kut, kap piaN3-chhut e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 choe3 lin2 e5 ong5.  34). Goa2 beh eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, kap chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2-kut, kap piaN3-chhut e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 tui3 liat8-pang-tiong chhoa7 lin2 chhut, iah8 tui3 lin2 si3-soaN3-khi3 hiah e5 kok chu7-chip8 lin2.  35). Goa2 beh chhoa7 lin2 kau3 goa7-pang lang5 e5 khong3-ia2, ti7-hia tng-bin7 sim2-mng7 lin2.  36). Goa2 an3-chaiN2-iuN7 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 khong3-ia2 sim2-mng7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2, iah8 beh an2-ni sim2-mng7 lin2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  37). Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 keng-ke3 koaiN2-a2-e7, iah8 beh hou7 lin2 siu7 iok e5 khu-sok.  38). Goa2 beh tui3 lin2 tiong-kan it-chin7 tu5 hiah e5 poe7-gek8 kap tek-choe7 Goa2 e5 lang5; chhoa7 in chhut in kia3-kha e5 toe7-hng, chong2-si7 in boe7-tit jip8 I2-sek-liat8 toe7; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  39). I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lun7-kau3 lin2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Khi3 ah, tak8-lang5 hok8-sai7 i e5 ngou2-siong7, tok8-tok8 au7-lai5 tek-khak beh thiaN Goa2, bo5 koh eng7 le2-mih8 kap ngou2-siong7 siat-tok8 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5.  40). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Ti7 Goa2 e5 seng3-soaN, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 koaiN5 e5 soaN, ti7-hia I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke e5 cheng3-lang5, beh ti7 hit e5 toe7 hok8-sai7 Goa2, ti7-hia Goa2 beh chiap-lap8 lin2, ti7-hia Goa2 beh ka7 lin2 tho2 le2-mih8, kap lin2 khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 thou2-san2, i2-kip8 lin2 it-chhe3 e5 seng3-mih8.  41). Goa2 tui3 chiah e5 peh-siN3-tiong chhoa7 lin2 chhut, tui3 lin2 si3-soaN3--khi3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong chu7-chip8 lin2; hit-si5 Goa2 beh chiap-lap8 lin2 chhin-chhiuN7 phang-hiuN; Goa2 beh ti7 lin2 tit-tioh8 hian2-beng5 choe3-seng3, hou7 goa7-pang lang5 khoaN3-kiN3.  42). Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 jip8 I2-sek-liat8 toe7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 kiah8-khi2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, kong2 beh siuN2-su3 lin2 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7, hit-si5 lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  43). Ti7-hia lin2 beh ki3-tit lin2 e5 sou2-kiaN5 sou2 choe3, chiu7-si7 lin2 tui3 hiah-e5 lai5 phah la5-sam5 lin2 ka-ki7--e5; koh beh in-ui7 lin2 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2, lai5 ka-ki7 iam3-ouN3.  44). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, Goa2 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 mia5 e5 ian5-kou3, bo5 chiau3 lin2 e5 phaiN2 sou2-kiaN5, kap lin2 e5 hu2-pai7 e5 sou2-choe3 khoan2-thai7 lin2; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	45). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 Goa2 kong2,  46). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 e5 bin7 tioh8 ng3 lam5-hng, ng3 lam5-hng piaN3-chhut oe7, kong-kek lam5-hng chhan5-ia2 e5 chhiu7-na5 lai5 soan-thoan5.  47). Tui3 lam5-hng e5 chhiu7-na5 kong2, Tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7; Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ti7 li2 tiong kan khi2 he2, sio li2 tiong-kan it-chhe3 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7, kap kou-ta5 e5 chhiu7; beng2-liat8 e5 he2-iam7, tek-khak bo5 sit; tui3 lam5 kau3 pak, tak8-bin7 long2 siu7 sio.  48). Hoan7-na7 u7 hiat-khi3--e5, long2 beh chai khi2-he2--e5, si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  49). Tui3 an2-ni goa2 kong2, HaiN7 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, lang5 long2 gi7-lun7 goa2 kong2, I kiam2 m7-si7 teh kong2 phi3-ju7?

[21]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 bin7 ng3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ng3 hiah e5 seng3-sou2 piaN3-chhut oe7 kong-kek I2-sek-liat8 toe7 lai5 soan-thoan5.  3). Tui3 I2-sek-liat8 toe7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh ti2-tek8 li2, iah8 beh puih8 Goa2 e5 to chhut i e5 siu3; tui3 li2 e5 tiong-kan chian2-tu5 gi7-lang5 phaiN2-lang5.  4). Goa2 ki3-jian5 beh tui3 li2 tiong-kan chian2-tu5 gi7-lang5 kap phaiN2-lang5, sou2-i2 Goa2 e5 to beh chhut i e5 siu3, tui3 lam5 kau3 pak, kong-kek it-chhe3 u7 hiat-khi3-e5.  5). It-chhe3 u7 hiat-khi3-e5 chiu7 chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng puih8 to chhut i e5 siu3, tek-khak bo5 koh siu-jip8.  6). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 thou2-khui3, io-kut chih8, thong3-khou2; thou2-khui3 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5.  7). In mng7 li2 kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 thou2-khui3? li2 chiu7 tioh8 kong2, In-ui7 u7 hong-siaN tai7-chi3 beh lai5, lang5 e5 sim long2 beh siau-iuN5, chhiu2 long2 sng-nng2, cheng-sin5 soe-pai7, kha-thau5-u loan2-jiok8 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2; khoaN3 ah, chit e5 su7 teh lai5, tek-khak oe7 chiaN5; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  9). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 kong2, U7 to, u7 to, si7 boa5-lai7 lu3-kng e5.  10). Boa5-lai7 si7 beh thai5 lang5, lu3-kng si7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3; lan2 kiam2 thang hoaN-hi2 mah? Goa2 e5 kiaN2 e5 koaiN2-a2 biau2-si7 cheng3 chhiu7-bak8.  11). Chit ki to i2-keng kau hou7 lang5 lu3-kng, thang hou7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 kiah8--i; i i2-keng boa5-lai7 lu3-kng, thang kau ti7 thai5-lang5--e5 e5 chhiu2.  12). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 hoah, au5-kio3; in-ui7 chit e5 lim5-kau3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, kap I2-sek-liat8 it-chhe3 e5 kui3-chok8; in kap Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 kau ti7 to-e7, sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tah toa7-thui2.  13). U7 chhi3-giam7 e5 su7; na7 hit e5 biau2-si7 e5 koaiN2-a2 kui ti7 bo5, beh an3-chaiN2-iuN7 ah? che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  14). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tah chhiu2 soan-thoan5, chit ki to tioh8 saN-pai2 ka-pe7, chiu7-si7 hou7 lang5 tioh8 tang7-siong e5 to, iah8 si7 hou7 tai7-jin5 tioh8 tang7-siong e5 to, jip8 ti7 bat8-pang5--e5.  15). Goa2 pi7-pan7 hou7 lang5 kiaN e5 to, kong-kek in it-chhe3 e5 siaN5-mng5; hou7 in e5 sim siau-iuN5, ke-thiN in poah8-to2 e5 su7; haiN7 ah, chit ki to chhong3 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3, boa5 kau3 chin-lai7, beh thai5-si2 lang5.  16). Li2 tioh8 hap8-oa2, ng3 chiaN3-peng5; pai5-tin7, ng3 to3-peng5; chhut-chai7 li2 e5 bin7 ng3 toh-loh8, chiu7 ng3 hia.  17). Goa2 iah8 beh tah-chhiu2, iah8 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 soah; che si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	18). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  19). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 ui7-tioh8 pun2-sin siat nng7 tiau5 lou7, thang hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 to-kiam3 tui3 hia lai5; chi2 nng7 tiau5 lou7 tioh8 tui3 chit8 sou2-chai7 pun-chhut; koh tioh8 ui7 chit ki chhiu2, ui7 ti7 thau3-kau3 siaN5 e5 lou7-thau5.  20). Li2 tioh8 siat chit8 tiau5 lou7, hou7 to lai5 kau3 A-bun5 lang5 e5 Lah8-pa, ia7 thang kau3 Iu5-tai7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  21). In-ui7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 khia7 ti7 siang-chhe lou7 hia, ti7 nng7 tiau5 lou7-thau5 beh chiam-pok, i e5 io5 chiN3; mng7 ngou2-siong7, giam7 seng-le2 e5 koaN.  22). Ti7 i e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, u7 chiam-pok khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 chiN3; siat iuN5-thau5-thui5, khui-chhui3 hoah thai5, toa7-siaN au5-kio3, siat iuN5-thau5-khui5, kong-kek siaN5-mng5, khi2 thou5-tui, cho7-tai5.  23). Hiah e5 bat tui3 in chiu3-choa7 e5 lang5 khoaN3 i choe3 ke2 e5 chiam-pok; chong2-si7 i beh hou7 lang5 ki3-tit in e5 phaiN2, ti3-kau3 in cheng3-lang5 siu7-liah8.
	24). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 e5 ke3-sit lou7-hian7, hou7 lin2 e5 choe7-koa3 tu2-tioh8 ki3-tit, ti3-kau3 lin2 e5 choe7-ok ti7 lin2 e5 kiaN5-choe3 long2 hian2-chhut; koh in-ui7 lin2 siu7 ki3-tit, beh hou7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 liah8.  25). Li2 chit e5 siu7 tang7-siong kiaN5-phaiN2 e5 I2-sek-liat8 ong5 ah, li2 e5 choe7-ok koan3-moa2, li2 e5 jit8-chi2 kau3 lah.  26). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tioh8 tu5-khi3 ong5-bo7, liu3 bian2-liu5, bo5 koh u7 chit ho7 keng2-hong2; taN beh hou7 ke7--e5 seng koaiN5, koaiN5-e5 kang3-ke7.  27). Goa2 beh chhia-to2, chhia-to2, chhia-to2--i; bo5 koh u7 chit-e5, theng3-hau7 eng-kai tit-tioh8--e5 kau3, Goa2 chiu7 hou7--i.
	28). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 A-bun5 lang5, kap in e5 bu2-ban7, u7 an2-ni kong2; li2 tioh8 kong2, U7 to, u7 puih8-chhut e5 to, i2-keng lu3-kng, beh thai5-si2 lang5; hou7 i chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3 beh thun-biat8 lang5.  29). Lang5 ui7-tioh8 li2 khoaN3 hu-ke2 e5 iN7-siong7, kiaN5 peh8-chhat8 e5 chiam-pok; chiong li2 he7 ti7 siu7 tang7-siong phaiN2-lang5 e5 am7-kun2; in e5 choe7-ok koan3-moa2, in e5 jit8-chi2 kau3 lah.  30). Hou7 to jip8 siu3, Goa2 beh ti7 li2 siu7-cho7 e5 ui7, seng-tiong2 e5 toe7, sim2-phoaN3 li2.  31). Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 thong3-hun7 piaN3 ti7 li2 e5 sin-chiuN7, chiong Goa2 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 he2 pun5 ti7 li2; kau li2 ti7 chan5-jim2 gau5 thai5-lang5--e5 e5 chhiu2.  32). Li2 beh choe3 hiaN5-he2 e5 chha5, li2 e5 huih beh lau5 ti7 chit e5 toe7-hng, li2 bo5 koh tit-tioh8 ki3-liam7; in-ui7 che si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[22]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 beh sim2-mng7, sim2-mng7 hou7 lang5 lau5 huih e5 siaN5 mah? tioh8 hou7 i chai i it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  3). Li2 tioh8 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chit e5 siaN5, u7 lau5 lang5 e5 huih ti7 hit lai7-bin7, hou7 i e5 jit8-chi2 kau3; koh chng ngou2-siong7 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7, ham7-hai7 ka-ki7.  4). In-ui7 li2 hou7 lang5 lau5 huih, chiu7 u7 choe7; li2 chng ngou2-siong7 si7 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7; chiu7 li2 hou7 li2 e5 jit8 kun7, li2 i2-keng kau3 li2 e5 ni5; sou2-i2 Goa2 hou7 li2 siu7 liat8-kok e5 leng5-jiok8, liat8-pang e5 thi2-chhio3.  5). Li2 chit-e5 chhau3-mia5 choe7-choe7 jiau2-loan7 e5 siaN5 ah! hiah-e5 li7-khui li2 kun7, li7-khui li2 hng7--e5, long2 beh thi2-chhio3 li2.  6). KhoaN3 ah, I2-sek-liat8 e5 siu2-leng2, tak8-e5 theng2 i khui3-lat8, ti7 li2 tiong-kan lau5 lang5 e5 huih.  7). Ti7 li2 tiong-kan u7 bu2-ban7 pe7-bu2; ti7 li2 tiong-kan u7 ap-che3 chhut-goa7 lang5; ti7 li2 tiong-kan u7 khui-hu7 kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7--e5.  8). Li2 khoaN3-khin Goa2 e5 seng3-mih8, hoan7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 an-hioh-jit8.  9). Ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 hui2-pong3 lang5, beh hou7 lang5 lau5 huih--e5; ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 ti7 soaN-teng2 chiah8 che3-mih8, ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 kiaN5 im5-loan7.  10). Ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 lou7-hian7 lau7-pe7 e5 e7-the2; ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 leng5-jiok8 geh8-keng bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5--e5.  11). U7 lang5 kap chhu3-piN e5 bou2 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7; ia7 u7 lang5 im5 i e5 sim-pu7 lai5 phah la5-sam5--i; ti7 lin2 tiong-kan iah8 u7 lang5 leng5-jiok8 i e5 chi2-be7, chiu7-si7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  12). Ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 siu7 pou3-lou7, lai5 lau5 lang5 e5 huih, li2 iah8 u7 theh8 lai7-chiN5, tho2 li7-sek; li2 in-ui7 tham-sim, lek8-sek chhu3-piN, tit-tioh8 chai5-li7; keng2-jian5 boe7-ki3-tit Goa2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 in-ui7 li2 sou2 tit put-gi7 e5 chiN5, kap li2 tiong-kan sou2 lau5 e5 huih, Goa2 chiu7 phah-chhiu2.  14). Kau3 Goa2 pan7 li2 e5 jit8, li2 e5 sim iau2 oe7 jim2-siu7 mah? li2 e5 chhiu2 iau2 oe7 u7 lat8 mah? Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 chit e5 oe7, chiu7 beh chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.  15). Goa2 beh hun-soaN3 li2 ti7 liat8-kok, si3-soaN3 li2 ti7 liat8-pang; Goa2 beh tu5 li2 tiong-kan e5 u3-oe3.  16). Li2 beh ti7 liat8-kok lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, in-ui7 ka-ki7 sou2 kiaN5--e5, siu7 siat-tok8; li2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	17). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  18). Jin5-chu2 ah, I2-sek-liat8-ke chai7 Goa2 khoaN3 si7 che-tai2; in long2 si7 he2-lou5-tiong e5 tang5, siah, thih, ian5; si7 gun5 e5 che-tai2.  19). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lin2 long2 chiaN5-choe3 che-tai2; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chu7-chip8 lin2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 tiong-kan.  20). Lang5 chaiN2-iuN7 chiong gun5, tang5, thih, ian5, siah, chu7-chip8 ti7 he2-lou5-tiong; khan-he2 hou7 i iuN5; an2-ni Goa2 iah8 beh eng7 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, kap toa7 siu7-khi3, chu7-chip8 lin2, he7 lin2 ti7-hia, lai5 iuN5-hoa3 lin2.  21). Goa2 beh chu7-chip8 lin2, eng7 Goa2 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 he2 pun5 lin2, lin2 chiu7 ti7 hit tiong-kan iuN5-hoa3.  22). Gun5 chaiN2-iuN7 iuN5 ti7 he2-lou5-tiong, lin2 iah8 beh an2-ni iuN5 ti7 hit tiong-kan; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa piaN3-chhut Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 lin2 e5 teng2-bin7.
	23). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  24). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 chit e5 toe7 kong2, Li2 si7 be7 tit-tioh8 chheng-khi3 e5 toe7, ti7 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 jit8, iah8 bo5 loh8-hou7 ti7 li2 hia.  25). I tiong-kan e5 sian-ti long2 kiat-tong2, chhin-chhiuN7 hm7-hm7-hau2 e5 sai, jiau3-tioh8 sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, in thun-chiah8 lang5 e5 sin5-hun5, chhiuN2 lang5 e5 he3-chai5 po2-mih8; hou7 in e5 tiong-kan e5 chiu2-koaN2-lang5 koh khah-choe7.  26). I e5 che3-si koe2-chhoah8 Goa2 e5 lut8-hoat, siat-tok8 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, bo5 hun-piat seng3-e5 kap chhou-siok8-e5, iah8 bo5 hou7 lang5 hun-piat bo5 chheng-khi3--e5, kap chheng-khi3--e5; koh ng bak8-chiu m7 khoaN3 Goa2 chiah e5 an-hioh-jit8, Goa2 iah8 ti7 in tiong-kan siu7 siat-tok8.  27). I e5 kui3-chok8 chhin-chhiuN7 chhai5-long5, jiau3-tioh8 sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, thai5 lang5 lau5 huih, siong-hai7 lang5 e5 siN3-mia7, ai3 tit-tioh8 put-gi7 e5 chiN5.  28). I e5 sian-ti chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 he-chui2 ka7 in chheng2-peh8, khoaN3 hu-ke2 e5 iN7-siong7, eng7 peh8-chhat8 ka7 in chiam-pok, kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, ki5-sit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5-iaN2 kong2.  29). Kok-lai7 e5 peh-siN3 it-bi7 kiaN5 ap-che3 koan3-lian7 chhiuN2 lang5; khui-hu7 song3-hiong khun3-khou2--e5, bo5 cheng5-li2 khi-ap chhut-goa7 lang5.  30). Goa2 ti7 in tiong-kan chhe7-khoaN3 u7 chit8-lang5 thang lai5 ui5-chhiuN5, ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ui7-tioh8 chit e5 kok khia7 ti7 phoa3-khiah e5 sou2-chai7, hou7 goa2 bo5 chau5-biat8 i; chong2-si7 chhe7 bo5 chit8-e5.  31). Sou2-i2 Goa2 eng7 Goa2 e5 thong3-hun7 piaN3 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, eng7 Goa2 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 he2 biat8--in; chiau3 in sou2 kiaN5--e5, po3-eng3 ti7 in e5 thau5-khak-teng2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[23]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, u7 nng7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, si7 siang5 chit8 e5 lau7-bu2 siN--e5.  3). In ti7 Ai-kip8 kiaN5-im5, chiu7-si7 ti7 siau3-lian5 e5 si5 kiaN5-im5; ti7-hia in e5 ni hou7 lang5 teh, koh ti7-hia lang5 nih8 i chai7-sek-lu2 e5 ni-thau5.  4). In e5 mia5, toa7-chi2 mia5 A-ho5-lah8, sio2-be7 mia5 A-ho5-li7-pa; in long2 ke3 hou7 Goa2, siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2; lun7-kau3 in e5 mia5, A-ho5-lah8 chiu7-si7 Sat-ma2-li7-a, A-ho5-li7-pa chiu7-si7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  5). A-ho5-lah8 ke3 hou7 Goa2 liau2-au7, chiu7 kiaN5 im5-loan7, loan5-ai3 i siong-ho2 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 i e5 keh-piah kok A-sut8 lang5.  6). In chheng7 lam5-sek e5 saN, choe3 seng2-tiuN2, choe3 koaN-oan5, long2 si7 kho2-ai3 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, khia5-be2 e5 iong2-su7.  7). I chiu7 kap in kiaN5-im5, chiu7-si7 kap i sou2 teng3-i3 e5 A-sut8 lang5; kiN3-na7 i sou2 loan5-ai3--e5, chiu7 eng7 in it-chhe3 e5 ngou2-siong7 lai5 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7.  8). I iah8 bo5 pang3-sak i ti7 Ai-kip8 koan3-lian7 kiaN5 e5 im5-loan7; in-ui7 i iau2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5, chiu7 u7 lang5 kap i saN-kap khun3; nih8 i chai7-sek-lu2 e5 ni, koh lau5-chhut i im5-loan7 e5 su7 ti7-hia.  9). In-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 chiong i kau ti7 i siong-ho2 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chiu7-si7 i sou2 loan5-ai3 e5 A-sut8 lang5 e5 chhiu2.  10). In chiu7 lou7-hian7 i e5 e7-the2, eng7 to thai5--i, liah8 i e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, hou7 i ti7 hu7-jin5-lang5 tiong lau5 chhau3 mia5; in-ui7 in tui3 i kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3.  11). I e5 sio2-be7 A-ho5-li7-pa khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ni, chiu7 pi2 i koh khah hong3-chhiong3 im5-iok8; kiaN5 im5-loan7, pi2 i e5 toa7-chi2 khah siong-tiong7.  12). I loan5-ai3 keh-piah kok e5 A-sut8 lang5, chiu7-si7 chheng7 kek8-sui2 e5 i-hok8, choe3 seng2-tiuN2, choe3 koaN-oan5; khia5-be2 e5 iong2-su7, long2 si7 kho2-ai3 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5.  13). Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 i siu7 phah la5-sam5, chi2-be7-a2 nng7-e5 kiaN5 siang5-lou7.  14). I iah8 ke-thiN i e5 im5-heng7, in-ui7 i khoaN3-kiN3 lang5 e5 siong7 ui7 ti7 piah--nih, chiu7-si7 eng7 chu-ang5-sek sou2 ui7 Ka-lek8-ti2 lang5 e5 siong7.  15). Io ha5 toa3, thau5-khak pau chhai2-sek e5 kun sui5-loh8--lai5; khoaN3-liau2 chhin-chhiuN7 kun-tiuN2, chiau3 Pa-pi2-lun5 lang5 e5 heng5-siong7; in e5 pun2 sou2-chai7 chiu7-si7 Ka-lek8-ti2.  16). I chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 loan5-ai3 in; chhe su3-chia2 khi3 Ka-lek8-ti2 hia, kiN3 in.  17). Pa-pi2-lun5 lang5 chiu7 lai5, kap i chiuN7 ai3-cheng5 e5 bin5-chhng5, kiaN5 im5, phah la5-sam5 i.  I siu7 phah la5-sam5 i2-au7, sim chiu7 kap in leng2-tam7.  18). An2-ni, i lou7-hian7 i e5 im5-heng7, koh lou7-hian7 i e5 e7-the2, Goa2 e5 sim chiu7 kap i leng2-tam7, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 kap i e5 toa7-chi2 leng2-tam7 chit8-iuN7.  19). I iau2-ku2 koh-khah im5-heng7, ki3-tit i siau3-lian5 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, kiaN5 im5-loan7 e5 jit8;  20). loan5-ai3 i siong-ho2 e5 lang5, sin-the2 iong2, cheng chiok, chhin-chhiuN7 lu5, chhin-chhiuN7 be2.  21). An2-ni li2 chiu7 ki3-tit li2 siau3-lian5 e5 si5 e5 im5-heng7; hit-si5 Ai-kip8 lang5 teh li2 e5 ni, it-tioh8 li2 siau3-lian5 e5 ni.
	22). A-ho5-li7-pa ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2-i2 an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh kek-tong7 li2 chiah e5 siong-ho2-e5, lai5 kong-kek li2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 sim sou2 leng2-tam7--e5, Goa2 beh hou7 i si3-ui5 lai5 kong-kek li2.  23). Chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 lang5, Ka-lek8-ti2 cheng3 lang5, kap Pi2-kat, Su-a, Ko-a, chiah e5 chok8.  A-sut8 e5 cheng3-lang5 kap in lai5, seng2-tiuN2, koaN-oan5, kun-tiuN2, u7 mia5-siaN--e5, khia5-be2 e5, long2 si7 kho2-ai3 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5.  24). In beh toa3 kun-khi3, chian3-chhia, un7-niu5 e5 chhia, chhoa7 toa7-tui7 e5 cheng3-lang5 lai5 kong-kek li2; in gia5 toa7-pai5 sio2-pai5, thau5-khoe, pai5-tin7 ti7 li2 e5 si3-ui5 kong-kek li2; Goa2 beh chiong sim2-phoaN3 e5 su7 kau-tai3 in, in beh eng7 in e5 lut8-hoat sim2-phoaN3 li2.  25). Goa2 beh eng7 Goa2 e5 tou3-khi7 kong-kek li2; in beh eng7 toa7 siu7-khi3 pan7 li2; in beh koah li2 e5 phiN7 kap hi7-a2; li2 sou2 chhun e5 lang5, beh to2 ti7 to-e7; in beh liah8 li2 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2; koh li2 sou2-lau5--e5 beh hou7 he2 sio-lio--khi3.  26). In beh pak li2 e5 i-hok8, chhiuN2 li2 sui2 e5 po2-mih8.  27). An2-ni, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 im5-heng7, kap li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 koan3-lian7 kiaN5 e5 im5-loan7 long2 soah; hou7 li2 bo5 koh kiah8-bak8 khoaN3--in, iah8 bo5 koh ki3-liam7 Ai-kip8.  28). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong li2 kau ti7 li2 sou2 oan3-hun7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 sim kap in leng2-tam7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2.  29). In beh oan3-hun7 lai5 pan7--li2, chhiuN2-theh8 li2 it-chhe3 lo5-lok8 lai5 tit-tioh8--e5; chhun li2 chit8-e5 chhiah-sin lou7-the2; li2 im5-loan7 e5 e7-the2, lian5 li2 e5 im5-heng7, kap li2 e5 im5-loan7, long2 beh lou7-hian7.  30). Li2 oe7 tu2-tioh8 hiah e5 tai7-chi3, in-ui7 li2 te3 goa7-pang lang5 lai5 kiaN5-im5; koh in-ui7 li2 tui3 in chiah e5 ngou2-siong7 lai5 bak la5-sam5.  31). Li2 u7 kiaN5 li2 e5 toa7-chi2 e5 lou7, sou2-i2 Goa2 beh chiong i e5 poe kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2.  32). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 beh lim li2 e5 toa7-chi2 sou2 lim e5 poe; hit e5 poe chhim koh khoah, toe2 chin-choe7; li2 chiu7 beh hou7 lang5 thi2-chhio3 ki-chhi3.  33). Li beh toa7 chiu2-chui3, toa7 iu-khou2; lim lin2 toa7-chi2 Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 poe; chiu7-si7 hou7 lang5 gong5-ngiah8 chhiN-chham2 e5 poe.  34). Li2 beh lim chit e5 poe, lim kau3 ta-ta; koh ka7 phoa3-poe e5 phe3, thiah-lih8 ka-ki7 e5 ni; in-ui7 chit e5 su7 Goa2 bat kong2--i; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  35). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 li2 boe7-ki3-tit Goa2, chiong Goa2 hiat ti7 li2 e5 ka-chiah-au7, taN li2 tioh8 tam-tng li2 e5 im5-loan7 kap li2 hong3-chhiong3 su-iok8 e5 choe7.
	36). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 beh sim2-mng7 A-ho5-lah8 kap A-ho5-li7-pa mah? tioh8 chi2-chhut in sou2 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  37). In kiaN5-im5, iah8 u7 huih ti7 i e5 chhiu2, koh kap ngou2-siong7 kiaN5-im5, iah8 hou7 in tui3 Goa2 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2 keng-ke3 he2, hou7 in thun-chiah8.  38). Chit e5 i2-goa7 in iau2 u7 tui3 Goa2 an2-ni kiaN5, chiu7-si7 siang5-jit8 phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, kan-hoan7 Goa2 chiah e5 an-hioh-jit8.  39). In thai5 kiaN2 hian3 hou7 ngou2-siong7, tng hit-jit8 koh jip8 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, lai5 phah la5-sam5--i; khoaN3 ah, in ti7 Goa2 e5 chhu3-lai7 an2-ni kiaN5.  40). Koh lin2 chhe su3-chia2 khi3 chhiaN2 hng7-hng7 e5 lang5; su3-chia2 kau3 in hia e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, in chiu7 lai5; li2 ui7-tioh8 in soe2 sin-khu, ui7 bak8-bai5, eng7 chhiu2-sek ka-ki7 chng-thaN7;  41). che7 ti7 sui2 e5 bin5-chhng5, chhng5-cheng5 chhai7 chit8 te3 toh, chiong Goa2 e5 hiuN-liau7, Goa2 e5 hiuN-iu5 pai5 ti7 hit teng2-bin7.  42). Kap i ti7-hia--e5, u7 kui-tin7 e5 lang5, an-iat8 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, iah8 u7 chhou-siok8 lang5 kap chiu2-han3, tui3 khong3-ia2 saN-kap lai5, chiong chhiu2-khoan5 koa3 ti7 in nng7-e5 e5 chhiu2, chiong sui2 bo7 ti3 ti7 in e5 thau5-khak.  43). Goa2 lun7-kau3 chit e5 lau7 e5 im5-hu7, u7 kong2, Hian7-chai7 lang5 iau2 beh kap i kiaN5 im5, i iah8 beh kap lang5 kiaN5-im5.  44). Lang5 jip8-khi3 chiu7-kun7 i, chhin-chhiuN7 chiu7-kun7 chhiong-ki; an2-ni in chiu7-kun7 nng7 e5 im5-hu7, A-ho5-lah8 kap A-ho5-li7-pa.  45). Beh u7 gi7-lang5 chiau3 sim2-phoaN3 im5-hu7 e5 le7, kap lau5 lang5 e5 huih e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 le7, lai5 sim2-phoaN3 in; in-ui7 in si7 im5-hu7, iah8 u7 huih ti7 i e5 chhiu2.  46). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh chhoa7 choe7-choe7 lang5 lai5 kong-kek in, hou7 in siu7 hiat-lai5 hiat-khi3, tu2-tioh8 chhiuN2-toat8.  47). Hiah e5 lang5 beh eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 in, eng7 to-kiam3 thai5-si2 in; koh thai5-si2 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, eng7 he2 sio in e5 chhu3-theh8.  48). An2-ni, Goa2 beh hou7 keng2-lai7 bo5 koh u7 im5-heng7, thang hou7 it-chhe3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 siu7 keng2-kai3, bo5 oh8 lin2 e5 im5-heng7.  49). Lang5 beh chiau3 lin2 e5 im5-heng7 po3-eng3 lin2; lin2 ia7 beh tam-tng chiah-e5 pai3 ngou2-siong7 e5 choe7; lin2 chiu7 oe7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[24]	Te7 kau2-ni5 chap8-geh8 chhoe-chap8 jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2, kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, kin-a2-jit8 tu2-tu2 si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 chiu7-kun7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 jit8, li2 tioh8 chiong kin-a2-jit8 ki3 i e5 mia5.  3). Tioh8 tui3 chit e5 poe7-gek8 e5 ke siat phi3-ju7, kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chiong tiaN2 chhai7 ti7 he2--nih; i2-keng chhai7 ho2, chiu7 piaN3 chui2 ti7 lai7-bin7,  4). chiong bah-te3, chiu7-si7 it-chhe3 pui5-sui2 e5 bah-te3, cheng5-thui2 au7-thui2, long2 khioh he7 ti7 lai7-bin7; keng2 ho2 e5 kut thiap8 hou7 i moa2.  5). Chhu2 iuN5-kun5-tiong te7-it ho2--e5, chiong chha5 thiap8 ti7 tiaN2-e7, hou7 tiaN2 kun2 chhiang5-chhiang5, thang chiong kut kun5 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7.
	6). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, U7 chai-e7 ah, chit e5 hou7 lang5 lau5-huih e5 siaN5, chiu7-si7 siN sian e5 tiaN2, i e5 sian iau2-be7 tu5--khi3, tioh8 chiong bah-te3 tui3 hit tiong-kan chit8-te3 chit8-te3 theh8-chhut-lai5; bo5 ka7 i liam-khau.  7). SiaN5-tiong u7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 e5 huih, piaN3 ti7 kng-kng e5 chioh8-poaN5-teng2, bo5 piaN3 ti7 toe7--nih, thang eng7 thou5 kham3.  8). Chit e5 siaN5-lai7 sou2 lau5 e5 huih, piaN3 ti7 kng-kng e5 chioh8-poaN5-teng2, bo5 thang jia-kham3, si7 Goa2 hou7 i an2-ni; ui7-tioh8 beh kek toa7 siu7-khi3, kiaN5 po3-eng3.  9). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, U7 chai-e7 ah, chit e5 hou7 lang5 lau5-huih e5 siaN5, Goa2 iah8 beh thiap8 toa7-tui e5 he2-chha5.  10). ThiN-chha5 hou7 he2 chin iam7, chiong bah kun5 noa7, chiong thng ngau5 kho2, hou7 kut hu-lu--khi3.  11). Chiong tiaN2, piaN3 khang, chhai7 ti7 teh toh8 e5 thoaN3-teng2, hou7 tiaN2 pek-jiat8, hou7 tang5 sio ang5, iuN5 ki5-tiong e5 u3-oe3, tu5 hit teng2-bin7 e5 sian.  12). I tioh8-boa5 ia3-sian7, chong2-si7 sou2 siN toa7-toa7 e5 sian, iu5-goan5 bo5 lak; i e5 sian chiu7 na7 ti7 he2--nih, iah8 boe7 tu5-khi3.  13). Ti7 li2 e5 u3-oe3 tiong u7 im5-heng7, Goa2 bat chheng-khi3 li2, li2 iau2-ku2 bo5 chheng-khi3; sou2-i2 li2 e5 u3-oe3 boe7 koh tit-tioh8 chheng-khi3, kau3 Goa2 tui3 li2 hoat-chhut e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 soah.  14). Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa bat kong2--i; hit e5 su7 tek-khak chiaN5, Goa2 ia7 beh kiaN5--i, tek-khak bo5 hoan2-hok, tek-khak bo5 lin5-bin2, iah8 bo5 the3-hoe2; lang5 beh chiau3 li2 e5 ku2-tong7, chiau3 li2 e5 kiaN5-choe3 sim2-phoaN3 li2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  16). Jin5-chu2 ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong li2 e5 bak8-chiu sou2 i3-ai3--e5 hut-jian5 chhu2--khi3; chong2-si7 li2 m7-thang pi-ai thi5-khau3, iah8 m7-thang lau5 bak8-sai2.  17). Tok8-tok8 thang am3-chiN7 thou2-khui3, m7-thang chhut-siaN, m7-thang pan7-li2 song-su7, thau5-khak iu5-goan5 tioh8 pau thau5-kun, kha iu5-goan5 tioh8 chheng7-oe5, m7-thang ng li2 e5 chhui3-tun5, ia7 m7-thang chiah8 tiau3-song e5 piaN2.  18). Tui3 an2-ni, goa2 chiong chit e5 su7 cha2-khi2-si5 ka7 peh-siN3 kong2; e5-hng goa2 e5 bou2 chiu7 si2; keh cha2-khi2, goa2 chiu7 than3 beng7-leng7 lai5 kiaN5.
	19). Peh-siN3 mng7 goa2 kong2, Li2 an2-ni choe3, kap goan2 u7 sim2-mih8 kan-siap8? li2 thai2-tho2 bo5 ka7 goan2 kong2?  20). Goa2 in3 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  21). Li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 se3-lek8 sou2 khoa-khau2, lin2 e5 bak8-chiu sou2 i3-ai3, lin2 e5 sim sou2 thiaN3-sioh--e5; koh lin2 sou2 lau5 ti7-hia e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 beh to2 ti7 to-e7.  22). Hit-si5, lin2 beh chiau3 goa2 sou2 kiaN5--e5 lai5 kiaN5, bo5 ng lin2 e5 chhui3-tun5, iah8 bo5 chiah8 tiau3-song e5 piaN2.  23). Lin2 e5 thau5-khak iu5-goan5 pau thau5-kun, kha beh chheng7 oe5, bo5 pi-ai, bo5 thi5-khau3; lin2 beh ti7 lin2 e5 choe7-ok tiong siau-biat8, saN tui3-bin7 thou2-khui3.  24). I2-se-kiat beh an2-ni choe3 lin2 e5 tiau7-thau5, hoan7-na7 i sou2 kiaN5--e5, lin2 iah8 beh an2-ni kiaN5, chit e5 tai7-chi3 na7 kau3, lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	25). Jin5-chu2 ah, tng Goa2 tu5-khi3 in sou2 oa2-kho3 e5, kap in sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 eng5-kng, in e5 bak8-chiu sou2 i3-ai3--e5, in e5 sim sou2 thiaN3-sioh--e5, chiu7-si7 in e5 kiaN2-ji5,  26). hit-jit8 tit-tioh8 thoat-li7 e5 lang5 kiam2 bo5 lai5 li2 chia, hou7 li2 chhin-hi7 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 su7 mah?  27). Tng hit-jit8, li2 e5 chhui3 chiu7 khui, li2 chiu7 kap tit-tioh8 thoat-li7 e5 lang5 kong2-oe7, bo5 koh e2-kau2; li2 beh an2-ni choe3 in e5 tiau7-thau5; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[25]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 bin7 ng3 A-bun5 chok8, soan-thoan5 kong-kek in, kong2, Lin2 tioh8 thiaN Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7;  3). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 siu7 phah la5-sam5, I2-sek-liat8 toe7 tu2-tioh8 pha-hng, Iu5-tai7-ke hou7 lang5 liah8; hit-si5 li2 in-ui7 chiah e5 su7, eng7 oe7 kong-kek in kong2, Hou7--chai7!  4). KhoaN3 ah, sou2-i2 Goa2 beh chiong li2 kau hou7 tang-hng e5 lang5 choe3-giap8; in beh ti7 li2 e5 sou2-chai7 chat-iaN5 khia7-khi2, chiah8 li2 e5 ke2-chi2, lim li2 e5 leng.  5). Goa2 beh hou7 Lah8-pa choe3 lok8-to5 e5 tiau5, hou7 A-bun5 chok8 e5 toe7 choe3 iuN5-kun5 to2 e5 sou2-chai7; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  6). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 li2 tah-chhiu2 tng3-kha, moa2-sim biau2-si7, ng3 I2-sek-liat8 toe7 hoaN-hi2;  7). khoaN3 ah, sou2-i2 Goa2 chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kong-kek li2, chiong li2 kau hou7 liat8-kok chhiuN2--khi3; Goa2 beh tui3 liat8-pang-tiong chian2-tu5 li2, hou7 li2 ti7 ban7-kok-tiong pai7-bo5; Goa2 beh tu5-biat8 li2; li2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	8). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 Mou5-ap kap Se-jiN2 u7 teh kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Iu5-tai7-ke kap cheng3-kok bo5 koh-iuN7;  9). khoaN3 ah, in-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 beh khui Mou5-ap e5 pian-kai3 tui3 chiah e5 siaN5, tui3 i pian-kai3 chiah e5 siaN5, choe3 i pun2-kok e5 eng5-kng--e5, chiu7-si7 Pek-ia5-se-boat8, Pa-lek8-bian2, Ki-liat8-teng5,  10). hou7 i kap A-bun5 chok8 long2 kau ti7 tang-hng e5 peh-siN3 choe3-giap8, hou7 A-bun5 chok8 bo5 koh siu7 ki3-liam7 ti7 liat8-pang-tiong.  11). Goa2 ia7 beh sim2-phoaN3 Mou5-ap; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	12). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 I2-tong e5 sou2-kiaN5, chiu7-si7 kong-kek Iu5-tai7-ke lai5 po3-siu5, tui3 in e5 po3-siu5 lai5 hoan7 tang7-choe7;  13). sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kong-kek I2-tong, chian2-tu5 in hia e5 lang5 kap cheng-siN; hou7 i pha-hng tui3 The5-ban7; kau3 Ti2-tan3 lang5 long2 si2 ti7 to-e7.  14). Koh Goa2 beh eng7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chhiu2, lai5 po3 Goa2 e5 kiu5-siu5 ti7 I2-tong; in beh chiau3 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3, chiau3 Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, lai5 kiaN5 ti7 I2-tong; chiu7 in beh chai Goa2 e5 po3-siu5; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 kiaN5 po3-siu5, chun5-sim biau2-si7 lai5 po3-siu5, kiat si2-oan3 beh chau5-biat8--in;  16). sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chhun Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kong-kek Hui-li7-su7 lang5; Goa2 beh chian2-tu5 Ki-the5 lang5, biat8-bo5 ian5-hai2 sou2 chhun e5 peh-siN3.  17). Goa2 beh eng7 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 chek-hoat8, tui3 in kiaN5 toa7 e5 po3-siu5; Goa2 tui3 in po3-siu5 e5 si5, in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[26]	Te7 chap8-it ni5, geh8 e5 chhoe-it, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, in-ui7 Chhui-lo5 ng3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kong2, Hou7--chai7! hit-e5 choe3 liat8-pang e5 mng5--e5, i2-keng phoa3, taN kui-ng3 goa2; i i2-keng pha-hng, goa2 beh hong-seng7.  3). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chhui-lo5 ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 kap li2 choe3 tui3-tek8, Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 choe7-choe7 kok khi2-lai5 kong-kek li2, chhin-chhiuN7 hai2 hou7 i e5 eng2 gia5--khi2-lai5 chit8-iuN7.  4). In beh hui2-hoai7 Chhui-lo5 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5, thiah i e5 chiu2-kiN-lau5; Goa2 iah8 beh khau i e5 thou5-hun2, hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 kng-ko7-ko7 e5 chioh8-poaN5.  5). I beh ti7 hai2-tiong choe3 phak8-bang7 e5 sou2-chai7, iah8 beh chiaN5-choe3 liat8-kok sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8; in-ui7 Goa2 u7 kong2--i; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  6). Siok8 ti7 Chhui-lo5 hiah e5 siaN5 e5 peh-siN3, beh hou7 to-kiam3 thai5-si2; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  7). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 liat8-ong5 e5 ong5, chiu7-si7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, tui3 pak-hng chhoa7 be2, chhia, be2-peng, kun-tui7, kap choe7-choe7 peh-siN3, lai5 kong-kek Chhui-lo5.  8). I beh eng7 to-kiam3 thai5-si2 siok8 ti7 li2 hiah e5 siaN5 e5 peh-siN3, iah8 beh chat-iaN5 kong-kek li2, khi2 tho5-tui kong-kek li2, koaN7-tin5 kong-kek li2.  9). I beh an-siat kong3-siaN5 e5 thui5, kong-phoa3 li2 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5, eng7 pou2-thau5 thiah-hui2 li2 e5 chiu2-kiN-lau5.  10). In-ui7 i e5 be2 chin-choe7, thou5-hun2 jia-kham3 li2; i jip8 li2 e5 siaN5-mng5, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 jip8 u7 phoa3-khiah e5 siaN5, hit-si5 in-ui7 khia5-be2--e5, kap un7-niu5-chhia, chian3-chhia e5 siaN, li2 e5 siaN5 beh tin2-tang7.  11). I e5 be2-toe5 beh thun2-tah8 li2 it-chhe3 e5 koe-lou7; i beh eng7 to thai5-si2 li2 e5 peh-siN3, li2 kian-kou3 e5 thiau7 beh to2 ti7 thou5-kha.  12). I beh chhiuN2 li2 e5 chai5-po2, kap li2 e5 he3-mih8, hui2 li2 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5, thiah li2 sui2 e5 chhu3, koh chiong li2 chiah e5 chioh8, chiah e5 chha5, chiah e5 thou5, long2 hiat ti7 chui2-tiong.  13). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 chhiuN3-koa e5 siaN long2 soah, li2 toaN5-khim5 e5 siaN bo5 koh thiaN-kiN3.  14). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 chiaN-choe3 kng-ko7-ko7 e5 chioh8-poaN5, choe3 phak8-bang7 e5 sou2-chai7; li2 bo5 koh siu7 khi2-cho7, in-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--i.  Che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Chhui-lo5 an2-ni kong2, Ti7 li2 tiong-kan u7 toa7-toa7 thai5-lang5 e5 su7, siu7-siong e5 lang5 ai-ai-chhan e5 si5, in-ui7 li2 to2-hoai7 e5 siaN, hai2-su7 kiam2 bo5 long2 tin2-tang7 mah?  16). Hit-si5 hai2-piN hiah e5 kun-ong5, beh tui3 i e5 ong5-ui7 loh8--lai5, tu5-khi3 i e5 le2-hok8, thng3--khi3 sui2 saN, chheng7 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, che7 ti7 thou5-kha, si5-si5 khek-khek teh tio7, ui7-tioh8 li2 gong5-ngiah8.  17). In beh ui7 li2 choe3 ai-ko, tui3 li2 kong2, Li2 chit e5 u7 mia5-siaN e5 siaN5, peng5-sou3 si7 kiaN5-chun5 e5 lang5 sou2 khia7-khi2, ti7 hai2-bin7 choe3 kian-kou3--e5; peng5-jit8 i kap khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, hou7 it-chhe3 tiam3 ti7-hia e5 lang5 bo5 m7 kiaN-hiaN5, taN chaiN2-iuN7 biat8-bo5 ah!  18). TaN ti7 li2 chit e5 to2-hoai7 e5 jit8, cheng3 hai2-su7 beh ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah; hai2-tiong chiah e5 hai2-su7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 bo5--khi3, chiu7 long2 kiaN-hiaN5.  19). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 hou7 li2 choe3 pha-hng e5 siaN5, chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 hiah e5 bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5; koh hou7 chhim-ian poaN5-ke3 li2, toa7-chui2 kham3-bat8 li2.  20). Hit-si5 Goa2 hou7 li2 kap hiah e5 loh8 im-hu2--e5 saN-kap loh8--khi3, kau3 kou2-cha2 lang5 hia; hou7 li2 tiam3 ti7 toe7-e7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7, tui3 kou2-cha2 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7, kap hiah e5 loh8 im-hu2 e5 lang5 ti7-teh, bo5 koh u7 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 bo5 koh u7 eng5-kng.  21). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 choe3 thang kiaN--e5, bo5 koh lau5 ti7 se3-kan; sui-jian5 lang5 chhe7 li2, iah8 eng2-eng2 chhe7-boe7-tioh8; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[27]	 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, tioh8 ui7 Chhui-lo5 choe3 ai-ko,  3). ka7 Chhui-lo5 kong2, Li2 khia7-khi2 hai2-khau2, kap liat8-kok cheng3 hai2-su7 boe2-boe7 choe3 seng-li2; Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: Chhui-lo5 ah, li2 bat kong2, Goa2 si7 oan5-choan5 sui2--e5.  4). Li2 e5 keng2-kai3 ti7 hai2-tiong; khi2-cho7 li2 e5, hou7 li2 e5 sui2 oan5-choan5.  5). In eng7 Si7-ni5-jiN2 e5 chheng5-chhiu7 choe3 li2 it-chhe3 e5 pang, eng7 Li7-pa-lun3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7 choe3 li2 e5 chun5-ui5.  6). Eng7 Pa-san e5 siong7-chhiu7 choe3 li2 e5 chiuN2, eng7 Ki-the5 hai2-su7 e5 ng5-iong5-chha5, jip8 chhiuN7-ge5 choe3 li2 che7 e5 pang.  7). Eng7 Ai-kip8 siu3-hoe e5 iu3-toe7-pou3 choe3 li2 e5 phang5, choe3 li2 e5 ki5; eng7 I2-li7-sa hai2-su7 lam5-sek chi2-sek e5 pou3, choe3 li2 e5 liang5-piN5.  8). Se-tun3 kap A-hoat khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, choe3 li2 e5 ko3-chiuN2--e5; li2 tiong-kan gau5 e5 lang5 choe3 li2 e5 hoaN7-toa7--e5.  9). Ka-pa-lek8 lau2-lian7--e5 kap gau5 e5 lang5, long2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan choe3 pou2 chun5-khang--e5; it-chhe3 ke3-hai2 e5 chun5-chiah, kap in e5 chui2-siu2, long2 ti7 li2 tiong-kan keng-eng5 seng-li2 e5 su7.  10). Pho-su, Lou7-tek, Hut e5 lang5, ti7 li2 kun-iaN5-tiong choe3 chian3-su7; in ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan kui3 tin5-pai5 kap thau5-khoe, hian2-beng5 li2 e5 sui2.  11). A-hoat lang5 kap li2 e5 kun-tui7, long2 ti7 li2 si3-ui5 e5 chhiuN5-teng2; li2 e5 chiu2-kiN-lau5 iah8 u7 iong2-su7, in kui3 in e5 tin5-pai5 ti7 li2 si3-ui5 e5 chhiuN5-piah, seng5-choan5 li2 e5 sui2.  12). Tha-si lang5 in-ui7 tak8-iuN7 e5 chai5-but8 chhiong-chiok, chiu7 choe3 li2 e5 kheh-siong; toa3 gun5, thih, siah, ian5, lai5 oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  13). Nga2-oan5 lang5, Thou2-pa lang5, Bi2-siat lang5, long2 kap li2 kau-koan; in eng7 jin5-khau2 kap tang5-khi3, lai5 oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  14). To-ka-ma2 chok8 eng7 be2, kap chian3-be2, kap lo5, lai5 oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  15). Ti2-tan3 lang5 kap li2 kau-koan; choe7-choe7 hai2-su7 choe3 li2 e5 e7-poaN5 seng-li2; in toa3 chhiuN7-ge5, ou-bak8-chha5, kap li2 kau-oaN7.  16). A-lan5 lang5 in-ui7 li2 e5 che3-cho7 chhiong-chiok, chiu7 choe3 li2 e5 kheh-siong; in eng7 lek8-po2-chioh8, chi2-sek e5 pou3, siu3-hoe e5 mih8, iu3-toe7-pou3, sian-ho5, ang5-po2-chioh8, lai5 oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  17). Iu5-tai7 kap I2-sek-liat8 toe7 e5 lang5, long2 kap li2 kau-koan; in eng7 Bi2-lek8 e5 beh8, piaN2, bit8, iu5, ju2-hiuN, lai5 oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  18). Tai7-ma2-sek lang5 in-ui7 li2 e5 che3-cho7 chhiong-chiok, koh in-ui7 tak8-iuN7 e5 chai5-but8 chhiong-chiok; chiu7 toa3 Hek-pun2 e5 chiu2, kap peh8 iuN5-mng5, kap li2 kau-koan.  19). Ui-tan3 lang5 kap Nga2-oan5 lang5, toa3 soaN3 kap kng e5 thih, jiok8-kui3, chhiong-pou5, ti7 li2 e5 koe-chhi7, oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  20). Ti2-tan3 lang5 eng7 sui2 e5 be2-oaN-chu7 kap li2 kau-koan.  21). A-lah8-pek lang5 kap Ki-tat8 it-chhe3 e5 leng2-siu3, long2 choe3 li2 e5 e7-poaN5 seng-li2; eng7 iuN5-ko, kang e5 mi5-iuN5, soaN-iuN5, kap li2 kau-koan.  22). Si7-pa kap Lah8-ma2 e5 seng-li2 lang5 kap li2 kau-koan; in eng7 tak8-lui7 siong7-ho2 e5 hiuN-liau7, tak8-lui7 e5 po2-chioh8 kap ng5-kim lai5 oaN7 li2 e5 he3-mih8.  23). Hap-lan5, Kan-ni5, I-tian5 lang5, Si7-pa e5 seng-li2 lang5, A-sut8 lang5, Ki-boat lang5 kap li2 kau-koan.  24). Chiah e5 seng-li2 lang5 eng7 chin-ho2 e5 he3-mih8, lam5-sek siu3-hoe e5 pou3, chng kui-pau; koh u7 sui2 e5 i-hok8, chng ti7 pek-hiuN-chha5 e5 siuN-a2-lai7, eng7 soh pak8-i, kap li2 kau-koan.  25). Tha-si e5 chun5-chiah tau3 kui-pang, ka7 li2 chai3-he3; li2 chiu7 ti7 hai2-tiong pu3-u7, kek8-ki5 eng5-kng.  26). Li2 e5 ko3-chiuN2--e5, i2-keng ko3 li2 kau3 toa7-chui2 e5 sou2-chai7; tang-hong ti7 hai2-tiong ka7 li2 kong3-phoa3.  27). Li2 e5 chiN5-chai5, li2 e5 mih8-kiaN7, li2 e5 he3-phin2, li2 e5 chui2-siu2, li2 e5 hoaN7-toa7--e5, li2 e5 that chun5-khang--e5, li2 e5 keng-eng5 seng-li2--e5, i2-kip8 li2 tiong-kan e5 chian3-su7, kap li2 tiong-kan e5 cheng3-lang5, ti7 li2 pai7-hoai7 e5 jit8, long2 beh tim5 ti7 hai2-tiong.  28). Li2 hoaN7-toa7--e5 au5-kio3 e5 siaN chit8-e7 hoah, kau-ia2 long2 beh tin2-tang7.  29). KiN3-na7 ko3-chiuN2-e5, kap chui2-siu2, kap it-chhe3 ke3-hai2 hoaN7-toa7--e5, long2 beh li7-khui chun5 chiuN7-hoaN7.  30). In beh ui7 li2 khui-siaN toa7-khau3, sam2 thou5-hun2 ti7 thau5-khak, ko7 ti7 he2-hu-tiong.  31). Koh ui7-tioh8 li2 lai5 thi3 kng-thau5, eng7 moa5-pou3 ha5-io, thong3-sim thi5-khau3, kek8-ki5 pi-ai.  32). In ai-siong e5 si5, ui7-tioh8 li2 choe3 ai-ko, thi5-khau3 li2; kong2, U7 sim2-mih8 siaN5 chhin-chhiuN7 Chhui-lo5, chhin-chhiuN7 i ti7 hai2-tiong chiaN5-choe3 cheng7 chhiN-chhiN--e5 ah?  33). Li2 e5 he3-mih8 tui3 hai2-bin7 chiuN7-soaN, chiu7 hou7 choe7-choe7 peh-siN3 chhiong-chiok; li2 eng7 choe7-choe7 chiN5-chai5 he3-mih8, hou7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 kun-ong5 ho2-giah8.  34). Li2 ti7 chhim-chui2-tiong hou7 hai2-eng2 long3-phoa3 e5 si5, li2 e5 he3-mih8, kap li2 tiong-kan it-chhe3 e5 cheng3-lang5, chiu7 long2 tim5--loh8-khi3.  35). Hai2-su7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, ui7-tioh8 li2 gong5-ngiah8; in e5 kun-ong5 long2 chin kiaN, bin7 tai3-iu-iong5.  36). Liat8-kok e5 seng-li2 lang5, long2 beh chhut ki-chhi3 e5 siaN; li2 hou7 lang5 thang kiaN, li2 bo5 thang koh ti7-teh tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.

[28]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 Chhui-lo5 e5 kun-ong5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: In-ui7 li2 sim-lai7 kiau-ngou7, li2 iah8 kong2, Goa2 si7 chit8 e5 siong7-te3, goa2 ti7 hai2-tiong che7 Siong7-te3 e5 ui7; li2 sui-jian5 chun5-sim ka-ki7 liah8-choe3 si7 Siong7-te3, ki5-sit8 li2 si7 lang5, m7-si7 Siong7-te3.  3). KhoaN3 ah, li2 pi2 Tan7-i2-li2 khah u7 ti3-hui7, bo5 chit8-hang7 pi3-bit8 e5 su7 tui3 li2 un2-bat8.  4). Li2 oa2-kho3 ka-ki7 e5 ti3-hui7 chhang-mia5, tit-tioh8 chai5-po2, tit-tioh8 kim-gun5, siu ti7 li2 e5 khou3-pang5.  5). Li2 oa2-kho3 ka-ki7 e5 toa7 ti3-hui7 kap seng-li2, ke-thiN li2 e5 ho2-giah8; iah8 li2 e5 sim ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 ho2-giah8 lai5 kiau-ngou7.  6). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 li2 chun5-sim, ka-ki7 liah8-choe3 si7 Siong7-te3,  7). khoaN3 ah, sou2-i2 Goa2 beh toa3 goa7-pang lang5, chiu7-si7 liat8-kok-tiong kiong5-po7 e5 lang5, lai5 li2 chia; in beh puih8-to kong-kek li2 tui3 ti3-hui7 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 ho2-mih8; phah la5-sam5 li2 e5 eng5-kng.  8). In beh hou7 li2 loh8 chhim-khiN; li2 beh si2 ti7 hai2-tiong, chhin-chhiuN7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 e5 si2 chit8-iuN7.  9). Ti7 thai5 li2 e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 iau2-be7 kong2, Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3 mah? ki5-sit8 li2 ti7 thai5-si2 li2 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, put-ko3 si7 lang5, m7-si7 Siong7-te3.  10). Li2 beh si2, ti7 goa7-kok lang5 e5 chhiu2-tiong, chhin-chhiuN7 be7 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 e5 si2 chit8-iuN7, in-ui7 Goa2 u7 kong2 i; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2-e5.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  12). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 ka7 Chhui-lo5 ong5 choe3 ai-ko, tui3 i kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 bo5 sou2 m7 chiau5-pi7, ti3-hui7 chhiong-chiok, oan5-choan5 sui2.  13). Li2 bat ti7 Ai-tian5 Siong7-te3 e5 hng5-lai7, eng7 tak8-iuN7 e5 po2-chioh8 choe3 li2 e5 chng-thaN7, chiu7-si7 ang5-po2-chioh8, ng5-gek8, kap kim-kong-chioh8, chhiN-gek8, ang5-be2-lo2, kap phek-gek8, lam5-gek8, lek8-po2-chioh8, kap chhiah-gek8, kap ng5-kim; koh li2 kou2 kap siau, ti7 li2 hia che3-cho7, tng li2 siu7-cho7 e5 jit8, chiu7 long2 chiau5-pi7.  14). Li2 si7 hit e5 siu7 boah-iu5 jia-kham3 e5 ki-lou7-peng; Goa2 an-ti3 li2 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 seng3-soaN; li2 ong2-lai5 ti7 chhut-he2 e5 chioh8 e5 tiong-kan.  15). Li2 tui3 siu7-cho7 e5 jit8 sou2 kiaN5 long2 oan5-choan5, tit8-kau3 chhe7-tioh8 put-gi7 ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan.  16). In-ui7 li2 seng-li2 chin-toa7, lang5 chiu7 eng7 kiong5-po7 chhiong-moa2 ti7 li2 e5 tiong-kan, ti3-kau3 li2 hoan7-choe7; in-ui7 an2-ni, Goa2 khoaN3 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 u3-oe3, chiu7 tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 soaN koaN2-tiok8 li2; jia-kham3 e5 ki-lou7-peng ah, Goa2 i2-keng chiong li2 tui3 chhut-he2 e5 chioh8 e5 tiong-kan tu5-biat8.  17). Li2 in-ui7 sui2, sim-tiong kiau-ngou7; koh in-ui7 li2 e5 eng5-kng pai7-hoai7 li2 e5 ti3-hui7; Goa2 i2-keng chhia-to2 li2 ti7 toe7--nih, hou7 li2 to2 ti7 kun-ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 in khoaN3-kiN3.  18). Li2 in-ui7 choe7-koa3 chin-choe7, choe3 seng-li2 bo5 kong-to7; li2 phah la5-sam5 li2 hiah e5 seng3-sou2; sou2-i2 Goa2 hou7 he2 tui3 li2 tiong-kan chhut, lai5 sio-biat8 li2; hou7 li2 ti7 sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, pian3-choe3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 he2-hu.  19). Cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, kiN3-na7 bat li2 e5 lang5, long2 beh ui7-tioh8 li2 lai5 gong5-ngiah8; li2 hou7 lang5 thang kiaN, eng2-oan2 bo5 thang koh ti7-teh.
	20). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  21). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 e5 bin7 tioh8 ng3 Se-tun3, tui3 i soan-thoan5, kong2,  22). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Se-tun3 ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 kap li2 choe3 tui3-tek8, Goa2 tek-khak ti7 li2 tiong-kan tit-tioh8 eng5-kng; Goa2 ti7 i tiong-kan kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3, hian2-beng5 Goa2 choe3-seng3 e5 si5, in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  23). Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 un-ek8 kap lau5-huih e5 su7 jip8 i e5 koe-lou7, tioh8-siong--e5 to2 ti7 i e5 tiong-kan, si3-ui5 u7 to-kiam3 kong-kek i; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  24). Si3-ui5 peng5-sou3 khoaN3-khin I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 lang5, i2-au7 bo5 koh ng3 in choe3 chhak8 lang5 e5 chhi3, hou7 lang5 kan-khou2 e5 chhau2-chhi3; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	25). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 chu7-chip8 I2-sek-liat8-ke, tui3 sou2 si3-soaN3--khi3 e5 peh-siN3-tiong, tui3 in hian2-beng5 Goa2 choe3-seng3, ti7 liat8-kok lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5; hit-si5 in beh khia7-khi2 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok e5 toe7.  26). In beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2 ti7 hi2 tiong-kan; Goa2 i2-keng kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3 ti7 si3-ui5 khoaN3-khin in e5 lang5, hit-si5 in beh khi2 chhu3, chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5, an-jian5 khia7-khi2; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in e5 Siong7-te3.

[29]	Te7 chap8--ni5, chap8-geh8 chap8-ji7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 e5 bin7 tioh8 ng3 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2, soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek i, i2-kip8 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7.  3). Li2 tioh8 thoan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 ah, Goa2 choe3 li2 e5 tui3-tek8; li2 chiu7-si7 toa7 gok8-hi5, to2 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 kang-ho5 tiong; li2 bat kong2, Goa2 e5 ho5 si7 goa2-e5, goa2 ui7 ka-ki7 lai5 cho7--e5.  4). Goa2 beh eng7 kau kau-tiau5 li2 e5 ge5-cho5; koh hou7 li2 kang-ho5-tiong e5 hi5 khah8-tiau5 ti7 li2 e5 lan5; Goa2 beh chiong li2 kap sou2 khah8-tiau5 ti7 li2 e5 lan5 e5 hi5, tui3 kang-ho5 tiong thoa chhut-lai5.  5). Goa2 beh chiong li2 kap li2 kang-ho5-tiong e5 hi5 long2 hiat ti7 khong3-ia2; li2 beh to2 ti7 chhan5--nih, bo5 khioh choe3-tui, bo5 siu-sip8; Goa2 chiong li2 hou7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3, khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  6). Ai-kip8 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 beh chai Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 in tui3 I2-sek-liat8-ke, bat choe3 lou5-ui2 e5 koaiN2-a2.  7). In eng7 chhiu2 kiah8 li2, li2 pit-khui, siong-tioh8 in e5 keng-thau5, in oa2--li2, li2 chih8-khi3, siam5-tioh8 in e5 io.  8). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 li2; tui3 lin2 tiong-kan chian2-tu5 lang5 kap cheng-siN.  9). Ai-kip8 toe7 beh hong-hoe3, leng2-cheng7; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 i ka-ki7 kong2, Chit e5 ho5 si7 goa2-e5, si7 goa2 cho7--e5.  10). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 kap li2 i2-kip8 li2 e5 kang-ho5 choe3 tui3-tek8; hou7 Ai-kip8 toe7 tui3 Sek-hut-ni5 e5 thah, tit8-kau3 Kou2-sit8 e5 kau-kai3 choan5-jian5 hong-hoe3 leng2-cheng7.  11). Lang5 e5 kha bo5 tui3 hia ke3, siu3 e5 kha ia7 bo5 tui3 hia ke3; lek8-ke3 si3-chap8-ni5 ku2, bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.  12). Goa2 beh hou7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ti7 leng2-cheng7 e5 toe7 chiaN5-choe3 leng2-cheng7; i e5 siaN5 ti7 hong-hoe3 e5 siaN5 tiong piN3-choe3 hong-hoe3, lek8-ke3 si3-chap8-ni5, Goa2 ia7 beh chiong Ai-kip8 lang5 hun-soaN3 ti7 liat8-kok, si3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-pang.  13). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Moa2 si3-chap8-ni5, Goa2 beh chio-chip8 Ai-kip8 lang5, tui3 in sou2 si3-soaN3--khi3 e5 liat8-kok lai5;  14). Goa2 beh hou7 Ai-kip8 siu7-liah8--e5 to3-lai5, hou7 in to3-lai5 in e5 pun2-toe7 Pa-thek-lo5; ti7-hia beh chiaN5-choe3 bi5-soe3 e5 kok.  15). Beh choe3 liat8-kok-tiong te7-it bi5-soe3--e5, iah8 bo5 koh chu7-ko ti7 liat8-kok e5 teng2-bin7; Goa2 beh kiam2-chio2 in, ti3-kau3 in bo5 koan2-hat liat8-kok.  16). I tek-khak bo5 koh choe3 I2-sek-liat8-ke sou2 oa2-kho3--e5, sou2 oat8-thau5 lai5 giong2-bong7-e5, bian2-tit Goa2 ki3-tit in e5 choe7; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	17). Ji7-chap8-chhit ni5, chiaN-geh8 chhoe-it, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  18). Jin5-chu2 ah, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5, Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, hou7 i e5 kun-peng toa7-toa7 tioh8-boa5, kong-kek Chhui-lo5; ti3-kau3 tak8-e5 thau5-khak bo5 mng5, keng-thau5 liu3-phe5; chong2-si7 i kap i e5 kun-peng, tui3 ti7 Chhui-lo5, long2 bo5 tit-tioh8 kang-chiN5, lai5 po3-tap i toa7-toa7 tioh8-boa5 e5 kong-kek.  19). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 toe7 siuN2-su3 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat, i beh liah8 i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, chhiuN2 i sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, kiap i sou2 kiap e5 mih8, che chiu7 thang choe3 i e5 kun-peng e5 kang-chiN5.  20). Goa2 chiong Ai-kip8 toe7 hou7 i, po3-tap i sou2 tioh8-boa5--e5; in-ui7 in thoe3 Goa2 choe3-kang; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2-e5.
	21). Tng hit-jit8, Goa2 beh hou7 chit8 ki kak, ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8 ke hoat-chhut; koh beh hou7 li2 khui-chhui3 ti7 in tiong-kan; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[30]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Chham2 ah chit-jit8, lin2 tioh8 thi5-khau3.  3). In-ui7 jit8 kun7--lah, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8 kun7--lah8, chiu7-si7 bat8-hun5 e5 jit8, beh choe3 liat8-kok e5 si5-ki5.  4). Beh u7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 Ai-kip8, ti7 Ai-kip8 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 to2--loh8-khi3 e5 si5, Kou2-sit8 lang5 chiu7 u7 thong3-khou2; in beh liah8 i e5 cheng3-lang5, thiah-hui2 i e5 toe7-ki.  5). Kou2-sit8, Hut, Lou7-tek, chham-chhap e5 peh-siN3, kap Kou2-pa, i2-kip8 tong5-beng5 e5 kok e5 peh-siN3, long2 beh kap in saN-kap to2 ti7 to-e7.
	6). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Hu5-chou7 Ai-kip8--e5 iah8 beh to2; i se3-lek8 e5 kiau-ngou7 beh kang3-ke7; tui3 Sek-hut-ni5 e5 thah khi2, in long2 beh ti7-hia to2 ti7 to-e7; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  7). In beh ti7 leng2-cheng7 e5 toe7 e5 tiong-kan, lai5 choe3 leng2-cheng7; i chiah e5 siaN5 iah8 beh liat8 ti7 chiah e5 hong-hoe3 e5 siaN5 e5 tiong-kan.  8). Tng Goa2 pang3-he2 ti7 Ai-kip8, kiN3-na7 pang-chan7 i--e5, long2 siu7 biat8-bo5; hit-si5, in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  9). Kau3 hit-jit8 beh u7 su3-chia2 tui3 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tah-chun5 chhut-khi3; hou7 an-jian5 khia7-khi2 e5 Kou2-sit8 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5; beh u7 thong3-khou2 lim5-kau3 in, chhin-chhiuN7 Ai-kip8 e5 jit8 chit8-iuN7; khoaN3 ah, tai7-chi3 lai5--lah.
	10). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh eng7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 Ni5-pou3-kah-ni5-sat e5 chhiu2, biat8 Ai-kip8 e5 cheng3-lang5.  11). I kap te3 i e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 liat8-kok-tiong kiong5-po7-e5, beh lai5 hui2-biat8 chit e5 toe7; in beh puih8-to kong-kek Ai-kip8, hou7 pian3-toe7 u7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5.  12). Goa2 beh hou7 hiah e5 kang-ho5 ta, iah8 beh eng7 hit e5 toe7 boe7 hou7 phaiN2-lang5 e5 chhiu2; Goa2 beh eng7 goa7-pang e5 chhiu2 hou7 hit e5 toe7 kap ki5-tiong sou2 u7--e5, piN3-choe3 leng2-cheng7; che si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	13). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh hui2-biat8 hiah e5 ngou2-siong7, tui3 Lo5-hut tu5-biat8 sin5-put8; tek-khak bo5 koh u7 kun-ong5 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhut; Goa2 beh kang3-loh8 kiaN-hiaN5 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7.  14). Goa2 beh hou7 Pa-thek-lo5 leng2-cheng7; pang3-he2 ti7 So2-an e5 tiong-kan; kiaN5 sim2-phoaN3 e5 su7 ti7 Lo5 e5 toe7-hng.  15). Goa2 beh piaN3-chhut Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 Sin3, chiu7-si7 Ai-kip8 e5 oe7-sou2; iah8 beh biat8 Lo5 e5 cheng3-lang5.  16). Goa2 beh pang3-he2 ti7 Ai-kip8, Sin3 beh tu2-tioh8 toa7 thong3-khou2; Lo5 beh tu2-tioh8 kong-phoa3, Lo5-hut tng-thau5 peh8-jit8 tu2-tioh8 tui3-tek8.  17). A-bun5 kap Pi2-pek-sit8 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, beh to2 ti7 to-e7; in beh hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3.  18). Goa2 ti7 Tap-pi2-lek8 at-chih8 Ai-kip8 chiah e5 taN, hou7 i in-ui7 se3-lek8 e5 kiau-ngou7, soah ti7 i e5 tiong-kan; hit-si5 ti7-hia jit8 ou-am3; lun7-kau3 chit e5 siaN5, beh u7 bat8-hun5 jia-kham3; i tiong-kan e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 beh hou7 lang5 liah8--khi3.  19). Goa2 beh an2-ni sim2-phoaN3 Ai-kip8; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	20). Chap8-it-ni5, chiaN-geh8 chhoe-chhit, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  21). Jin5-chu2 ah, Goa2 i2-keng at-chih8 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2-kut; bo5 pau i e5 siong, bo5 kou5-ioh8, bo5 chat pou3-liau5, thang hou7 i u7 lat8 kiah8-to.  22). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 kap Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 choe3 tui3-tek8, beh chiong i nng7 ki chhiu2-kut, iong2--e5, siu7 at-chih8--e5, beh choe3 chit8-e7 at-chih8; hou7 to tui3 i e5 chhiu2 ka-lauh8.  23). Goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 lang5 hun-soaN3 ti7 liat8-kok, si3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-pang.  24). Goa2 beh hou7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2-kut u7 lat8, chiong Goa2 e5 to kau ti7 i e5 chhiu2; Goa2 beh at-chih8 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2-kut, i beh ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 hiN-hiN-chhan, chhin-chhiuN7 siu7 si2-siong e5 lang5 hiN-hiN-chhan.  25). Goa2 beh hu5 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2-kut; Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2-kut beh se5-loh8-khi3; Goa2 chiong Goa2 e5 to kau ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 chhiu2; i beh chhun-chhut hit ki to ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7; hit-si5 in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  26). Goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 lang5 hun-soaN3 ti7 liat8-kok, si3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-pang; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[31]	Chap8-it--ni5, saN-geh8 chhoe-it, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2:  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2, i2-kip8 i e5 cheng3-lang5 kong2, Li2 hiah toa7-te3, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chi7-chui7?  3). KhoaN3 ah, A-sut8 bat choe3 Li7-pa-lun3 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7, ki-oaiN7 chin sui2, im3-ng2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-na5, chhiu7-sin koaiN5-toa7, ki-be2 chhun jip8 hun5-tiong.  4). Hiah e5 chui2 iuN2 i toa7-chang5, chhim-ian hou7 i hoat chin-koaiN5, i hiah e5 kang-ho5 seh8-lau5 ti7 chai-cheng3 i e5 sou2-chai7; thiah-chhe e5 chui2, lau5 kau3 chhan5-hng5 e5 chhiu7-bak8.  5). Sou2-i2 i koaiN5-toa7 poaN5-ke3 chhan5--nih e5 cheng3-chhiu7; i e5 ki chin-am7; i e5 oaiN7 chin-tng5; in-ui7 ti7 i hoat-siN e5 si5 u7 chui2 choe7-choe7.  6). Khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, long2 ti7 ki-teng2 choh-siu7; chhan5-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 long2 ti7 ki-e7 siN-kiaN2; choe7-choe7 toa7-kok long2 tiam3 ti7 i e5 im3-e7.  7). Chhiu7 toa7, ki tng5, chiaN5-choe3 chin sui2; in-ui7 kun soan ti7 toa7 chui2-piN.  8). Siong7-te3 hng5-lai7 e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7 jia i boe7-tioh8; chheng5-chhiu7 put-kip8 i e5 ki, png-chhiu7 put-kip8 i e5 oaiN7, Siong7-te3 hng5-lai7 chiah e5 chhiu7 long2 boe7 pi2-tit i e5 sui2.  9). Goa2 hou7 i e5 ki-oaiN7 bou7-seng7, chiaN5-choe3 sui2; ti3-kau3 Siong7-te3 hng5-lai7 Ai-tian5 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7, long2 oan3-tou3 i.  10). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 li2 koaiN5-toa7, ki-be2 chhun jip8 hun5-tiong, i e5 sim in-ui7 i e5 koaiN5-toa7 lai5 chu7-ko,  11). an2-ni, Goa2 beh chiong i kau ti7 liat8-kok tiong u7 toa7 se3-lek8--e5; i tek-khak beh pan7--i, in-ui7 i e5 choe7-ok, Goa2 koaN2-tiok8 i.  12). Goa7-pang-lang5, chiu7-si7 liat8-pang-tiong kiong5-po7--e5, chiong i chho3-tng7, hiat-kak8, i e5 oaiN7 ka-lauh8 ti7 soaN--nih kap it-chhe3 e5 soaN-kok-tiong; i e5 ki chih8 ti7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 ho5-piN; toe7-chiuN7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 i2-keng loh8-khi3, li7-khui i e5 im3-ng2.  13). Khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, long2 beh hioh ti7 chit e5 soe-pai7 e5 chhiu7-teng2; chhan5-ia2 e5 chau2-siu3 long2 beh toa3 ti7 i e5 chhiu7-ki;  14). thang hou7 chui2-piN chiah e5 chhiu7, bo5 in-ui7 koaiN5 toa7 lai5 chu7-ko; iah8 bo5 chiong ki-be2 chhun-jip8 hun5-tiong; koh hiah e5 tit-tioh8 chui2 lun7-tek8 u7 se3-lek8 e5, iah8 boe7 tit-tioh8 koaiN5-toa7 lai5 khia7--khi2-lai5; in-ui7 in ti7 se3-kan lang5 e5 tiong-kan, kap loh8 im-kan e5 lang5, long2 kau hou7 si2-bo5, kau3 chhim-chhim e5 toe7-e7.
	15). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I loh8 im-kan e5 hit-jit8, Goa2 hou7 lang5 pi-ai; Goa2 ui7-tioh8 i jia-kham3 chhim-ian, iok-sok kang-ho5, hou7 toa7-chui2 theng5-lau5; Goa2 iah8 hou7 Li7-pa-lun3 ui7-tioh8 i chhiN-chham2; chhan5-ia2 chiah e5 chhiu7 long2 in-ui7 i hun7-khi3.  16). Goa2 chiong i hiat-loh8 im-kan, kap loh8-khiN e5 lang5 saN-kap loh8--khi3; hit-si5 liat8-kok thiaN-kiN3 i tui7-loh8 e5 siaN, chiu7 long2 tin2-tang7; Ai-tian5 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7, Li7-pa-lun3 tit-tioh8 chui2 lun7-tek8, te7-it ho2 te7-it sui2 e5, long2 ti7 toe7-e7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7, siu7 an-ui3.  17). In iah8 kap i saN-kap loh8 im-kan, kau3 siu7 to thai5 e5 lang5 hia; in bat choe3 i e5 chhiu2-kut, ti7 liat8-kok-tiong khia7-khi2 i e5 im3-ng2-e7.
	18). Ti7 chiah-e5 eng5-kng koaiN5-toa7, ti7 Ai-tian5 chiah e5 chhiu7-tiong, li2 chhin-chhiuN7 chi7-chui7? chong2-si7 li2 beh kap Ai-tian5 chiah e5 chhiu7 saN-kap loh8-khi3 toe7-e7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7; li2 beh kap siu7 to thai5 e5 lang5, to2 ti7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.  Che chiu7-si7 Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[32]	Chap8-ji7--ni5, chap8-ji7-geh8, chhoe-it, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 ui7 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 choe3 ai-ko, ka7 i kong2, Chiong5-cheng5 li2 ti7 liat8-kok-tiong, chhin-chhiuN7 iong2 e5 sai; taN li2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-tiong e5 gok8-hi5; li2 chong5-chhut li2 e5 kang-ho5, eng7 kha tin2-tang7 chiah e5 chui2, ti3-kau3 kang-ho5 e5 chui2 piN3-lo5.  3). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh eng7 choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3, chiong Goa2 e5 bang7 pha ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7, in beh eng7 Goa2 e5 bang7, ka7 li2 thoa--chhut-lai5.  4). Goa2 beh hiat li2 ti7 toe7--nih, pang3-he7 ti7 chhan5-ia2, hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2 long2 hioh ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7; hou7 pian3-toe7 e5 ia2-siu3 chiah8 li2 kau3 pa2.  5). Goa2 beh chiong li2 e5 bah hiat ti7 soaN-nih, eng7 li2 koaiN5-toa7 e5 sin-si thun7-moa2 soaN-kok.  6). Goa2 koh beh eng7 li2 e5 huih, koan3-ak li2 sou2 siu5 e5 toe7; im-kau3 chiah e5 soaN; ho5-kau beh tui3 li2 lai5 chhiong-moa2.  7). Goa2 phah-biat8 li2 e5 si5, beh jia-kham3 chiah e5 thiN, hou7 cheng3 chhiN ou-am3; eng7 bat-hun5 jia-iam2 jit8-thau5, geh8 iah8 bo5 hoat-chhut kng.  8). Goa2 beh hou7 thiN e5 kng ti7 li2 e5 teng2-bin7 long2 ou-am3; koh hou7 li2 e5 toe7 ou-am3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  9). Goa2 hou7 li2 pai7-bo5 e5 hong-siaN kau3 li2 sou2 m7-bat e5 tak8-kok, hit-si5 Goa2 beh hou7 choe7-choe7 peh-siN3 e5 sim hoan5-lo2.  10). Goa2 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 bu2 Goa2 e5 kiam3 e5 si5, Goa2 beh hou7 choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3 ui7-tioh8 li2 gong5-ngiah8, kun-ong5 iah8 beh ui7-tioh8 li2 toa7 kiaN-hiaN5; ti7 li2 to2--loh8-khi3 e5 jit8, in tak8-lang5 ui7 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.  11). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Pa-pi2-lun5 ong5 e5 to beh lim5-kau3 li2.  12). Goa2 beh eng7 iong2-su7 e5 to hou7 li2 e5 choe7-choe7 lang5 to2--loh8-khi3.  Chiah e5 iong2-su7 long2 si7 liat8-kok-tiong kiong5-po7--e5; in beh hou7 Ai-kip8 e5 kiau-ngou7 kui ti7 bo5, Ai-kip8 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 beh siu7 chau5-biat8.  13). Goa2 beh tui3 Ai-kip8 choe7-choe7 chui2-piN tu5-biat8 sou2 u7 e5 chau2-siu3, lang5 e5 kha bo5 koh phah-lo5 chit e5 chui2, siu3 e5 toe5 iah8 bo5 koh tah8--i.  14). Hit-si5 Goa2 beh hou7 in e5 chui2 che7-chheng, hou7 in e5 ho5 lau5 chhin-chhiuN7 iu5; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  15). Goa2 hou7 Ai-kip8 toe7 hong-hoe3 leng2-cheng7, chit e5 toe7 choat8-bo5 chiong5-cheng5 sou2 chhiong-moa2--e5; koh Goa2 kong-kek ki5-tiong it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3; hit-si5 in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  16). Chit-e5 si7 ai-ko, lang5 beh eng7 chit-e5 lai5 ai-khau3; liat8-kok chiah e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 beh eng7 an2-ni lai5 ai-khau3; in ui7-tioh8 Ai-kip8 kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, iah8 beh eng7 chit-e5 lai5 ai-khau3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	17). Chap8-ji7--ni5, chap8-ji7 geh8 chap8-gou7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  18). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 in-ui7 Ai-kip8 e5 cheng3-lang5 ai-khau3; koh tioh8 chiong Ai-kip8 kap u7 mia5-siaN e5 kok chiah e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2, kap loh8-khiN e5 lang5, choe3 chit8-e7 hiat-loh8 toe7-e7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7.  19). Li2 e5 sui2 iaN5-ke3 chi7-chui7 ah? li2 tioh8 loh8-khi3, kap bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 saN-kap to2--teh.  20). In beh to2 ti7 hou7 to thai5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, i siu7 kau-hu3 ti7 to-kiam3, tioh8 chiong i kap i e5 cheng3-lang5 thoa--khi3.  21). Kiong5-beng2 e5 iong2-su7 beh ti7 im-kan tui3 i kap pang-chan7 i--e5 kong2-oe7; in si7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2, siu7 to thai5 e5 lang5; i2-keng loh8--khi3, to2-teh bo5 tin2-tang7.  22). A-sut8 kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, long2 ti7-hia; i e5 bong7 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5; in long2 si7 siu7-thai5, to2 ti7 to-e7--e5.  23). In e5 bong7 ti7 khiN-tiong kek8-chhim e5 sou2-chai7, i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 ti7 i e5 bong7 e5 si3-chiu-ui5, long2 si7 siu7-thai5 to2 ti7 to-e7--e5; in bat ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 hou7 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5.  24). I2-lan5 iah8 ti7-hia, i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 ti7 i e5 bong7 e5 si3-ui5, long2-si7 siu7-thai5, to2 ti7 to-e7, bo5 siu7 kat-le2 loh8-khi3 toe7-e7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7--e5; in bat ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 hou7 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5, koh kap loh8-khiN e5 lang5 saN-kap tam-tng leng5-jiok8.  25). In ka7 i kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, ti7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, an bin5-chhng5; in e5 bong7 ti7 i e5 si3-chiu-ui5; in long2 si7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2, siu7 to thai5--e5; in bat ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 hou7 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5, koh kap loh8-khiN e5 lang5 saN-kap tam-tng leng5-jiok8; i i2-keng he7 ti7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.  26). Bi2-siat, Thou2-pa, kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, long2 ti7-hia; i e5 bong7 long2 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5, in long2 si7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2, hou7 to thai5--e5; in bat ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7, hou7 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5.  27). In boe7 tit-tioh8 kap hiah e5 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 to2-teh e5 iong2-su7, saN-kap to2-teh; chiah e5 iong2-su7 toa3 ke-si loh8 im-kan; thau5-khak khun3 ti7 to-kiam3, kut-thau5-teng2 u7 in e5 choe7-ok; in bat ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7 hou7 iong2-su7 kiaN-hiaN5.  28). Li2 beh pai7-hoai7 ti7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, kap hiah-e5 siu7 to thai5 e5 lang5 saN-kap to2-teh.  29). I2-tong iah8 ti7-hia, i hiah e5 kok-ong5 kap it-chhe3 e5 siu2-leng2, sui-jian5 u7 se3-lek8, iu5-goan5 he7 ti7 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan; in beh kap bo5 siu7 kat-le2--e5, i2-kip8 loh8-khiN e5 lang5 saN-kap to2-teh.  30). Ti7-hia u7 pak-hng cheng3-ong5 e5 kiaN2, kap it-chhe3 Se-tun3 lang5, long2 kap siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 loh8-khi3; in sui-jian5 u7 se3-lek8, hou7 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5, iu5-goan5 siu7 kian3-siau3; in bo5 siu7 kat-le2, kap siu7 to thai5--e5 saN-kap to2-teh, kap loh8-khiN e5 lang5 saN-kap tam-tng leng5-jiok8.  31). Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 kun-peng long2 hou7 to thai5--si2; Hoat-lo2 khoaN3-kiN3, ui7-tioh8 i hiah e5 cheng3-lang5 chiu7 siu7 an-ui3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  32). Goa2 hou7 i ti7 oah8-lang5 e5 toe7, choe3 thang kiaN-hiaN5; Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 cheng3-lang5, beh kap siu7 to thai5 e5 lang5 saN-kap he7 ti7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[33]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 pun2-kok e5 peh-siN3 kong2-oe7, ka7 in kong2, Goa2 hou7 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 chit8-kok e5 si5, hi2 chit8-kok e5 peh-siN3 tui3 in tiong-kan keng2 chit8-lang5, siat-lip8 i choe3 siu2-bang7 e5;  3). i khoaN3-kiN3 to-kiam3 lim5-kau3 hit sou2-chai7, na7 pun5 sau3-kak keng2-kai3 cheng3 peh-siN3;  4). kiN3-na7 thiaN-kiN3 sau3-kak e5 siaN, bo5 siu7 keng2-kai3--e5, to-kiam3 na7 lai5 chau5-biat8 i, i e5 choe7 beh kui ti7 i e5 thau5-khak-teng2.  5). I thiaN-kiN3 sau3-kak e5 siaN, bo5 siu7 keng2-kai3, i e5 choe7 beh kui ti7 i pun2-sin; i na7 siu7 keng2-kai3, chiu7 oe7 kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7.  6). Siat-su2 siu2-bang7 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 to-kiam3 kau3, bo5 pun5 sau3-kak, ti3-kau3 peh-siN3 bo5 siu7 keng2-kai3, to-kiam3 lai5 thai5-si2 in tiong-kan e5 chit8-lang5, hit e5 lang5 sui-jian5 si2 ti7 i e5 choe7, chong2-si7 Goa2 beh tui3 siu2-bang7 e5 lang5 tho2 i sit-loh8 siN3-mia7 e5 choe7.  7). Jin5-chu2 ah, Goa2 an2-ni siat-lip8 li2 choe3 I2-sek-liat8-ke siu2-bang7 e5 lang5, sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 thiaN Goa2 chhui3-lai7 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, thoe3 Goa2 keng2-kai3 in.  8). Goa2 tui3 phaiN2-lang5 kong2, PhaiN2-lang5 ah, li2 tek-khak oe7 si2; li2 na7 bo5 khui-chhui3 keng2-kai3 phaiN2-lang5, hou7 i li7-khui sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7; chit e5 phaiN2-lang5 beh si2 ti7 i e5 choe7, chong2-si7 Goa2 beh tui3 li2 tho2 i sit-loh8 siN3-mia7 e5 choe7.  9). Siat-su2 li2 keng2-kai3 phaiN2-lang5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7; i iu5-goan5 m7 oat8-tng2 li7-khui, i beh si2 ti7 i e5 choe7, li2 chiu7 oe7 kiu3 li2 e5 oah8-mia7.
	10). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2, Lin2 siong5-siong5 an2-ni kong2, Goan2 e5 ke3-sit goan2 e5 choe7-ok, ti7 goan2 e5 sin-chiuN7; goan2 si7 in-ui7 an2-ni chiam7-chiam7 siau-bo5, thai2-tho2 oe7 oah8 ah?  11). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 toan3-toan3 bo5 hoaN-hi2 phaiN2-lang5 si2-bo5, tok8-tok8 hoaN-hi2 phaiN2-lang5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7 lai5 oah8; I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 tioh8 oat8-to3-tng2, li7-khui phaiN2-lou7, lin2 siaN2-su7 beh chhu2-si2 ah?  12). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 li2 e5 peh-siN3 kong2, Gi7-lang5 e5 gi7, ti7 i hoan7-choe7 e5 jit8 boe7-oe7 kiu3 i; lun7-kau3 phaiN2-lang5 e5 phaiN2, ti7 i oat8-tng2 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 jit8, iah8 boe7-oe7 hou7 i poah8-to2; gi7-lang5 ti7 hoan7-choe7 e5 jit8, ia7 boe7-oe7 in-ui7 i e5 gi7 lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8.  13). Goa2 tui3 gi7-lang5 kong2, i tek-khak oah8; i na7 oa2-kho3 i e5 gi7 lai5 kiaN5-phaiN2, chiu7 i sou2-kiaN5 e5 gi7, long2 bo5 tit-tioh8 ki3-liam7; i beh in-ui7 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2 lai5 si2.  14). Koh, Goa2 tui3 phaiN2-lang5 kong2, Li2 tek-khak si2, i na7 oat8-tng2 li7-khui i e5 choe7, kiaN5 cheng3-tit8 kap hap8-li2 e5 su7;  15). koh heng5 lang5 e5 tng3-thau5 kap sou2 chhiuN2 lang5 e5 mih8, chun-than3 oah8-mia7 e5 lut8-le7, bo5 koh choe3 phaiN2, i tek-khak oah8, bo5 ti3-kau3 si2.  16). I sou2 hoan7 it-chhe3 e5 choe7, bo5 koh ka7 i ki3-tit; i kiaN5 cheng3-tit8 kap hap8-li2 e5 su7, tek-khak oe7 oah8.  17). Li2 e5 peh-siN3 iau2 teh kong2, Chu2 e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5, ki5-sit8 si7 in e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5.  18). Gi7-lang5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui i e5 gi7, lai5 kiaN5-phaiN2; chiu7 beh in-ui7 an2-ni lai5 si2.  19). PhaiN2-lang5 oat8-tng2 li7-khui i e5 phaiN2, kiaN5 cheng3-tit8 kap hap8-li2 e5 su7; chiu7 beh in-ui7 an2-ni lai5 oah8.  20). Lin2 iau2 teh kong2, Chu2 e5 lou7 bo5 kong-peng5; I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, Goa2 beh chiau3 lin2 tak8-lang5 sou2-kiaN5--e5, sim2-phoaN3 lin2.
	21). Goan2 siu7 liah8 e5 liau2-au7 chap8-ji7-ni5, chap8-geh8 chhoe-gou7, u7 chit8-lang5 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 to5-chau2 kau3 goa2 chia; kong2, SiaN5 i2-keng kong-phoa3.  22). To5-chau2 e5 lang5 iau2-be7 kau3, cheng5 chit8-jit8 e5 e5-hng, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7; khui goa2 e5 chhui3; kau3 keh cha2-khi2, hit lang5 lai5 kau3 goa2 chia; goa2 e5 chhui3 chiu7 khui, bo5 koh e2-kau2.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  24). Jin5-chu2 ah, tiam3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 hong-hoe3 e5 toe7 e5 lang5 teh kong2, A-pek-lah8-han2 tok8-tok8 chit8-lang5, u7 tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8; lan2 lang5-giah8 chin-choe7, chit e5 toe7 si7 hou7 lan2 choe3-giap8--e5.  25). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lin2 chiah8 iau2 u7 huih e5 bah, koh kiah8-khi2 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu, giong2-bong7 lin2 e5 ngou2-siong7; koh thai5-lang5 lau5-huih, lin2 iau2 oe7 tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8 mah?  26). Lin2 oa2-kho3 lin2 e5 to-kiam3, kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7; lang5-lang5 phah la5-sam5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2; lin2 iau2 oe7 tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8 mah?  27). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in an2-ni kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7; ti7 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7--e5, beh to2 ti7 to-e7, ti7 chhan5-ia2 e5 tiong-kan--e5, Goa2 beh kau in hou7 ia2-siu3 thun-chiah8; ti7 oe7-sou2 kap tong7-lai7--e5, beh si2 ti7 un-ek8.  28). Goa2 beh hou7 chit e5 toe7 leng2-cheng7, hou7 lang5 gong5-ngiah8; i in-ui7 se3-lek8 e5 kiau-ngou7 ia7 beh soah; I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN long2 beh leng2-cheng7, bo5 lang5 keng-ke3.  29). Goa2 in-ui7 in sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, hou7 toe7 pha-hng; ti3-kau3 lang5 gong5-ngiah8; hit-si5 in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	30). Jin5-chu2 ah, Li2 e5 peh-siN3 ti7 chhu3-piN, ti7 chhu3 mng5-khau2, tam5-lun7 li2; hiaN-ti7 tui3 hiaN-ti7 saN-kap kong2, Lai5 ah, lai5 thiaN, thiaN-khoaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 si7 kong2 sim2-mih8.  31). In lai5 li2 chia, chhin-chhiuN7 peh-siN3 lai5 chu7-hoe7; che7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3; in thiaN li2 e5 oe7, iah8 bo5 khi3-kiaN5; in-ui7 in e5 chhui3 hian2-chhut choe7-choe7 chhin-ai3, chong2-si7 sim si7 teh jip8 chiN5.  32). KhoaN3 ah, in khoaN3 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 gau5 chok-gak8, ho2 siaN-im e5 lang5 sou2 chhiuN3 e5 nga2-ko; in thiaN li2 e5 oe7 ia7 bo5 khi3 kiaN5.  33). KhoaN3 ah, sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 kin2-kin2 beh chiaN5; kau3 chiaN5 e5 si5, in chiu7 chai bat u7 sian-ti ti7 in tiong-kan.

[34]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 kong-kek I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 bok8-chia2; li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 lai5 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 chiah e5 bok8-chia2 an2-ni kong2, Chai-e7 ah, I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 bok8-chia2, in-ui7 in iuN2-chhi7 ka-ki7; bok8-chia2 kiam2 m7 eng-kai iuN2-chhi7 iuN5-kun5 mah?  3). Lin2 chiah8 i e5 iu5, chheng7 i e5 mng5, thai5 i e5 pui5--e5, ia7 bo5 iuN2-chhi7 iuN5-kun5.  4). Loan2-jiok8--e5, lin2 bo5 kou3 hou7 i iong2; phoa3-piN7--e5, lin2 bo5 ka7 i i-ti7; siu7-siong--e5, lin2 bo5 ka7 i pau; siu7 koaN2-tiok8--e5, lin2 bo5 chhoa7 i to3--lai5, sit-loh8--e5, lin2 bo5 chhe7--i; tok8-tok8 eng7 kiong5-po7, giam5-giam5 e5 koan2-hat.  5). In-ui7 bo5 bok8-chia2, iuN5 chiu7 si3-soaN3; i2-keng si3-soaN3, chiu7 choe3 it-chhe3 ia2-siu3 e5 chiah8-mih8.  6). Goa2 e5 iuN5 si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 chiah e5 soaN--nih, ti7 tak8-e5 koaiN5 e5 soaN-teng2, si3-soaN3 ti7 choan5-toe7, bo5 lang5 khi3 tui, bo5 lang5 khi3 chhe7.  7). Sou2-i2 lin2 chiah e5 bok8-chia2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  8). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 e5 iuN5 in-ui7 bo5 bok8-chia2, chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 siu7-chhiuN2 e5 mih8, iuN5 ia7 choe3 it-chhe3 ia2-siu3 e5 chiah8-mih8; ia7 Goa2 e5 bok8-chia2 bo5 chhe7 Goa2 e5 iuN5; chiah e5 bok8-chia2 in-ui7 in iuN2-chhi7 ka-ki7, bo5 iuN2-chhi7 Goa2 e5 iuN5;  9). sou2-i2 lin2 chiah e5 bok8-chia2 tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7;  10). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 kap bok8-chia2 choe3 tui3-tek8, beh tui3 in e5 chhiu2 tui-tho2 Goa2 e5 iuN5, hou7 in bo5 koh iuN2-chhi7 iuN5-kun5; bok8-chia2 ia7 bo5 koh iuN2-chhi7 ka-ki7; Goa2 beh kiu3 Goa2 e5 iuN5 thoat-li7 in e5 chhui3, bo5 koh choe3 in e5 chiah8-mih8.  11). In-ui7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2, Goa2 beh pun2-sin chhe7 Goa2 e5 iuN5, lai5 chhe7-tioh8--i.  12). Bok8-chia2 ti7 iuN5-kun5 si3-soaN3 e5 jit8, chaiN2-iuN7 chhe7 i e5 iuN5, Goa2 ia7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni chhe7 Goa2 e5 iuN5; chiah e5 iuN5 ti7 bat8-hun5 ou-am3 e5 jit8, si3-soaN3 kau3 tak8 sou2-chai7, Goa2 beh tui3-hia kiu3 in to3--lai5.  13). Goa2 beh tui3 liat8-kok-tiong chhoa7 in chhut, tui3 tak8-kok e5 lai7-bin7 chu7-chip8 in, chhoa7 in to3-lai5 in e5 pun2 sou2-chai7; ia7 beh ti7 I2-sek-liat8 soaN chiah e5 khoe-piN, keng2-lai7 it-chhe3 thang khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, lai5 iuN2-chhi7 in.  14). Goa2 beh ti7 ho2-ho2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 iuN2-chhi7 in, in e5 iuN5-tiau5 beh ti7 I2-sek-liat8 koaiN5-ui7 e5 soaN; in beh ti7 ho2-ho2 e5 iuN5-tiau5-lai7 to2-teh-khun3, ia7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 soaN pui5-sui2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 chiah8-chhau2.  15). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh pun2-sin iuN2-chhi7 Goa2 e5 iuN5, hou7 in to2-teh-khun3.  16). Sit-loh8--e5 Goa2 beh chhe7 i; siu7 koaN2-tiok8--e5, Goa2 beh chhoa7 i to3-lai5; siu7-siong--e5 Goa2 beh pau--i; phoa3-piN7--e5, Goa2 beh i-ti7 i; tok8-tok8 pui5--e5, iong2--e5, Goa2 beh tu5-biat--i, ia7 beh peng2-kong iuN2-chhi7 in.  17). Goa2 e5 iuN5-kun5 ah, lun7-kau3 lin2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh ti7 iuN5 kap iuN5 e5 tiong-kan, kang e5 mi5-iuN5 kap kang e5 soaN-iuN5 e5 tiong-kan, kiaN5 phoaN3-toan3.  18). Li2 ti7 ho2-ho2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 chiah8-chhau2, iau2 liah8-choe3 sio2-khoa2 su7 mah? chhun e5 chhau2 lin2 keng2-jian5 eng7 kha thun2-tah8--i? lin2 lim chheng e5 chui2; chhun--e5 lin2 keng2-jian5 eng7 kha phah-lo5--i?  19). Lun7-kau3 Goa2 e5 iuN5 si7 chiah8 lin2 eng7 kha tah8--e5, lim lin2 eng7 kha phah-lo5--e5.
	20). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 in an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 pun2-sin ti7 pui5 e5 iuN5 kap san2 e5 iuN5 e5 tiong-kan, kiaN5 phoaN3-toan3.  21). In-ui7 lin2 eng7 sin-khu, eng7 keng-thau5 khoeh--in, eng7 lin2 e5 kak tak phoa3-piN7--e5, ti3-kau3 hou7 in si3-soaN3 ti7 goa7-bin7.  22). Sou2-i2 Goa2 beh chin2-kiu3 Goa2 e5 iuN5-kun5, bo5 koh choe3 siu7 chhiuN2 e5 mih8; Goa2 iah8 beh ti7 iuN5 kap iuN5 e5 tiong-kan kiaN5 phoaN3-toan3.  23). Goa2 beh siat-lip8 chit8 e5 bok8-chia2, chiau3-kou3 in, i beh iuN2-chhi7 in; chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8; i beh iuN2-chhi7 in, choe3 in e5 bok8-chia2.  24). Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3; Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 beh ti7 in e5 tiong-kan choe3 siu2-leng2; che si7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  25). Goa2 beh kap in lip8 peng5-an e5 iok, hou7 ok-siu3 tui3 keng2-lai7 toan7-choat8; in chiu7 beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2 ti7 khong3-ia2, khun3 ti7 chhiu7-na5-lai7.  26). Goa2 beh hou7 in kap Goa2 e5 soaN si3-ui5 e5 sou2-chai7 chiaN5-choe3 hok-khi3 e5 goan5-thau5; Goa2 iah8 beh chiau3-si5 loh8-hou7, beh u7 si hok-khi3 e5 toa7-hou7.  27). Chhan5-ia2 e5 chhiu7 beh kiat ke2-chi2; toe7 ia7 beh chhut-san2; in beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7; Goa2 at-chih8 in sou2 pe7 e5 taN, kiu3 in thoat-li7 hit e5 liah8 in choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2; hit-si5 in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  28). In bo5 koh choe3 goa7-pang lang5 sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, toe7-chiuN7 e5 ia2-siu3 ia7 bo5 koh thun-chiah8 in; si7 beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2, bo5 lang5 hou7 in kiaN-hiaN5.  29). Goa2 beh ka7 in heng-khi2 chit8 e5 chhut-mia5 chai-cheng3 e5 sou2-chai7; in ti7 keng2-lai7, bo5 koh hou7 ki-hng sou2 biat8; ia7 bo5 koh siu7-tioh8 goa7-pang-lang5 e5 leng5-jiok8.  30). In beh chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3, si7 kap in ti7-teh; ia7 chai in I2-sek-liat8-ke si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  31). Lin2 si7 Goa2 e5 iuN5, si7 Goa2 chhau2-tiuN5 e5 iuN5; lin2 si7 lang5; Goa2 ia7 si7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[35]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 bin7 ng3 Se-jiN2 soaN, soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek i.  3). Tui3 i kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Se-jiN2 soaN ah, Goa2 kap li2 choe3 tui3-tek8, Goa2 beh chhun-chhiu2 kong-kek li2; hou7 li2 leng2-cheng7, thang hou7 lang5 gong5-ngiah8.  4). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 chiah e5 siaN5 piN3-choe3 pha-hng, hou7 li2 leng2-cheng7; li2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  5). In-ui7 li2 khng3 eng2-oan2 e5 oan3-hun7; ti7 I2-sek-liat8 chok8 tu2-tioh8 chai-e7, choe7-koa3 kiat-kiok8 e5 si5, li2 chiong in kau hou7 to-kiam3 e5 se3-lek8.  6). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 chi2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7, Goa2 tek-khak hou7 li2 tu2-tioh8 lau5-huih e5 po3-eng3; choe7 tek-khak tui-koaN2 li2; li2 i2-keng bo5 oan3-hun7 thai5 lang5 lau5 huih, sou2-i2 chit e5 choe7 tek-khak tui-jip li2.  7). Goa2 beh hou7 Se-jiN2-soaN pha-hng leng2-cheng7; tui3-hia ong2-lai5 e5 lang5 Goa2 beh chian2-tu5 i.  8). Goa2 beh hou7 i hiah e5 soaN, siu7 thai5 e5 lang5 moa2-moa2; hou7 to-kiam3 thai5-si2--e5 beh to2 ti7 li2 e5 sio2-soaN, kap soaN-kok, kap it-chhe3 e5 khiN-kau.  9). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 eng2-oan2 pha-hng, li2 chiah e5 siaN5 tek-khak bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2; chiu7 lin2 tek-khak chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  10). In-ui7 lin2 kong2, Chi2 nng7-kok nng7 e5 toe7-hng, long2 beh kui goa2, goan2 beh tit-tioh8; ki5-sit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7-hia.  11). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 chiu3-choa7; Goa2 beh chiau3 li2 e5 siu7-khi3, kap chiau3 li2 ui7-tioh8 oan3-hun7 lai5 kiaN5 ti7 in e5 oan3-tou3, khoan2-thai7 li2; chiu7 Goa2 sim2-phoaN3 li2 e5 si5 beh hian2-beng5 ka-ki7 ti7 in tiong-kan.  12). Li2 chiu7 chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 li2 kong-kek I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN sou2 kong2 e5 pong3-tok8, si7 kong2, Pha-hng lah, in i2-keng kau ti7 goan2, hou7 goan2 thang thun i.  13). Koh lin2 eng7 chhui3 ng3 Goa2 lai5 ka-ki7 khoa-khau2; ke-thiN lin2 chiah e5 oe7 lai5 kong-kek Goa2; Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 lah.  14). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tng choan5-toe7 hoaN-hi2 e5 si5, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 pha-hng.  15). Li2 in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8-ke e5 ki-giap8 pha-hng, lai5 hoaN-hi2; Goa2 ia7 beh an2-ni khoan2-thai7 li2; Se-jiN2 soaN ah, li2 beh pha-hng, i2-kip8 I2-tong choan5-toe7 ia7 an2-ni; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[36]	Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN lai5 soan-thoan5, kong2, I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  2). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 tui3-tek8 kong-kek li2 kong2, Hou7--chai7, kou2-cha2 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 long2 hou7 goan2 choe3-giap8 lah.  3). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 in hou7 li2 pha-hng, ti7 si3-ui5 thun-ka7 li2; beh hou7 li2 kui ti7 sou2 chhun e5 goa7-pang-lang5 choe3 giap8; ia7 hou7 kau7-khau2-siat8 e5 lang5 gi7-lun7 li2, hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 hui2-pong3 li2;  4). sou2-i2 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN ah, tioh8 thiaN Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7: Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 chiah e5 soaN, chiah e5 nia2, chiah e5 khiN-kau, chiah e5 soaN-kok, chiah e5 pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7, siu7 khi3-sak e5 siaN5, hou7 si3-ui5 sou2 chhun e5 goa7-pang-lang5 chhiuN2-kiap ki-chhi3--e5, an2-ni kong2;  5). sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 sit8-chai7 ti7 jiat8-jiat8 e5 oan3-tou3, eng7 oe7 chek-pi7 liat8-pang sou2 chhun--e5 i2-kip8 I2-tong e5 choan5-toe7; in-ui7 in hun-phai3 Goa2 e5 toe7 choe3 ka-ki7 e5 giap8; moa2-sim hoaN-hi2, sin5-hun5 biau2-si7; ai3 koaN2-tiok8 i e5 peh-siN3, lai5 chhiuN2-kiap--i.  6). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 lun7 I2-sek-liat8 toe7 lai5 soan-thoan5; tui3 i chiah e5 soaN, chiah e5 nia2, chiah e5 khiN-kau, chiah e5 soaN-kok kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 ti7 goa2 e5 oan3-tou3, kap Goa2 e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 lai5 kong2, in-ui7 li2 i2-keng siu7 iN7-pang lang5 e5 leng5-jiok8;  7). sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ku2-khi2 Goa2 e5 chhiu2, kong2, Ti7 lin2 si3-ui5 e5 iN7-pang lang5, in sit8-chai7 beh siu7 in e5 leng5-jiok8.  8). Tok8-tok8 lin2 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 soaN ah, lin2 tek-khak hoat-chhut lin2 e5 ki-oaiN7, koh beh kiat ke2-chi2 hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8; in-ui7 in kun7-kun7 beh kau3 lah.  9). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 si7 ui7 lin2 e5, goa2 beh oat8-tng2 ng3 lin2, chiu7 lin2 beh hou7 lang5 cheng3-choh.  10). Goa2 koh beh ke-thiN lang5 ti7 lin2 e5 teng2-bin7, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 ke-ke hou7-hou7, it-chhe3 long2 an2-ni; chiu7 i chiah e5 siaN5 beh u7 lang5 khia7-khi2; pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 tit-tioh8 khi2-cho7.  11). Goa2 ia7 beh ke-thiN lang5 kap cheng-siN ti7 lin2 e5 teng2-bin7; in beh siN-thoaN3 chin-choe7; Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 chiau3-ku7 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2; koh beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 lin2, iaN5-ke3 khi2-thau5 e5 si5; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  12). Goa2 beh hou7 lang5 kiaN5 ti7 lin2 e5 teng2-bin7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8; in beh tit-tioh8 li2, li2 beh choe3 in e5 giap8; li2 ia7 bo5 koh hou7 in choat8-su5.  13). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, In-ui7 lang5 tui3 lin2 kong2, Li2 si7 thun-chiah8 lang5--e5, koh hou7 peh-siN3 choat8-su5;  14). sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 bo5 beh koh thun-chiah8 lang5, iah8 bo5 beh koh hou7 li2 e5 kok-bin5 choat8-su5.  15). Goa2 bo5 beh hou7 li2 koh thiaN-kiN3 goa7-pang lang5 e5 leng5-jiok8, li2 ia7 bo5 koh siu7 ban7 peh-siN3 e5 hui2-pong3, li2 ia7 bo5 koh hou7 li2 e5 kok-bin5 tioh8-tak; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  17). Jin5-chu2 ah, I2-sek-liat8-ke, khia7-khi2 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7 e5 si5, eng7 in e5 sou2-kiaN5 sou2-choe3, phah la5-sam5--i; in e5 sou2-kiaN5 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 keng-ki5 kau3 e5 la5-sam5.  18). In-ui7 in ti7 hit e5 sou2-chai7 lau5 lang5 e5 huih, koh in-ui7 in eng7 ngou2-siong7 phah la5-sam5--i; sou2-i2 Goa2 piaN3-chhut Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7.  19). Goa2 hun-soaN3 in ti7 liat8-kok, in chiu7 si3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-pang-tiong; Goa2 chiu7 chiau3 in e5 sou2-kiaN5, in e5 sou2-choe3 lai5 sim2-phoaN3--in.  20). In khi3 kau3 in sou2 kau3 e5 goa7-pang lang5 hia, siat-tok8 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5; in-ui7 lang5 chi2 in lai5 kong2, Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 peh-siN3, tui3 I e5 toe7 chhut-lai5--e5.  21). Chong2-si7 Goa2 po2-sioh Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5; chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8-ke, ti7 in sou2 kau3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong, sou2 siat-tok8--e5.  22). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, Goa2 kiaN5 chit-e5, m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 ian5-kou3, chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5 e5 ian5-kou3; chiu7-si7 lin2 kiaN5-kau3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong sou2 siat-tok8--e5.  23). Goa2 e5 toa7-mia5 siu7 siat-tok8 ti7 iN7-pang-tiong, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 siat-tok8 ti7 in tiong-kan--e5; Goa2 beh hou7 i choe3-seng3; koh Goa2 tui3 lin2 hian2-beng5 ka-ki7 choe3-seng3 ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5; chiu7 iN7-pang-lang5 beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5.  24). Goa2 beh toa3 lin2 chhut liat8-pang, tui3 liat8-kok-tiong chu7-chip8 lin2, chhoa7 lin2 jip8 lin2 e5 pun2 sou2-chai7.  25). Goa2 ia7 beh eng7 chheng e5 chui2 hiu3 lin2, lin2 chiu7 chheng-khi3; Goa2 beh soe2-chheng lin2, tu5-khi3 lin2 it-chhe3 e5 la5-sam5, kap lin2 it-chhe3 e5 ngou2-siong7.  26). Goa2 beh eng7 sin e5 sim siuN2-su3 lin2; ia7 beh eng7 sin e5 sin5 he7 ti7 lin2 e5 lai7-bin7; koh beh tui3 lin2 e5 jiok8-the2-tiong tu5-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 chioh8 e5 sim, siuN2-su3 lin2 chhin-chhiuN7 bah e5 sim.  27).
