Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 sin5 he7 ti7 lin2 e5 lai7-bin7, hou7 lin2 sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, siu2 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5--i.  28). Lin2 beh khia7-khi2 ti7 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7; lin2 beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh choe3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  29). Goa2 beh kiu3 lin2 thoat-li7 lin2 it-chhe3 e5 u3-oe3; ia7 beh kio3 ngou2-kok hou7 i hong-seng7, bo5 hou7 lin2 tu2-tioh8 ki-hng.  30). Goa2 beh ke-thiN chhiu7-bak8 e5 ke2-chi2, i2-kip8 chhan5-hng5 e5 thou2-san2; hou7 lin2 bo5 koh in-ui7 ki-hng siu7 goa7-pang-lang5 e5 leng5-jiok8.  31). Hit-si5 lin2 beh ki3-tit lin2 e5 phaiN2 sou2-kiaN5, kap lin2 m7-ho2 e5 sou2-choe3; chiu7 in-ui7 lin2 e5 choe7-koa3, kap kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, ti7 ka-ki7 e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 iam3-chian7 ka-ki7.  32). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chai Goa2 an2-ni kiaN5 m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 ian5-kou3; I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 tioh8 ui7 ka-ki7 e5 sou2-kiaN5, lai5 lau3-khui3 kian3-siau3.  33). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 soe2-chheng lin2, tu5-khi3 lin2 it-chhe3 choe7-koa3 e5 jit8, beh hou7 lin2 e5 siaN5 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2, pha-hng e5 sou2-chai7 tit-tioh8 khi2-cho7.  34). Cheng5 ke3-lou7 e5 lang5 khoaN3-choe3 hong-hoe3 e5 toe7, taN chit e5 hong-hoe3 e5 toe7 koh u7 lang5 cheng3-choh.  35). Lang5 beh kong2, Cheng5 choe3 hong-hoe3 e5 toe7, taN chhin-chhiuN7 Ai-tian5 e5 hng5; chit e5 hong-hoe3, leng2-cheng7, hui2-hoai7 e5 siaN5, taN khi2 chin kian-kou3, u7 lang5 khia7-khi2.  36). Hit-si5 ti7 lin2 si3-ui5 sou2 chhun e5 goa7-pang-lang5, beh chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2-cho7 hiah e5 to2-hoai7 e5 sou2-chai7, chai-poe5 hong-hoe3 e5 toe7; Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng kong2--i, tek-khak chiaN5--i.
	37). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 I2-sek-liat8-ke ui7-tioh8 chit e5 su7 kiu5 Goa2, ti3-kau3 Goa2 ka7 in chiaN5; Goa2 beh ke-thiN in e5 lang5-giah8, chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5-kun5.  38). Chhin-chhiuN7 hian3-che3 e5 iuN5-kun5, chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siu2-choeh e5 si5 e5 iuN5-kun5; an2-ni, chiah e5 pha-hng e5 siaN5, tek-khak u7 kui-kun5 lang5 moa2-moa2; in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[37]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7, Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 I e5 sin5 chhoa7 goa2 chhut-khi3, he7 goa2 ti7 soaN-kok-tiong; hit e5 soaN-kok u7 kut-thau5 moa2-moa2.  2). I hou7 goa2 tui3 kut-thau5 e5 si3-ui5 keng-ke3; khoaN3 ah, ti7 soaN-kok e5 bin7-chiuN7 u7 kut-thau5 chin-choe7, khoaN3 ah, in chin kou-ta5.  3). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, chiah e5 kut oe7 oah8 boe7? Goa2 in3 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 chai--i.  4). I koh tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 chiah e5 kut soan-thoan5, lai5 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 kou-ta5 e5 kut ah, tioh8 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7.  5). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 chiah e5 kut an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh hou7 oah8-khi3 jip8 lin2 e5 lai7-bin7, lin2 chiu7 beh oah8.  6). Goa2 beh hou7 lin2 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 kun, koh hou7 lin2 u7 bah, koh eng7 phe5 ka7 lin2 pau, eng7 oah8-khi3 jip8 ti7 lin2, lin2 chiu7 oe7 oah8; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  7). Tui3 an2-ni, goa2 than3 beng7-leng7 lai5 soan-thoan5; tng goa2 teh soan-thoan5 e5 si5, u7 siaN, hut-jian5 toe7-tang7, chiah e5 kut saN lian5-hap8, tak8-ki kui i e5 pun2-ui7.  8). Goa2 khoaN3 i, khoaN3-kiN3 kut e5 teng2-bin7 u7 kun, ia7 u7 bah, koh u7 phe5 pau ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7; chong2-si7 lai7-bin7 bo5 oah8-khi3.  9). I chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 ng3 hong lai5 soan-thoan5; jin5-chu2 ah, tioh8 soan-thoan5, lai5 tui3 hong kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Oah8-khi3 ah, tui3 hiah e5 hong lai5, pun5 ti7 chiah e5 siu7-thai5--e5, hou7 in oe7 oah8.  10). Tui3 an2-ni, goa2 chiau3 I sou2 beng7-leng7 goa2--e5 lai5 soan-thoan5; oah8-khi3 chiu7 lai5, jip8 ti7 in; in chiu7 oah8, khi2--lai5 khia7, chiaN5-choe3 kek8-toa7 e5 kun-tui7.  11). I chiu7 ka7 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, chiah e5 kut chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 choan5-ke; khoaN3 ah, in kong2, Goan2 e5 kut long2 kou-ta5, goan2 e5 ng3-bang7 long2 sit-loh8; goan2 it-chin7 chau5-biat8.  12). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 soan-thoan5, lai5 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh khui lin2 e5 bong7, hou7 lin2 tui3 lin2 e5 bong7 khi2--lai5, chhoa7 lin2 jip8 I2-sek-liat8 toe7.  13). Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 ah, Goa2 khui lin2 e5 bong7, hou7 lin2 tui3 lin2 e5 bong7 khi2--lai5, lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  14). Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 sin5 he7 ti7 lin2 e5 lai7-bin7, lin2 chiu7 beh oah8; Goa2 an-ti3 lin2 ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7, lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, ia7 an2-ni chiaN5; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	15). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 koh lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  6). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 theh8 chit8-te3 chha5-pan2, ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7 sia2, Ui7 Iu5-tai7 kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 I2-sek-liat8 chok8; koh theh8 chit8 te3 chha5-pan2, ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7 sia2, Ui7-tioh8 Iok-sek, I2-hoat-lian5, kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke e5 chha5-pan2.  17). Li2 tioh8 hou7 in saN-oa2, lian5 choe3 chit8-te3 chha5-pan2; chiu7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2-tiong beh chiaN5-choe3 chit8-te3.  18). Siat-su2 li2 e5 peh-siN3 mng7 li2 kong2, Li2 choe3 chit-e5 sim2-mih8 i3-su3, li2 m7 chi2-si7 goan2 mah?  19). li2 chiu7 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh theh8 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 kiah8 Iok-sek e5 chha5-pan2, kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 chi-phai3; Goa2 beh he7--i oa2 ti7 Iu5-tai7 e5 chha5-pan2, hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 chit8-te3 e5 chha5-pan2, chiu7 i beh chiaN5-choe3 chit8-te3 ti7 Goa2 e5 chhiu2.  20). Li2 sou2 sia2 hi2 nng7 te3 chha5-pan2, tioh8 ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, kiah8 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2.  21). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 beh chhu2 I2-sek-liat8 chok8 tui3 in sou2 kau3 e5 tak8-kok chhut--lai5; koh tui3 si3-ui5 chu7-chip8 in, chhoa7 in to3-lai5 pun2 sou2-chai7.  22). Goa2 beh hou7 in ti7 hit e5 toe7, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 soaN, hap8-choe3 chit8 peh-siN3; u7 chit8 e5 ong5 choe3 in cheng3-lang5 e5 ong5; in bo5 koh choe3 nng7-peng5 e5 peh-siN3, ia7 bo5 koh pun-choe3 nng7-kok.  23). Ia7 bo5 koh in-ui7 ngou2-siong7, kap kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-koa3, phah la5-sam5 pun2-sin; Goa2 beh kiu3 in chhut in it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 in hoan7-choe7 hia; Goa2 beh chheng-khi3 in; an2-ni, in beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3; Goa2 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3.  24). Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 beh choe3 in e5 ong5; in long2 beh kui ti7 chit8 e5 bok8-chia2; in beh sun7-than3 Goa2 e5 hoat-tou7, siu2 Goa2 e5 lut8-le7 lai5 kiaN5.  25). In beh khia7-khi2 ti7 Goa2 siuN2-su3 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok e5 toe7; chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 khia7-khi2--e5; in kap in e5 kiaN2-sun, i2-kip8 kiaN2-kiaN2 sun-sun, long2 eng2-oan2 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia. Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Tai7-pit8 beh choe3 in e5 jin5-kun, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.  26). Koh Goa2 beh kap in lip8 peng5-an e5 iok, kap in choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 iok; Goa2 ia7 beh kian3-siat in, hou7 in e5 lang5-giah8 ke-thiN, koh ti7 in e5 tiong-kan siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.  27). Goa2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 beh ti7 in tiong-kan; Goa2 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3, in beh choe3 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3.  28). Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 ti7 in tiong-kan, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2; goa7-pang-lang5 chiu7 beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 chiaN5-choe3 seng3-e5.

[38]	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lim5-kau3 goa2 kong2,  2). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 bin7 ng3 Ma2-kok toe7 e5 Ko-kek, chiu7-si7 Lo5-si, Bi2-siat, Thou2-pa e5 jin5-kun, soan-thoan5 lai5 kong-kek i, kong2,  3). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lo5-si, Bi2-siat, Thou2-pa e5 jin5-kun, Ko-kek ah, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 choe3 li2 e5 tui3-tek8;  4). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 oat8-tng2, eng7 kau kau li2 e5 ge5-cho5, chiong li2 kap li2 e5 kun-peng, be2-phit, be2-peng, toa3--chhut-lai5, long2 chheng7 chin sui2 e5 chian3-kah, chiaN5-choe3 toa7 e5 kun-tui7, gia5 toa7-sio2 e5 tin5-pai5, tak8-e5 kiah8 to-kiam3;  5).Pho-su-lang5, Kou2-sit8-lang5 kap Hut-lang5 kap in lai5, tak8-e5 gia5 tin5-pai5 ti3 thau5-khoe;  6). Ko-biat8 kap i e5 kun-tui7; pak-hng kek8-thau5 e5 To5-ka-ma2-chok8 kap i e5 kun-tui7; koh u7 choe7-choe7 peh-siN3 kap li2 choe3-tin7.  7). Li2 tioh8 ka-ki7 pi7-pan7, li2 kap chu7-chip8 ti7 li2 hia e5 kun-tui7 long2 tioh8 pi7-pan7, li2 tioh8 choe3 in e5 goan5-soe3.  8). Choe7-choe7 jit8 au7 li2 beh siu7 pan7-li2; kau3 lou7-be2 e5 ni5 li2 beh lai5 kau3 thoat-li7 to-kiam3, tui3 liat8-kok siu-hoe5 e5 toe7, kau3 I2-sek-liat8 ku2-ku2 pha-hng e5 soaN; chong2-si7 i i2-keng tui3 liat8-kok-tiong toa3-chhut, in long2 beh an-jian5 khia7-khi2.  9). Li2 kap li2 e5 kun-tui7, i2-kip8 kap li2 saN-kap lai5 choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3, long2 beh chiuN7-lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 kong5-hong lai5, li2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 hun5 jia-kham3 toe7.  10). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Kau3 hit-jit8 beh u7 i3-su3 heng-khi2 ti7 li2 e5 sim, li2 beh tou5-bou5 phaiN2 e5 ke3-bou5;  11). kong2, Goa2 beh chiuN7-kau3 hiuN-sia7 e5 toe7, kau3 cheng7-cheng7 an-jian5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 hia, in sou2 khia7-khi2-e5 long2 bo5 siaN5-chhiuN5, ia7 bo5 mng5 bo5 chhoaN3; 12). thang chhiuN2 sou2 beh chhiuN2--e5, kiap sou2 beh kiap--e5, oat8-tng2 li2 e5 chhiu2, kong-kek hiah e5 cheng5 pha-hng taN u7 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7, i2-kip8 hit e5 khia7-khi2 se3-kai3 e5 tiong-sim-tiam2, tui3 liat8-kok chu7-chip8, tit-tioh8 cheng-siN he3-chai5 e5 peh-siN3.  13). Si7-pa lang5, Ti2-tan3 lang5, Tha-si e5 seng-li2 lang5, kap in tiong-kan iong2 e5 sai, long2 beh tui3 li2 kong2, Li2 lai5 si7 beh chhiuN2 sou2-chhiuN2--e5 mah? li2 chu7-chip8 li2 e5 kun-tui7 si7 beh kiap sou2 kiap--e5 mah? beh theh8 kim-gun5, toa3 cheng-siN he3-chai5 khi3 mah? Beh toa7-toa7 chhiuN2 sou2 chhiuN2-e5 mah?
	14). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 in-ui7 an2-ni soan-thoan5, tui3 Ko-kek kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Tng Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 an-jian5 khia7-khi2 e5 jit8, li2 kiam2 bo5 tit-tioh8 chai mah?  15). Li2 beh tui3 li2 e5 pun2 sou2-chai7, tui3 pak-hng e5 kek8-thau5 lai5, li2 kap choe7-choe7 kok e5 peh-siN3 saN-kap lai5, long2 si7 khia5-be2, choe3 toa7-tin7, choe7-choe7 e5 kun-tui7.  16). Li2 beh chiuN7-lai5 kong-kek Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8, chhin-chhiuN7 bat8-hun5 jia-kham3 toe7; ti7 lou7-be2 e5 jit8 Goa2 beh chhoa7 li2 lai5 kong-kek Goa2 e5 toe7, Ko-kek ah, kau3 Goa2 ti7 liat8-pang e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 li2 e5 sin-chiuN7 hian2-beng5 choe3-seng3 e5 si5, thang hou7 in bat Goa2.  17). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ti7 cha2-si5, eng7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, I2-sek-liat8 e5 sian-ti, sou2 kong2--e5, chiu7-si7 li2 mah? tng hiah e5 jit8 in lek8-ni5 chham3-gu2 Goa2 beh chhoa7 li2 lai5 kong-kek in.  18). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Ko-kek chiuN7--lai5 kong-kek I2-sek-liat8 toe7 e5 jit8, Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3 beh tui3 Goa2 e5 phiN7-khang chhut.  19). In-ui7 Goa2 oan3-tou3 kap toa7 siu7-khi3 chhin-chhiuN7 he2, chiu7 kong2, Hit-jit8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 toe7 tek-khak u7 toa7 tin2-tang7;  20). sim7-chi3 hai2-tiong e5 hi5, khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, chhan5-ia2 e5 siu3, i2-kip8 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 teh so5 e5 thang5-thoa7, kap toe7-bin7-chiuN7 e5 cheng3-lang5, ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 long2 beh tin2-tang7, soaN-nia2 beh pang-lih8, soaN-kham3 beh to2-hoai7, chhiuN5-piah long2 beh to2--loh8-khi3.  21). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh beng7-leng7 Goa2 chiah e5 soaN hoat-chhut to-kiam3 lai5 kong-kek Ko-kek; tak8-lang5 beh eng7 i e5 to-kiam3 thai5 i e5 hiaN-ti7.  22). Goa2 beh eng7 un-ek8 kap lau5-huih lai5 pan7 i; Goa2 ia7 beh eng7 toa7-hou7, toa7-phauh8, kap he2, kap jiu5-ng5, kang3-loh8 hou7 i kap i e5 kun-tui7, i2-kip8 kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3.  23). Goa2 beh hian2-beng5 ka-ki7 choe3 toa7, hian2-beng5 ka-ki7 choe3-seng3, ia7 beh hian2-hian7 ti7 choe7-choe7 kok lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5; in chiu7 chai Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

[39]	Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 ng3 Ko-kek lai5 soan-thoan5 kong-kek i kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Lo5-si, Bi2-siat, Thou2-pa e5 jin5-kun, Ko-kek ah, Goa2 kap li2 choe3 tui3-tek8;  2). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 oat8-tng2, beh chhoa7 li2 chin3-cheng5, hou7 li2 tui3 pak-hng e5 kek8-thau5 lai5, toa3 li2 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 soaN;  3). Goa2 beh tui3 li2 e5 to3-chhiu2 phah ka-lauh8 li2 e5 keng, tui3 li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 phah-lak li2 e5 chiN3.  4). Li2 kap li2 e5 kun-tui7 i2-kip8 kap li2 lai5 e5 liat8-kok lang5 beh to2 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 soaN; Goa2 beh chiong li2 hou7 tak8-iuN7 e5 eng-chiau2 kap chhan5-ia2 e5 ia2-siu3 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  5). Li2 beh to2 ti7 chhan5-ia2; in-ui7 Goa2 bat kong2--i; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  6). Goa2 ia7 beh kang3-loh8 he2 ti7 Ma2-kok kap hai2-su7 an-jian5 khia7-khi2 e5 lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7; in chiu7 chai Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  7). Goa2 beh ti7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 tiong hian2-chhut Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5, ia7 bo5 iong5-un2 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5 koh siu7 siat-tok8; liat8-kok lang5 chiu7 chai Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 tiong e5 Seng3--e5.  8). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, tai7-chi3 lai5--lah ia7 beh chiaN5 i; che si7 Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5 jit8.  9). Khia7-khi2 I2-sek-liat8 siaN5 e5 lang5 beh chhut--khi3, khi2-he2 sio i e5 ke-si, chiu7-si7 toa7-soe3 e5 tin5-pai5, keng-chiN3, thui5-a2 kap chhiuN, long2 beh eng7 in lai5 hiaN5-he2 lek8-ke3 chhit-ni5 ku2;  10). sim7-chi3 in bo5 beh tui3 chhan5-ia2 khioh-chha5, ia7 bo5 beh tui3 chhiu7-na5 chho3-chhiu7; in-ui7 in beh eng7 ke-si hiaN5-he2; koh beh chhiuN2 hiah e5 chhiuN2 in e5 lang5, kiap hiah e5 kiap in e5 lang5; che chiu7-si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.
	11). Tng hit-jit8 goa2 beh chiong I2-sek-liat8 toe7, hai2 e5 tang--si3, lang5 sou2 keng-ke3 e5 soaN-kok, siuN2-su3 Ko-kek choe3 thiong2-toe7 chou2-tong3 keng-ke3 e5 lang5 e5 lou7; ti7-hia lang5 beh bai5-chong3 Ko-kek kap i e5 cheng3-lang5; beh chheng hit sou2-chai7 choe3 Hap-bun5-ko-kek e5 soaN-kok.  12). I2-sek-liat8-ke beh bai5-chong3 in lek8-ke3 chhit-geh8 jit8 e5 ku2, hou7 hit e5 toe7 chheng-khi3.  13). Thong-kok e5 peh-siN3 beh bai5-chong3 in; tng Goa2 tit-tioh8 eng5-kng e5 jit8, chit e5 su7 beh hou7 in tit-tioh8 mia5-siaN; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  14). In beh phai3 lang5 siong5-siong5 sun5-cha pian3-toe7; kap keng-ke3 e5 lang5 saN-kap chong3 hiah e5 chhun ti7 toe7--nih e5 sin-si, thang chheng-khi3 hit e5 toe7-hng; kau3 chhit-geh8 jit8 moa2, in beh koh si3-koe3 chhe7.  15). Sun5-cha pian3 toe7 e5 lang5 beh keng-ke3; na7 u7 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 lang5 e5 kut-hai5, chiu7 ti7-hia lip8 chit8 e5 ki3-ho7, theng3-hau7 bai5-chong3 e5 lang5 bai5-chong3 i ti7 Hap-bun5-ko-kek e5 soaN-kok.  16). Ia7 beh u7 chit8 e5 siaN5, mia5 kio3 Hap-bun5-na2.  In beh an2-ni chheng-khi3 hit e5 toe7.
	17). Jin5-chu2 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 tak8-iuN7 e5 pe-chiau2 i2-kip8 chhan5-ia2 e5 ia2-siu3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 choe3-tin7 lai5; tioh8 tui3 si3-hng chu7-chip8 kau3 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 sou2 hian3 e5 che3, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 soaN e5 toa7-che3, hou7 lin2 thang chiah8-bah lim-huih.  18). Lin2 beh chiah8 iong2-su7 e5 bah, lim toe7-chiuN7 siu2-leng2 e5 huih, kang e5 mi5-iuN5, iuN5-a2, kang e5 soaN-iuN5, kang e5 gu5, long2 si7 Pa-san pui5 e5 cheng-siN.  19). Lin2 chiah8 Goa2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 sou2 hian3 e5 che3, beh chiah8 iu5 kau3 pa2, lim-huih kau3 chui3.  20). Lin2 beh ti7 Goa2 e5 toh chiah8 be2-phit kap che7-chhia-e5, kap iong2-su7 kap it-chhe3 e5 chian3-su7 kau3 pa2-pa2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  21). Goa2 beh hian2-beng5 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng ti7 liat8-kok-tiong, liat8-kok ia7 beh khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 sim2-phoaN3, kap Goa2 sou2 he7 ti7 in sin-chiuN7 e5 chhiu2.  22). An2-ni tui3 hit-jit8 i2-au7 I2-sek-liat8-ke beh chai Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa in e5 Siong7-te3.  23). Liat8-kok ia7 beh chai I2-sek-liat8-ke siu7-liah8 si7 in-ui7 in e5 choe7-koa3; in tek-choe7 Goa2, Goa2 tui3 in ng Goa2 e5 bin7; chiong in kau ti7 in e5 tui3-tek8 e5 chhiu2; in chiu7 long2 to2 ti7 to-e7.  24). Goa2 chiau3 in e5 u3-oe3 chiau3 in e5 ke3-sit khoan2-thai7 in; tui3 in ng Goa2 e5 bin7.
	25). Sou2-i2 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 Nga2-kok siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3--lai5; ia7 beh lin5-bin2 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke;  26). ia7 beh ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5 jiat8-sim.  27). In ti7 pun2 sou2-chai7 an-jian5 khia7-khi2, bo5 lang5 hou7 in kiaN, ti7 Goa2 chiong in tui3 liat8-kok-tiong chhoa7 to3--lai5, tui3 tui3-tek8 e5 toe7 chu7-chip8 lai5, Goa2 ti7 liat8-kok e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 in sin-chiuN7 hian2-beng5 choe3-seng3 e5 si5, in beh tam-tng in e5 kian3-siau3 kap in kan-hoan7 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 choe7.  28). Goa2 hou7 in siu7-liah8 ti7 liat8-pang, koh chu7-chip8 in to3--lai5 pun2 sou2-chai7, bo5 lau5 chit8-lang5 ti7-hia, in chiu7 chai Goa2 si7 in e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  29). Goa2 ia7 bo5 koh tui3 in ng Goa2 e5 bin7; in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng chiong Goa2 e5 sin5 kang3-loh8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8-ke; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[40]	Goan2 siu7-liah8 e5 ji7-chap8-gou7 ni5, ti7 ni5-thau5, geh8 e5 chhoe-chap8 jit8 siaN5 phoa3 liau2-au7 te7 chap8-si3 ni5, tu2-tu2 hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7, chhoa7 goa2 kau3 hia.  2). Ti7 Siong7-te3 iN7-siong7-tiong toa3 goa2 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 toe7, an-ti3 goa2 ti7 chin-koaiN5 e5 soaN, soaN-teng2 e5 lam5-peng5 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 khi2-cho7 e5 siaN5.  3). I chhoa7 goa2 kau3 hia; khoaN3 ah, u7 chit8-lang5, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 tang5 e5 khoan2-sit, chhiu2 theh8 moa5-soh, kap chhek-liong5 e5 ko-chhioh, khia7 ti7 mng5-khau2.  4). Hit e5 lang5 tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, kiN3 goa2 sou2 hou7 li2 khoaN3--e5, li2 tioh8 eng7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3, eng7 li2 e5 hi7-khang thiaN, ia7 tioh8 eng7 li2 e5 sim ki3-tiau5; in-ui7 li2 siu7 toa3 lai5 chia tiau5-ti5 ui7-tioh8 beh hou7 li2 khoaN3 chiah e5 su7; kiN3 li2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3--e5, li2 long2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8-ke kong2.
	5). KhoaN3 ah, chhu3 e5 goa7-bin7 si3-ui5 u7 chhiuN5, hit lang5 e5 chhiu2 theh8 chhek-liong5 e5 ko-chhioh, tng5 lak8 tiu2, mui2-tiu2 si7 chit8-tiu2 koh chit8 pa-chiuN2; i chiu7 niu5 chhiuN5 kau7 chit8 ko-chhioh, koaiN5 chit8 ko-chhioh.  6). I chiu7 kau3 ng3 tang e5 mng5, chiuN7 i e5 kia7-a2; niu5 mng5 e5 hou7-teng7, khoah chit8 ko-chhioh; koh chit8 e5 hou7-teng7, khoah ia7 chit8 ko-chhioh.  7). Koh si7-oe7-pang5, tak8-keng tng5 chit8 ko-chhioh, khoah chit8 ko-chhioh; saN-li7 gou7 tiu2; mng5 e5 hou7-teng7, chiu7-si7 oa2-kun7 ng3-chhu3 e5 mng5 e5 leng2-long5, khoah chit8 ko-chhioh.  8). I ia7 niu5 ng3 chhu3 e5 mng5 e5 leng2-long5, khoah chit8 ko-chhioh.  9). Koh niu5 mng5 e5 long5, khoah poeh-tiu2; i e5 thiau7 nng7 tiu2; hit e5 mng5 e5 leng2-long5 si7 ng3-chhu3.  10). Tang--si3 e5 mng5 u7 si7-oe7-pang5, chit-peng5 saN-keng, hit-peng5 saN-keng, long2 tang5-chit8-iuN7 e5 chhun3-chhioh; chit-peng5 e5 thiau7 kap hit peng5 e5 thiau7 ia7 si7 chit8-iuN7 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  11). I niu5 mng5-khau2, khoah chap8 tiu2, mng5 e5 tng5 chap8-saN tiu2.  12). Si7-oe7-pang5 thau5-cheng5 e5 kai3, chit-peng5 chit8-tiu2, hit-peng5 ia7 u7 kai3, chit8-tiu2; si7-oe7-pang5 chit-peng5 lak8-tiu2, hit-peng5 lak8-tiu2.  13). Koh niu5 mng5 tui3 chit e5 si7-oe7-pang5 e5 chhu3-teng2 kau3 hit e5 si7-oe7-pang5 e5 chhu3-teng2, khoah ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2; mng5 kap mng5 saN-tui3.  14). Koh choe3 hiah e5 thiau7 lak8-chap8 tiu2; u7 iN7 eng7 thiau7 choe3-kai3, ti7 mng5 e5 si3-ui5.  15). Tui3 jip8-mng5 e5 thau5-cheng5 kau3 lai7-bin7 mng5 e5 leng2-long5 e5 thau5-cheng5, kiong7 gou7-chap8 tiu2.  16). Chiah e5 si7-oe7-pang5 kap mng5-lai7 si3-ui5 e5 thiau7, i2-kip8 in e5 leng2-long5, long2 u7 koaiN-bat8 e5 thang; koh si3-ui5 u7 thang ng3 lai7-bin7; tak8 ki thiau7 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 chang-chhiu7.
	17). I chhoa7 goa2 jip8 goa7-iN7; khoaN3 ah, u7 pang5-keng, koh ti7 iN7 e5 si3-ui5 u7 phou-chioh8 e5 toe7; phou-chioh8 toe7 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 pang5 saN-chap8 keng.  18). Phou-chioh8 e5 toe7 si7 ti7 hiah e5 mng5 e5 sin-piN, kap hiah e5 mng5 piN5-tng5; che si7 e7-bin7 phou-chioh8 e5 toe7.  19). I tui3 e7-bin7 mng5 e5 thau5-cheng5 niu5 kau3 lai7-iN7 thau5-cheng5 e5 goa7-bin7, khoah chit8-pah tiu2; tang-bin7 pak-bin7 long2 si7 an2-ni.  20). Goa7-iN7 ng3 pak e5 mng5, i niu5 i e5 tng5 khoah.  21). I e5 si7-oe7-pang5 chit-peng5 saN-keng, hit-peng5 saN-keng; i e5 thiau7, i e5 leng2-long5, long2 chiau3 thau5 chit8 e5 mng5 e5 pan7; tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2.  22). I e5 thang i e5 leng2-long5 kap i e5 chang-chhiu7, long2 si7 chiau3 ng3-tang e5 mng5; lang5 tui3 chhit-chan3 e5 kia7-a2 chiuN7 kau3 hia; thau5-cheng5 u7 hiah e5 long5.  23). Lai7-iN7 u7 mng5 kap tang--si3 e5 mng5 pak--si3 e5 mng5 saN-tui3; i tui3 mng5 kau3 mng5 niu5--i, chit8-pah tiu2.  24). I chhoa7 goa2 ng3 lam5--si3 khi3; khoaN3 ah, u7 mng5 ng3-lam5; koh chiau3 cheng5 e5 chhun3-chhioh niu5 i e5 thiau7 kap i e5 leng2-long5.  25). I e5 lai7-bin7 kap i e5 leng2-long5 si3-ui5 long2 u7 thang, kap cheng5 sou2 niu5 e5 thang tang5 chit8-iuN7; tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2.  26). U7 chhit-chan3 kia7-a2 thang chiuN7 kau3 hia; thau5-cheng5 u7 hiah e5 leng2-long5; thiau7-teng2 u7 chang-chhiu7, chit-peng5 chit8-chang5, hit-peng5 chit8-chang5.  27). Lai7-iN7 u7 mng5 ng3-lam5; tui3 mng5 kau3 mng5 i ng3-lam5 niu5-i chit8-pah tiu2.
	28). I chhoa7 goa2 tui3 lam5-mng5 kau3 lai7-iN7; chiu7 chiau3 cheng5 e5 chhun3-chhioh niu5 lam5-mng5;  29). i e5 pang5, i e5 thiau7, i e5 leng2-long5, long2 chiau3 cheng5 e5 chhun3-chhioh; i e5 lai7-bin7 kap i leng2-long5 si3-ui5 long2 u7 thang; tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2.  30). Chiu-ui5 u7 leng2-long5, tng5 ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2, khoah gou7-tiu2.  31). I e5 long5 ng3 goa7-iN7, thiau7-teng2 u7 chang-chhiu7, chiuN7 poeh-chan3 kia7-a2 kau3 hia.  32). I chhoa7 goa2 kau3 lai7-iN7, ng3 tang; i niu5 hit e5 mng5, chiau3 cheng5 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  33). I e5 pang5, i e5 thiau7, i e5 leng2-long5, long2 chiau3 cheng5 e5 chhun3-chhioh; i e5 lai7-bin7, kap i leng2-long5 si3-ui5 long2 u7 thang, tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2.  34). I e5 long5 ng3 goa7-iN7, thiau7-teng2 ti7 chit-peng5 hit-peng5 u7 chang-chhiu7; chiuN7 poeh chan3 kia7-a2 kau3 hia.  35). I koh chhoa7 goa2 kau3 pak-mng5, niu5--i chiau3 cheng5 e5 chhun3-chhioh.  36). Koh niu5 i e5 pang5, i e5 thiau7, i e5 leng2-long5; lai7-bin7 si3-ui5 long2 u7 thang, i e5 tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8-gou7 tiu2.  37). I e5 thiau7 ng3 goa7-iN7, thiau7-teng2 ti7 chit-peng5 hit-peng5 u7 chang-chhiu7; chiuN7 poeh chan3 kia7-a2 kau3 hia.
	38). Mng5 e5 thiau7-piN u7 pang5, kap i e5 mng5; ti7-hia soe2 sio-che3 e5 seng-le2;  39). ti7 mng5-long5 e5 lai7-bin7, chit-peng5 u7 nng7 te3 toh, hit peng5 u7 nng7 te3 toh; ti7 hit teng2-bin7 thang lai5 thai5 sio-che3, siok8-choe7 che3, pou2-ke3-sit e5 che3 e5 seng-le2.  40). ChiuN7 kau3 ng3 pak e5 mng5-khau2, chit-peng5 e5 goa7-bin7 u7 nng7 te3 toh, mng5-long5 hit peng5 ia7 u7 nng7 te3 toh.  41). Ti7 mng5-piN chit-peng5 u7 si3-te3 toh, hit-peng5 u7 si3-te3 toh, kiong7 poeh te3; ti7 hit teng2-bin7 thai5 seng-le2.  42). Ui7-tioh8 sio-che3 e5 lou7-eng7 e5 si3 te3 toh, si7 chioh8 phah--e5, tng5 tiu2-poaN3, khoah tiu2-poaN3, koaiN5 chit8-tiu2; thai5 sio-che3 kap chiah e5 che3, sou2 eng7 e5 khi3-ku7 he7 ti7 hit teng2-bin7.  43). U7 kau, khoah chit8 pa-chiuN2, teng3-tiau5 ti7 lai7-bin7 e5 si3-ui5; toh-teng2 u7 che3-bah.  44). Lai7-mng5 e5 goa7-bin7, pak-mng5-piN e5 lai7-iN7, u7 pang5-keng; ui7-tioh8 chhiuN3-koa e5 lang5 lai5 siat; hiah e5 pang5-keng ng3-lam5, tang-mng5-piN ia7 u7 chit8-keng ng3-pak.  45). I ka7 goa2 kong2, Chit-keng ng3-lam5 e5 pang5 si7 hou7 tam-tng kou3-chhu3 e5 che3-si eng7.  46). Hit-keng ng3-pak e5 pang5 si7 hou7 tam-tng kou3-toaN5 e5 che3-si eng7; chiah-e5 si7 Li7-bi7 chok8-tiong Sat-tok e5 kiaN2-sun, chiu7-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hok8-sai7--e5.  47). I koh niu5 hit e5 iN7, tng5 chit8-pah tiu2, khoah chit8-pah tiu2; si7 su3-hong--e5; toaN5 si7 ti7 chhu3-cheng5.
	48). I chhoa7 goa2 kau3 chhu3-cheng5 e5 leng2-long5, niu5 leng2-long5 e5 tak8 ki thiau7, chit-peng5 gou7 tiu2, hit-peng5 gou7 tiu2. Mng5 e5 khoah, chit-peng5 saN tiu2, hit-peng5 saN tiu2.  49). Leng2-long5 tng5 ji7-chap8 tiu2, khoah chap8-it tiu2; u7 lang5 peh-chiuN7 e5 kia7-a2; hiah e5 thiau7-piN, koh u7 soe3-ki thiau7; chit-peng5 chit8 ki, hit-peng5 chit8-ki.

[41]	I koh chhoa7 goa2 kau3 tian7 hia, niu5 hiah e5 thiau7; chit-bin7 khoah lak8-tiu2, hit-bin7 khoah lak8-tiu2; khoah oeh8 kap pou3-piN5 saN-tang5.  2). Mng5-khau2 khoah chap8 tiu2; mng5 e5 siang-peng5-piN, chit-peng5 gou7 tiu2, hit-peng5 gou7 tiu2, i niu5 i e5 tng5 si3-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8 tiu2.  3). I kau3 lai7-bin7, niu5 mng5-khau2 e5 thiau7, nng7 tiu2; mng5-khau2 lak8-tiu2, mng5-khau2 e5 khoah chhit tiu2.  4). I niu5 i e5 tng5 ji7-chap8 tiu2, khoah ji7-chap8 tiu2, ti7 tian7 e5 cheng5-bin7; i tui3 goa2 kong2, Che si7 chi3-seng3-sou2.  5). I niu5 chhu3 e5 chhiuN5 lak8 tiu2, chhu3 si3-chiu-ui5 e5 piN-pang5, kok khoah si3 tiu2.  6). PiN-pang5 u7 saN-chan3, chit-chan3 thah8 ti7 hit-chan3 e5 teng2-bin7, tak8-chan3 u7 saN-chap8 keng; chit e5 chhu3 leng7-goa7 u7 chit8 phiN3 chhiuN5, choe3 si3-ui5 piN-pang5 e5 lou7-eng7, hou7 i e5 iN5-a2 thang khoa3 ti7-hia, bian2-tit khoa3 ti7 chhu3 e5 chhiuN5.  7). Chiah e5 si3-ui5 e5 piN-pang5, na2-koaiN5 na2-khoah; in-ui7 chhu3 e5 ui5 ti7 chhu3 e5 si3-bin7 na2-koaiN5, sou2-i2 chhu3 e5 khoah tit8-tit8 kau3 teng2-bin7; tui3 e7-chan3 kau3 teng2-chan3, tioh8 tui3 tiong-chan3 chiuN7--khi3.  8). Goa2 koh khoaN3-kiN3 chhu3 e5 si3-ui5 u7 koaiN5 e5 gim5; piN-pang5 e5 toe7-ki, koaiN5 chiok-chiok chit8 ko-chhioh, chiu7-si7 lak8 toa7-tiu2.  9). PiN-pang5 goa7-bin7 e5 chhiuN5, kau7 gou7 tiu2; sou2 chhun e5 toe7 chiu7-si7 chhu3 e5 piN-pang5 e5 sou2-chai7.  10). Si3-bin7 ui5 chhu3 hiah e5 pang5-keng, saN-li7 ji7-chap8 tiu2 e5 khoah.  11). PiN-pang5 e5 mng5 long2 ng3 sou2 chhun e5 toe7; chit8 e5 mng5 ng3-pak, chit8 e5 mng5 ng3-lam5; si3-ui5 sou2 chhun e5 toe7, long2 khoah gou7 tiu2.  12). Ti7 sai-peng5 leng7-goa7 keh-khui e5 toe7 thau5-cheng5 e5 chhu3-theh8 khoah chhit-chap8 tiu2; i e5 chhiuN5 si3-ui5 kau7 gou7 tiu2; tng5 kau2-chap8 tiu2.  13). An2-ni, i niu5 chhu3, tng5 chit8-pah tiu2; ia7 niu5 keh-khui e5 sou2-chai7, kap sou2 khi2-cho7--e5, kap i e5 chhiuN5, kiong7 tng5 chit8-pah tiu2.  14). Chhu3 e5 cheng5-bin7, kap ng3-tang keh-khui e5 toe7, khoah chit8-pah-tiu2.
	15). I niu5 au7-bin7 keh-khui e5 toe7 thau5-cheng5 e5 chhu3-theh8, i2-kip8 chit-peng5 hit-peng5 lau5 e5 long5, tng5 chit8-pah tiu2; koh niu5 lai7-tian7, kap iN7 e5 long5.  16). I e5 hou7-teng7, i e5 koaiN-bat8 e5 thang-a2, i e5 si3-ui5 saN-chan3 e5 lau5 e5 long5; ti7 hou7-teng7 e5 tui3-bin7, si3-ui5 e5 chhiuN5 long2 aN2 chha5-pan2; tui3 thou5-kha kau3 thang-a2, (thang-a2 long2 u7 jia-kham3),  17). tit8-kau3 mng5 e5 teng2-bin7, chiu7-si7 kau3 lai7-bin7 e5 chhu3 kap goa7-bin7, lai7-goa7 si3-ui5 e5 chhiuN5-piah, long2 chiau3 chhun3-chhioh.  18). U7 khek ki-lou7-peng kap chang-chhiu7, nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng e5 tiong-kan u7 chit8-chang5 e5 chang-chhiu7; ki-lou7-peng tak8-e5 u7 nng7 e5 bin7;  19). chit-peng5 u7 lang5 e5 bin7, ng3 chang-chhiu7, hit-peng5 u7 sai e5 bin7, ng3 chang-chhiu7; chhu3-lai7 si3-ui5 long2 si7 an2-ni.  20). Tui3 thou5-kha kau3 mng5-teng2, long2 u7 khek ki-lou7-peng kap chang-chhiu7; tian7 e5 chhiuN5 long2 si7 an2-ni.  21). Tian7 e5 mng5-khia7 si7 su3-hong--e5; chi3-seng3-sou2 e5 cheng5-bin7, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 tian7 e5 khoan2-sit.  22). ToaN5 si7 chha5-choe3--e5, koaiN5 saN tiu2, tng5 nng7 tiu2, i e5 kak, i e5 cho7, kap i e5 si3-piN long2 si7 chha5-choe3--e5; i tui3 goa2 kong2, Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 e5 toh.  23). Tian7 kap chi3-seng3-sou2 u7 nng7 e5 mng5.  24). Tak8 e5 mng5 u7 nng7-siN3, chit e5 nng7-siN3 si7 oe7 au2-tit--e5; chit e5 mng5 nng7-siN3, hit e5 mng5 ia7 nng7-siN3.  25). Tian7 e5 mng5-teng2 u7 khek ki-lou7-peng kap chang-chhiu7, kap khek ti7 chhiuN5-teng2--e5 chit8-iuN7; ti7 goa7-bin7 long5 e5 thau5-cheng5 u7 kau7 e5 chha5-pan2.  26). Long5 e5 piN-thau5, chit-peng5 hit-peng5, long2 u7 koaiN-bat8 e5 thang-a2 kap chang-chhiu7; chhu3 e5 piN-pang5, kap kau7 e5 chha5-pan2, long2 si7 an2-ni.

[42]	I chhoa7 goa2 chhut-lai5 kau3 goa7-iN7; koh chhoa7 goa2 jip8 leng7-goa7 keh-khui e5 toe7 saN-tui3-bin7 e5 pang5; hit keng pang5 ng3-pak, ti7 chhu3-theh8 e5 tui3-bin7.  2). Ti7 chit8-pah tiu2 tng5, gou7-chap8 tiu2 khoah e5 thau5-cheng5, u7 pak-mng5.  3). Siok8 lai7-iN7 ji7-chap8 tiu2 e5 tui3-bin7, koh siok8 goa7-iN7 phou-chioh8-toe7 e5 tui3-bin7, u7 lau5 e5 long5 tui3 lau5 e5 long5, saN-chan3.  4). Ti7 hiah e5 pang5 e5 thau5-cheng5 u7 chit8-tiau5 lou7, khoah chap8 tiu2, ng3 lai7-bin7 chit8-pah tiu2 e5 lou7; in e5 mng5 long2 ng3-pak.  5). Teng2-chan3 e5 pang5 khah oeh8, in-ui7 hou7 lau5 e5 long5 chiam3 i e5 toe7; pi2 tiong-chan3, e7-chan3, chiam3 khah-choe7.  6). In-ui7 i u7 saN-chan3, chong2-si7 bo5 thiau7, chhin-chhiuN7 hiah e5 iN7 e5 thiau7; sou2-i2 i e5 teng2-chan3 pi2 toe7-piN5 e5 e7-chan3 tiong-chan3 khah-oeh8.  7). Koh ti7 goa7-bin7 e5 pang5 e5 piN-thau5, ng3 hit e5 pang5 e5 thau5-cheng5 e5 goa7-iN7, tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2.  8). In-ui7 goa7-iN7 chiah e5 pang5, tng5 gou7-chap8 tiu2; khoaN3 ah, tian7 e5 thau5-cheng5 u7 chit8-pah tiu2.  9). Ti7 pang5 e5 e7-bin7, tui3 tang-peng5 u7 jip8-khi3 e5 sou2-chai7; chiu7-si7 lang5 tui3 goa7-iN7 oe7 jip8-khi3 hia.  10). Ng3-lam5 ti7 iN7 e5 chhiuN5 e5 khoah, ti7 keh-khui e5 sou2-chai7 tui3-bin7, ia7 ti7 chhu3-theh8 e5 tui3-bin7, u7 hiah e5 pang5;  11). i e5 thau5-cheng5 u7 lou7, in chhin-chhiuN7 ng3-pak e5 pang5 e5 khoan2-sit; tng5 khoah long2 saN-tang5; chhut-jip8 e5 sou2-chai7, long2 chiau3 in e5 khoan2-sit, ia7 chiau3 in e5 mng5.  12). Chiau3 ng3-lam5 hiah e5 pang5 e5 mng5, ti7 lou7 e5 thau5 u7 mng5, chiu7-si7 tang--si3 e5 chhiuN5 bin7-cheng5 e5 lou7, ti7 jip8-khi3 e5 sou2-chai7.  13). I ka7 goa2 kong2, Keh-khui e5 sou2-chai7 e5 thau5-cheng5, chiah e5 pak--si3 e5 pang5, lam5--si3 e5 pang5, long2 si7 seng3 e5 pang5; chhin-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 che3-si beh ti7-hia chiah8 chi3-seng3 e5 mih8; ia7 eng7 chi3-seng3 e5 mih8, chiu7-si7 sou3-che3, siok8-choe7-che3, pou2-ke3-sit e5 che3, he7 ti7 hit sou2-chai7, in-ui7 chit sou2-chai7 si7 seng3.  14). Che3-si jip8-khi3 e5 si5, chiu7 m7-thang tui3 seng3-sou2 chhut-lai5 kau3 goa7-iN7; tioh8 ti7-hia pang3-he7 in kiaN5 chit-hun7 e5 si5 sou2 chheng7 e5 saN; in-ui7 he si7 seng3; tioh8 oaN7 in e5 saN, chiah thang kau3 siok8 ti7 peh-siN3--e5.  15). I niu5 lai7-chhu3 beng5-pek8, chiu7 chhoa7 goa2 chhut ng3-tang e5 mng5, niu5 i e5 si3-ui5.  16). I eng7 ko-chhioh niu5 tang-hng, chiu7-si7 eng7 ko-chhioh niu5 i e5 si3-ui5, gou7-pah ko-chhioh.  17). I eng7 ko-chhioh niu5 pak-hng, niu5 i e5 si3-ui5, gou7-pah ko-chhioh.  18). I eng7 ko-chhioh niu5 lam5-hng gou7-pah ko-chhioh.  19). I oat8 kau3 sai-hng eng7 ko-chhioh niu5--i, gou7-pah ko-chhioh.  20). I niu5 i e5 si3-hng, si3-ui5 u7 chhiuN5, tng5 gou7-pah, khoah gou7-pah, lai5 hun-piat seng3--e5 kap peng5-siong5--e5.

[43]	Au7-lai5 i chhoa7 goa2 kau3 chit8 e5 mng5, chiu7-si7 ng3-tang e5 mng5.  2). KhoaN3 ah, I2-sek-liat8 Siong7-te3 e5 eng5-kng tui3 tang--si3 lai5; I e5 siaN chhin-chhiuN7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 siaN; toe7 chiu7 in-ui7 I e5 eng5-iau7 lai5 hoat-chhut kng.  3). I e5 khoan2-sit si7 chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 khoan2-sit, chiu7-si7 goa2 cheng5 lai5 beh biat8 siaN5 e5 si5 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 khoan2-sit; hit e5 iN7-siong7 ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 ti7 Ka-pa-lou2 ho5-piN sou2 khoaN-kiN3 e5 iN7-siong7; goa2 chiu7 phak-loh8 toe7.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tui3 ng3-tang e5 mng5 jip8 ti7 tian7-lai7.  5). Tui3 an2-ni sin5 chiu7 ku2-khi2 goa2, toa3 goa2 jip8 lai7-iN7; khoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng chhiong-moa2 tian7-lai7.  6). Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 u7 chit8-ui7 tui3 tian7-lai7 ng3 goa2 kong2-oe7; u7 chit8-lang5 khia7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-piN.  7). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, che si7 Goa2 po2-cho7 e5 sou2-chai7, si7 Goa2 kha-chiuN2 sou2 tah8 e5 toe7, Goa2 beh ti7-chia tiam3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan kau3 eng2-oan2.  I2-sek-liat8-ke kap in e5 kun-ong5 bo5 beh koh eng7 in e5 im5-heng7 i2-kip8 in e5 kun-ong5 e5 sin-si ti7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5;  8). in he7 in e5 mng5-teng7 kun7-oa2 Goa2 e5 mng5-teng7, in e5 mng5-khia7 kun7-oa2 Goa2 e5 mng5-khia7; in kap Goa2 e5 tiong-kan put-ko3 keh chit8-choa7 chhiuN5; koh eng7 in sou2 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 seng3-mia5; sou2-i2 Goa2 siu7-khi3 lai5 biat8 in.  9). TaN in tioh8 tui3 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tu5--khi3 in e5 im5-heng7 kap kun-ong5 e5 sin-si li7-khui hng7-hng7, Goa2 chiu7 tiam3 ti7 in e5 tiong-kan kau3 eng2-oan2.
	10). Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 tioh8 chiong chit e5 tian7 chi2-si7 I2-sek-liat8-ke, hou7 in in-ui7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7-koa3 lai5 kian3-siau3; in ia7 tioh8 niu5 tian7 e5 kui-bou5.  11). In na7 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 it-chhe3 sou2-kiaN5 e5 su7 lai5 kian3-siau3, li2 tioh8 chi2-si7 in chit e5 tian7 e5 bou5 kap i e5 khoan2-sit, i chhut e5 sou2-chai7, i jip8 e5 sou2-chai7, kap i it-chhe3 e5 kui-bou5, i it-chhe3 e5 le2-gi5, i it-chhe3 e5 kui-bou5, i it-chhe3 e5 hoat-tou7, long2 sia2 ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5; hou7 in siu2 it-chhe3 e5 kui-bou5, it-chhe3 e5 le2-gi5 lai5 kiaN5 i.  12). Tian7 e5 hoat-tou7 chiu7-si7 an2-ni, ti7 soaN-teng2 si3-ui5 e5 kai3-lai7 long2 choe3 chi3-seng3.  KhoaN3 ah, che chiu7-si7 tian7 e5 hoat-tou7.
	13). I2-ha7 si7 toaN5 e5 niu5-sou3, si7 eng7 tiu2 niu5 i; (chit8 e5 tiu2 si7 chit8 tiu2 koh ke chit8 pa-chiuN2); toaN5-toe2 chit8-tiu2, khoah chit8-tiu2, si3-ui5 e5 kiN5 u7 ian7, koaiN5 chit8 pa-chiuN2; che chiu7-si7 toaN5 e5 cho7.  14). Tui3 oa2 thou5-kha e5 toe2-cho7 kau3 e7-chan3 e5 khat, koaiN5 nng7 tiu2, khoah chit8 tiu2, tui3 soe3-khat kau3 toa7-khat koaiN5 si3 tiu2, khoah chit8-tiu2.  15). Teng2-bin7 e5 toaN5 u7 si3 tiu2; toaN5 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 thong2 si3 ki kak.  16). ToaN5 tng5 chap8-ji7 tiu2, khoah chap8-ji7 tiu2, khoan2-sit su3-hong.  17). Si3-bin7 e5 khat, tng5 chap8-si3 tiu2, khoah chap8-si3 tiu2; si3-ui5 e5 ian7 u7 poaN3-tiu2; i e5 toe2-cho7 si3-ui5 chit8-tiu2; i e5 kia7-chan3 ng3-tang.
	18). I tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: Khi2-cho7 che3-toaN5 ui7-tioh8 beh ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7 hian3 sio-che3, hiu3-huih; kau3 cho7-chiaN5 e5 si5 i e5 le7 chhin-chhiuN7 e7-toe2.  19). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 tioh8 chiong chit8 chiah kang e5 gu5-a2, choe3 siok8-choe7 e5 che3, kau hou7 che3-si Li7-bi7-lang5, Sat-tok e5 hou7-e3, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 chhin-kun7 Goa2 hok8-sai7 Goa2 e5.  20). Li2 tioh8 chhu2 gu5-a2 e5 huih, boah ti7 toaN5 e5 si3-kak, kap khat-a2 e5 si3-kak; kap si3-ui5 e5 ian7; an2-ni lai5 hou7 i chheng-khi3, koh ui7-tioh8 i siok8-choe7.  21). Li2 ia7 tioh8 chiong hit chiah choe3 siok8-choe7-che3 e5 gu5-a2, sio ti7 seng3-sou2 e5 goa7-bin7, chhu3-lai7 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 sou2-chai7.  22). Te7-ji7-jit8 tioh8 chiong bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5 soaN-iuN5-kong2 hian3 choe3 siok8-choe7 e5 che3; in beh chheng-khi3 hit e5 toaN5 chhin-chhiuN7 bat eng7 kang e5 gu5-a2 chheng-khi3 i chit8-iuN7.  23). Li2 i2-keng chheng-khi3 i, tioh8 hian3 chit8-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 kang e5 gu5 kap iuN5-kun5 tiong chit8-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 kang e5 mi5-iuN5.  24). Li2 tioh8 chiong chiah e5 mih8 hian3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, che3-si tioh8 eng7 iam5 sam2 ti7 in teng2-bin7, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 sio-che3.  25). Chhit-jit8-lai7 mui2-jit8 li2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 chit8-chiah kang e5 soaN-iuN5 choe3 siok8-choe7 e5 che3; in ia7 tioh8 pi7-pan7 chit8-chiah kang e5 gu5-a2 kap iuN5-kun5-tiong chit8-chiah kang e5 mi5-iuN5, long2 bo5 ha5-chhu5--e5.  26). Lek8-ke3 chhit-jit8 in beh ui7 toaN5 siok8-choe7, hou7 i chheng-khi3; an2-ni hun-piat i choe3 seng3.  27). Hiah e5 jit8 i2-keng moa2, tui3 te7 poeh-jit8 i2-au7 che3-si beh ti7 toaN5-teng2 hian3 lin2 e5 sio-che3 kap peng5-an e5 che3; Goa2 beh chiap-lap8 lin2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[44]	I koh toa3 goa2 to3-tng2 kau3 seng3-sou2 e5 goa7-bin7 ng3-tang e5 mng5; hit e5 mng5 koaiN--teh.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Chit e5 mng5, tek-khak tioh8 koaiN, m7-thang khui; bo5-lun7 sim2-mih8 lang5 m7-thang tui3-hia jip8, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, i2-keng tui3-hia jip8; sou2-i2 tioh8 tng5-tng5 koaiN--teh.  3). Lun7-kau3 jin5-kun, in-ui7 i si7 jin5-kun, thang che7 ti7 hit lai7-bin7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 chiah8 piaN2; i tioh8 tui3 chit e5 mng5 e5 long5 jip8, ia7 tioh8 tui3-hia chhut.  4). I koh toa3 goa2 tui3 pak-mng5 kau3 tian7 e5 thau5-cheng5; goa2 chiu7 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng chhiong-moa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 tian7; goa2 chiu7 phak-loh8 toe7.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, Goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 kong2-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tian7-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 le2-gi5 hoat-tou7 li2 tioh8 chu3-i3, eng7 bak8-chiu khoaN3, eng7 hi7-khang thiaN, ia7 tioh8 chu3-i3 tian7-tng5 jip8 e5 sou2-chai7, kap seng3-sou2 it-chhe3 chhut-khi3 e5 sou2-chai7.  6). Li2 ia7 tioh8 tui3 hiah e5 poe7-gek8-e5, tui3 I2-sek-liat8-ke, kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8-ke ah, lin2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 tioh8 liah8-choe3 kau3-giah8;  7). lin2 hian3 Goa2 e5 piaN2 kap iu5 kap huih e5 si5, lin2 chhoa7 hiah e5 sim bo5 siu7 kat-le2, seng-khu ia7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 goa7-pang lang5 jip8 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, lai5 phah la5-sam5 Goa2 e5 tian7, koh poe7 Goa2 e5 iok, ke-thiN lin2 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  8). Lin2 ia7 bo5 chin7-tiong ti7 kou3-siu2 Goa2 seng3-mih8 e5 chit-hun7; si7 ui7-tioh8 lin2 pun2-sin phai3 pat8-lang5 ti7 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 kou3-siu2 Goa2 kau-tai3 lin2 e5 chit-hun7.  9). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, I2-sek-liat8 chok8-tiong e5 goa7-pang lang5, chiu7-si7 sim bo5 siu7 kat-le2, seng-khu bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 goa7-pang lang5, long2 m7-thang jip8 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2.  10). Tng I2-sek-liat8 kiaN5 be5-lou7 e5 si5, u7 Li7-bi7 lang5 li7-khui Goa2 hng7-hng7, chiu7-si7 kiaN5 be5-lou7 li7-khui Goa2 khi3 te3 in e5 ngou2-siong7; in tioh8 tam-tng in e5 choe7-koa3.  11). Chong2-si7 in beh ti7 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2 choe3 chhe-eng7, koan2-li2 tian7-tng5 e5 mng5, ti7 tian7-lai7 choe3 chhe-eng7; ui7-tioh8 peh-siN3 thai5 sio-che3 kap che3-su7 e5 cheng-siN, beh khia7 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 hok8-sai7 in.  12). Ki3-jian5 ti7 in e5 ngou2-siong7 e5 bin7-cheng5 choe3 peh-siN3 e5 chhe-eng7, koh choe3 that-gai7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8-ke ham7-loh8 choe7-koa3; sou2-i2 Goa2 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2 kong-kek in, in beh tam-tng in e5 choe7-koa3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  13). In boe7 thang chhin-kun7 Goa2, tui3 Goa2 kiaN5 che3-si e5 chit-hun7, ia7 m7-thang chhin-kun7 Goa2 chit8-kiaN7 seng3-mih8, chiu7-si7 chi3-seng3 e5 mih8; in beh tam-tng in e5 kian3-siau3 kap in sou2 kiaN5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7.  14). Chong2-si7 Goa2 beh hou7 in tam-tng kou3-siu2 tian7 e5 chit-hun7, pan7-li2 ki5-tiong it-chhe3 e5 su7, kap hit lai7-bin7 sou2 tioh8 choe3 e5 kang.
	15). I2-sek-liat8 chok8 kiaN5 be5-lou7 li7-khui Goa2 e5 si5, che3-si Li7-bi7 lang5, Sat-tok e5 kiaN2-sun, iu5-goan5 kou3-siu2 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, in beh chhin-kun7 Goa2, hok8-sai7 Goa2, koh khia7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5, eng7 iu5 kap huih hian3 hou7 Goa2; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  16). In beh jip8 Goa2 e5 seng3-sou2, chiu7-kun7 Goa2 e5 toh, hok8-sai7 Goa2, siu2 Goa2 sou2 kau-tai3 in choe3--e5.  17). In jip8 lai7-iN7 e5 mng5 e5 si5 tioh8 chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN; in ti7 lai7-iN7 e5 mng5 kap ti7 tian7-lai7 kiaN5 chit-hun7 e5 si5, long2 m7-thang chheng7 iuN5-mng5 e5 i-hok8.  18). In e5 thau5-khak-teng2 tioh8 ti3 iu3-toe7-pou3 e5 bo7, kha-thui2 tioh8 chheng7 iu3-toe7-pou3 e5 khou3; hit e5 oe7 lau5-koaN7-e5 long2 m7-thang chheng7.  19). In chhut-khi3 kau3 goa7-iN7, chiu7-si7 kau3 goa7-iN7 e5 peh-siN3 hia, tioh8 thng3 kiaN5 chit-hun7 e5 i-hok8 he7 ti7 seng3 e5 pang5-keng, chheng7 pat8-ho7 e5 i-hok8, bian2-tit eng7 in e5 saN hou7 peh-siN3 chiaN5-seng3.  20). In m7-thang thi3-thau5, ia7 m7-thang hou7 thau5-mng5 hoat tng5-tng5; tok8-tok8 tioh8 chian2 thau5-mng5.  21). Che3-si jip8 lai7-iN7 e5 si5 long2 m7-thang lim-chiu2.  22). Ia7 m7-thang chhoa7 koaN2-hu7 kap siu7 li5-chhut e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 choe3-bou2; tok8-tok8 tioh8 chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 chok8-tiong e5 chai7-sek-lu2 a2-si7 che3-si e5 koaN2-hu7.  23). In tioh8 hou7 Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 chai seng3-e5 kap peng5-siong5-e5 e5 cheng-chha; koh hou7 in hun-piat bo5 chheng-khi3-e5 kap chheng-khi3-e5.  24). U7 saN-ko3 e5 su7 in tioh8 khia7-teh phoaN3-toan3, tioh8 chiau3 Goa2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 lai5 phoaN3-toan3; ti7 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 choeh-ki5 tioh8 siu2 Goa2 chiah e5 hoat-tou7 lut8-le7; ia7 tioh8 siu2 Goa2 chiah e5 an-hioh-jit8 choe3-seng3.  25). In m7-thang kun7-oa2 si2-lang5, phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7; tok8-tok8 thang ui7-tioh8 lau7-pe7, lau7-bu2, kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, hiaN-ti7, kap iau2-be7 chhut-ke3 e5 chi3-be7 phah la5-sam5 ka-ki7.  26). I i2-keng chheng-khi3 liau2-au7, tioh8 ka7 i koh sng3 chhit-jit8.  27). Tng i jip8 seng3-sou2 kau3 lai7-iN7 e5 jit8, beh ti7 seng3-sou2 hok8-sai7, tioh8 ui7 pun2-sin hian3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  28). In tek-khak u7 san2-giap8, Goa2 si7 in e5 san2-giap8; m7-thang ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong hou7 in ki-giap8, Goa2 si7 in e5 ki-giap8.  29). Sou3-che3, siok8-choe7-che3, pou2-ke3-sit-che3, in long2 thang chiah8 i; I2-sek-liat8 tiong sou2 hian3 it-chhe3 e5 mih8 long2 kui ti7 in.  30). KiN3-na7 khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 mih8 e5 te7-it e5, kap it-chhe3 le2-mih8-tiong e5 le2-mih8, long2 kui ti7 che3-si; lin2 ia7 tioh8 eng7 khi2-thau5 chhut e5 beh8-hun2 hou7 che3-si, thang hou7 hok-khi3 lim5-kau3 li2 e5 ke.  31). Bo5-lun7 chiau2 a2-si7 siu3, kiN3-na7 ka-ki7 si2--e5, a2-si7 siu7 peh-thiah--e5, che3-si long2 m7-thang chiah8.

[45]	Lin2 liam-khau pun toe7 choe3-giap8, tioh8 hian3 chit8-hun7 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 choe3-seng3, tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng ko-chhioh, khoah chit8-ban7 ko-chhioh; i e5 kai3 e5 si3-ui5 long2 choe3-seng3.  2). Ki5-tiong hun-piat chit8-toaN7 choe3 seng3-sou2, tng5 gou7-pah, khoah gou7-pah, i e5 khoan2-sit su3-hong; si3-ui5 koh gou7-chap8 tiu2 choe3 kau-ia2 e5 toe7.  3). Ti7 sou2 niu5-e5 e5 tiong-kan li2 tioh8 niu5, tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, khoah chit8-ban7; hit tiong-kan u7 seng3-sou2, chiu7-si7 chi3-seng3--e5.  4). Che si7 choan5-toe7 chit8-hun7 e5 seng3-toe7; tioh8 kui ti7 che3-si, chiu7-si7 choe3 seng3-sou2 e5 chhe-eng7, kun7-oa2 lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5; chit e5 toe7 thang choe3 in khi2-chhu3 e5 sou2-chai7, kap seng3-sou2 e5 seng3-toe7.  5). Iu7-koh chit8-hun7, tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, khoah chit8-ban7, tioh8 kui ti7 tian7-lai7 choe3 chhe-eng7 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, choe3 in e5 giap8, ji7-chap8 keng pang5.  6). Lin2 tioh8 hun-phai3 choe3 siaN5 e5 giap8, khoah gou7-chheng, tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, kap sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 saN-pai5; che si7 beh choe3 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke e5 lou7-eng7.  7). KiN3-na7 kui ti7 jin5-kun--e5 si7 ti7 sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 i2-kip8 siaN5 e5 giap8 chit-peng5 hit-peng5, ti7 sou2 hian3 seng3-toe7 e5 thau5-cheng5 kap siaN5 e5 giap8 e5 thau5-cheng5, tui3 sai-hng ng3-sai, tui3 tang-hng ng3-tang; i e5 tng5 tioh8 kap in e5 chit8 chi-phai3 e5 hun7-giah8 saN-tang5, tui3 sai-kai3 kau3 tang-kai3.  8). Ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 keng2-lai7 jin5-kun beh tit-tioh8 chit-e5 choe3 ki-giap8; au7-lai5 Goa2 chiah e5 jin5-kun bo5 koh khi-ap Goa2 e5 peh-siN3; beh eng7 toe7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8-ke chiau3 in e5 chi-phai3.
	9). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 jin5-kun ah, lin2 taN kau3-giah8--lah; tioh8 tu5--khi3 kiong5-po7 kap chhiuN2-kiap e5 su7, peng2-kong kiaN5-gi7; bo5 koh pa3-chiam3 peh-siN3 e5 giap8; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  10). Lin2 tioh8 eng7 kong-to7 e5 thian-pheng5, kong-to7 e5 i-hoat, kong-to7 e5 pa3-tek.  11). I-hoat kap pa3-tek tioh8 piN5-toa7, hou7 pa3-tek thang toe2 ho7-mui5-ni2 chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, i-hoat ia7 thang toe2 ho7-mui5-ni2 chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7; long2 eng7 ho7-mui5-ni2 choe3 phiau-chun2.  12). Sia3-khek-lek8 tioh8 choe3 ji7-chap8 kui3-lah8; ji7-chap8 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, ji7-chap8-gou7 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chap8-gou7 e5 sia3-khek-lek8 si7 choe3 lin2 e5 bi2-na2.  13). Lin2 sou2 eng-kai hian3 e5 le2-mih8 tioh8 an2-ni; sio2-beh8 chit8 ho7-mui5-ni2 tioh8 hian3 i-hoat lak8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, toa7-beh8 chit8 ho7-mui5-ni2 tioh8 hian3 i-hoat lak8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7;  14). lun7-kau3 iu5 e5 teng7-le7, tui3 iu5 e5 pa3-tek, chiu7-si7 tui3 chit8 kho-ni2, chiu7-si7 chap8 e5 pa3-tek, koh si7 chit8 ho7-mui5-ni2, hian3 chit8 pa3-tek chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7; in-ui7 chap8 pa3-tek, chiu7-si7 chit8 ho7-mui5-ni2;  15). tui3 I2-sek-liat8 pui5 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 ti7 iuN5-kun5-tiong mui2 nng7-pah chiah iuN5 tioh8 hian3 chit8 chiah iuN5-ko, choe3 sou3-che3, sio-che3, sia7-un-che3, thoe3 in siok8-choe7; che chiu7-si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.  16). Keng2-lai7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 eng7 chit e5 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 jin5-kun.  17). Jin5-kun e5 pun2-hun7 ti7 choeh-ki5, tak8-geh8 e5 chhoe-it, tak8-pai2 an-hioh-jit8 kap I2-sek-liat8 ke-tiong sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 choeh-ki5 tioh8 hian3 sio-che3, sou3-che3, koan3-tian7-che3; i tioh8 pi7-pan7 siok8-choe7-che3, sou3-che3, sio-che3, kap peng5-an-che3, ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8-ke siok8-choe7.
	18). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2, Ti7 chiaN-geh8 chhoe-it lin2 tioh8 chhu2 bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5 gu5-kang2, lai5 chheng-khi3 seng3-sou2.  19). Che3-si tioh8 chiong siok8-choe7-che3 e5 huih boah ti7 tian7 e5 mng5-khia7, kap toaN5-khat e5 si3-kak, kap lai7-iN7 e5 mng5-khia7.  20). Hit-geh8 e5 chhoe chhit ia7 tioh8 an2-ni choe3 ui7-tioh8 chho3-gou7 hoan7-choe7-e5, kap gu5-gong7 lai5 hoan7-tioh8--e5, lai5 ui7-tioh8 tian7 siok8-choe7.
	21). ChiaN-geh8 chap8-si3, lin2 tioh8 siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh, siu2 chit e5 choeh chhit-jit8; tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3 e5 piaN2.  22). Hit-jit8 jin5-kun tioh8 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 kap kok-lai7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 pi7-pan7 chit8 chiah kang e5 gu5 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3.  23). Tng choeh-ki5 e5 chhit-jit8 i tioh8 pi7-pan7 sio-che3 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lian5-lian5 chhit-jit8, tak8-jit8 tioh8 eng7 chhit-chiah gu5-kang2 kap chhit chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, long2 bo5 ha5-chhu5--e5; tak8-jit8 ia7 tioh8 pi7-pan7 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3.  24). I ia7 tioh8 pi7-pan7 sou3-che3, chit8 chiah gu5-kang2 chit8 e5 i-hoat, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8 e5 i-hoat, mui2 i-hoat tioh8 iu5 chit8-him.  25). Chhit-geh8 chap8-gou7; siu2 choeh e5 si5 chhit-jit8 ku2 i tioh8 an2-ni choe3; chiau3 siok8-choe7-che3, chiau3 sio-che3, chiau3 sou3-che3, ia7 tioh8 chiau3 iu5.

[46]	Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: Lai7-iN7 ng3-tang e5 mng5 ti7 choe3-kang e5 lak8-jit8-lai7 tek-khak tioh8 koaiN; tok8-tok8 ti7 an-hioh-jit8 tioh8 khui, geh8 e5 chhoe-it ia7 tioh8 khui.  2). Jin5-kun tioh8 tui3 chit e5 mng5 e5 long5 tui3 goa7-bin7 jip8, khia7 ti7 mng5-khia7-piN; che3-si tioh8 pi7-pan7 i e5 sio-che3 kap i e5 sia7-un-che3, i tioh8 ti7 mng5-teng7 hit tah keng3-pai3; jian5-au7 chhut-khi3, chit e5 mng5 kau3 e5-hng-si5 m7-thang koaiN.  3). Ti7 chiah e5 an-hioh-jit8, kap geh8 e5 chhoe-it, kok-lai7 e5 peh-siN3 tioh8 ti7 chit e5 mng5-khau2 keng3-pai3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  4). Jin5-kun ti7 an-hioh-jit8 sou2 tioh8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sio-che3, tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5 iuN5-ko lak8-chiah, bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5 mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah;  5). i e5 sou3-che3 ui7-tioh8 hit chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2 tioh8 chit8 e5 i-hoat, ui7-tioh8 hiah e5 iuN5-ko e5 sou3-che3 si7 chiau3 i e5 lek8-liong7 chit8 e5 i-hoat phoe3 iu5 chit8 him.  6). Tng geh8 e5 chhoe-it tioh8 hian3 bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5 gu5-kang2 chit8-chiah, iuN5-ko lak8-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah; long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5--e5.  7). I ia7 tioh8 pi7-pan7 sou3-che3, ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2 hian3 chit8 e5 i-hoat, ui7-tioh8 mi5-iuN5-kang2 hian3 chit8 e5 i-hoat, ui7-tioh8 hiah e5 iuN5-ko chiu7 chiau3 i e5 lek8-liong7, chit8 e5 i-hoat phoe3 iu5 chit8-him.  8). Jin5-kun jip8-lai5 e5 si5, tioh8 tui3 chit e5 mng5 e5 long5 jip8, ia7 tioh8 tui3 chit e5 lou7 chhut.  9). Ti7 tak8 e5 choeh-ki5, kok-lai7 e5 peh-siN3 tiau5-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 si5, tui3 pak-mng5 jip8-lai5 keng3-pai3-e5 tioh8 tui3 lam5-mng5 chhut-khi3; tui3 lam5-mng5 jip8-lai5-e5 tioh8 tui3 pak-mng5 chhut-khi3; m7-thang tui3 sou2 jip8 e5 mng5 oat8-to3-tng2, tioh8 tit8-tit8 chin3-cheng5 chhut-khi3.  10). Peh-siN3 jip8-khi3 e5 si5, jin5-kun ia7 tioh8 ti7 in e5 tiong-kan jip8-khi3; peh-siN3 chhut-khi3, jin5-kun ia7 tioh8 kap in chhut-khi3.  11). Ti7 choeh-ki5 kap tai7-hoe7 e5 si5, sou3-che3 tioh8 ui7-tioh8 chit8-chiah gu5-kang2 hian3 chit8 e5 i-hoat, ui7-tioh8 chit8-chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2 hian3 chit8 e5 i-hoat, ui7-tioh8 hiah e5 iuN5-ko chiu7 chiau3 i e5 lek8-liong7, chit8 e5 i-hoat phoe3 iu5 chit8-him.  12). Jin5-kun na7 pi7-pan7 kam-sim e5 che3, sio-che3 a2-si7 sia7-un-che3 choe3 kam-sim e5 che3, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tioh8 u7 lang5 ka7 i khui ng3-tang e5 mng5, i tioh8 pi7-pan7 i e5 sio-che3 kap i e5 sia7-un-che3 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 an-hioh-jit8 sou2 choe3 chit8-iuN7; jian5-au7 i tioh8 chhut-khi3; chhut-khi3-liau2 tioh8 u7 lang5 ka7 i koaiN-mng5.  13). Tak8-jit8 li2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 bo5 ha5-chhu5, be7 moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-ko chit8-chiah, choe3 sio-che3 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; tak8 cha2-khi2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 i.  14). Tak8 cha2-khi2 ia7 tioh8 pi7-pan7 saN-kap hian3 e5 sou3-che3, chit8 i-hoat lak8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, kap chit8 him iu5 saN-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 chhiau-ho5 mi7-hun2; chit e5 sou3-che3 tioh8 siong5-siong5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, choe3 eng2-oan2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 le7.  15). Tak8 cha2-khi2 in tioh8 an2-ni pi7-pan7 iuN5-ko, sou3-che3, kap iu5, choe3 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3.
	16). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: Jin5-kun na7 chiong san2-giap8 hou7 i e5 kiaN2 e5 chit8-e5, chiu7-si7 choe3 i e5 giap8, kui ti7 i hiah e5 kiaN2, si7 in seng5-chiap choe3 giap8--e5.  17). Chong2-si7 i na7 chiong i e5 san2-giap8 e5 chit8-hun7 hou7 i e5 jin5-sin5 e5 chit8-e5, si7 choe3 jin5-sin5-e5 kau3 chu7-iu5 e5 ni5, hit-si5 iu5-goan5 kui ti7 jin5-kun; lun7-kau3 i e5 san2-giap8 tioh8 lau5 hou7 i hiah e5 kiaN2.  18). Jin5-kun m7-thang chhiuN2-toat8 peh-siN3 e5 san2-giap8, lai5 koaN2 in li7-khui in sou2 seng5-chiap-e5; i tioh8 tui3 ka-ki7 e5 giap8-tiong chiong san2-giap8 hou7 i e5 kiaN2; bian2-tit Goa2 e5 peh-siN3 si3-soaN3, tak8-lang5 li7-khui i sou2 seng5-chiap--e5.
	19). I chiu7 chhoa7 goa2 tui3 mng5-piN e5 lou7 jip8-lai5 kau3 che3-si ng3 pak hiah e5 seng3 e5 pang5-keng; khoaN3 ah, au7-bin7 sai-si3 u7 chit8 sou2-chai7.  20). I chiu7 ka7 goa2 kong2, Che si7 che3-si chu2 pou2-ke3-sit-che3 kap siok8-choe7-che3, i2-kip8 pek sou3-che3 e5 sou2-chai7; bian2-tit toa3-kau3 goa7-iN7, hou7 peh-siN3 chiaN5-choe3 seng3.  21). I koh chhoa7 goa2 chhut-khi3 kau3 goa7-iN7, hou7 goa2 keng-ke3 iN7 si3 e5 kak-thau5; khoaN3 ah, ti7 hit e5 iN7 tak8 e5 kak-thau5 kok u7 chit8 e5 iN7.  22). Ti7 iN7 e5 si3 kak-thau5 u7 iN7, si3-bin7 u7 chhiuN5 ui5-teh; tak8 e5 iN7, tng5 si3-chap8 tiu2, khoah saN-chap8; si3 e5 kak-thau5 e5 iN7, in e5 chhun3-chhioh long2 chit8-iuN7.  23). Si3 e5 iN7 e5 chiu-ui5 u7 khi2 chit8-liat8, i e5 e7-bin7 long2 u7 chu2-mih8 e5 sou2-chai7.  24). I ka7 goa2 kong2, Chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 chu2-mih8 e5 chau3-kha; tian7-lai7 chiah-e5 choe3 chhe-eng7--e5 ti7-chia chu2 peh-siN3 e5 che3-su7.

[47]	I chhoa7 goa2 to3-tng2 kau3 tian7-mng5, khoaN3 ah, u7 chui2 tui3 tian7 e5 mng5-teng7-e7 ng3-tang lau5 chhut; in-ui7 tian7 e5 thau5-cheng5 ng3-tang; chiah e5 chui2 tui3 e7-bin7 tui3 tian7 e5 chiaN3-peng5, che3-toaN5 e5 lam5-peng5, lau5-loh8.  2). I chiu7 chhoa7 goa2 tui3 pak-mng5 chhut-khi3, chhoa7 goa2 tui3 goa7-bin7 oan kau3 goa7-mng5, tui3 ng3 tang-peng5 e5 mng5 e5 lou7; khoaN3 ah, chui2 tui3 chiaN3-peng5 piak-chhut-lai5.  3). Hit-lang5 chhiu2 theh8 chin5-soh, ng3-tang kiaN5 chhut-khi3 e5 si5, i chiu7 niu5 chit8-chheng tiu2, kah goa2 tui3 chui2 ke3--khi3, chui2 im kha-bak8.  4). I koh niu5 chit8-chheng, kah goa2 tui3 chui2 liau5--ke3 khi3, chui2 im kha-thau5-u.  Koh niu5 chit8-chheng, kah goa2 liau5--ke3-khi3, chui2 im kau3 io.  5). Koh niu5 chit8-chheng; chui2 chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 ho5, goa2 boe7-oe7 liau5--ke3-khi3; in-ui7 chui2 tiong3-tiN7, chiaN5-choe3 oe7 siu5--tit e5 chui2, boe7 liau5-tit e5 ho5.  6). I chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, Jin5-chu2 ah, li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit-e5 mah? I chiu7 chhoa7 goa2, hou7 goa2 oat8-tng2 kau3 ho5-piN.  7). Goa2 to3-tng2-khi3 e5 si5, khoaN3 ah, ti7 ho5-piN siang-peng5 u7 chhiu7-bak8 chin-choe7.  8). I ka7 goa2 kong2, Chiah e5 chui2 ng3-tang lau5-khi3, beh loh8 kau3 A-lah8-pa, tit8-tit8 lau5 kau3 hai2; sou2 hoat-chhut e5 chui2 beh lau5 jip8 iam5-hai2, hai2--nih e5 chui2 chiu7 pian3-ho2.  9). Ho5-chui2 sou2 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7, tak8-iuN7 siN-thoaN3 e5 tong7-but8 long2 beh tit-tioh8 oah8, ia7 beh u7 hi5 chin-choe7; in-ui7 chui2 lau5 kau3 hia, hai2--nih e5 chui2 pian3-ho2; hit e5 ho5 sou2 lau5 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7, sou2 u7 e5 mih8 long2 beh tit-tioh8 oah8.  10). Chiong-lai5 beh u7 tho2-hi5 lang5 khia7 ti7 hoaN7-piN; tui3 Un2-ki-ti2 kau3 Un2-i2-kek-lian5 long2 choe3 pha-bang7 e5 sou2-chai7, hiah e5 hi5 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-hai2 e5 hi5 chin-choe7.  11). Chong2-si7 noa7-thou5 e5 toe7 kap chui2-teh8 e5 sou2-chai7 boe7 tit-tioh8 i-ho2, lau5--teh chhut iam5.  12). Ti7 ho5 e5 siang-peng5-piN beh hoat-siN tak8-lui7 e5 chhiu7-bak8, thang choe3 chiah8-mih8, hioh8 boe7 kou-ta5, ke2-chi2 chhut bo5 tng7; tak8 geh8-jit8 beh kiat sin e5 ke2-chi2, in-ui7 chiah e5 chui2 si7 tui3 seng3-sou2 lau5-chhut-e5; chhiu7-teng2 e5 ke2-chi2 beh choe3 chiah8-mih8, hioh8 u7 i-ti7 e5 kong-iong7.
	13). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni kong2: Lin2 pun chit e5 toe7 choe3 giap8 chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3; i e5 toe7-kai3 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 e7-toe2; Iok-sek beh tit-tioh8 nng7 hun7.  14). Lin2 seng5-chiap chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8 tioh8 saN-kap piN5-pun; in-ui7 Goa2 bat kiah8-khi2 chhiu2 eng3-un2, chiong chit e5 toe7 hou7 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2; chit e5 toe7 beh kui ti7 lin2 choe3-giap8.  15). Toe7 e5 kai3-han7 chiu7-si7 an2-ni; pak-peng5 e5 kai3 tui3 toa7-hai2, khi3 Hi-tek8-lun5 e5 lou5, tit8-tit8 kau3 Se-tat8-tat8 chhut-jip8 e5 sou2-chai7;  16). kau3 Hap-ma2, Pi2-lo5-tha, Se-pek-lian5, chiu7-si7 ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 keng2-kai3 kap Hap-ma2 e5 keng2-kai3 e5 tiong-kan; kau3 Ho5-lan5 piN-kai3 e5 Hap-sat-hap-the5-kan.  17). Tui3 hai2 e5 keng2-kai3 chiu7-si7 Hap-sat-i2-lan5 kun7 ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 keng2-kai3, koh ti7 pak-peng5 ng3-pak si7 Hap8-boat e5 keng2-kai3; che si7 pak-peng5 e5 kai3.  18). Tang-peng5 e5 kai3 ti7 Ho5-lan5, Tai7-ma2-sek, Ki-liat8 kap I2-sek-liat8 toe7 e5 tiong-kan chiu7-si7 Iok-tan3-ho5; lin2 tioh8 tui3 pak-peng5 e5 kai3 niu5 kau3 tang-hai2; che chiu7-si7 tang--si3 e5 kai3.  19). Lam5-peng5 ng3-lam5 e5 kai3 si7 tui3 Tha-ma2 kau3 Bi2-li7-pa-ka-te-su e5 chui2, soa3 kau3 Ai-kip8 e5 khoe, thang3-kau3 toa7-hai2; che si7 lam5-peng5 ng3-lam5 e5 kai3.  20). Sai-peng5 e5 kai3 chiu7-si7 toa7 hai2, tui3 lam5-peng5 e5 keng2-kai3, tit8-kau3 Hap-ma2 chhut-jip8 tui3-bin7 e5 sou2-chai7; che chiu7-si7 sai-peng5 e5 kai3.  21). An2-ni lin2 tioh8 chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chi-phai3 ui7 ka-ki7 pun chit e5 toe7.  22). Lin2 tioh8 liam-khau pun chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8 kui ti7 lin2 pun2-sin kap ti7 lin2 tiong-kan kia3-kha e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, chiu7-si7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5; lin2 tioh8 khoaN3 in chhin-chhiuN7 I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 tiong-kan sou2 siN--e5 chit8-iuN7; in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 chi-phai3 e5 tiong-kan kap lin2 saN-kap tit-tioh8 toe7 choe3-giap8.  23). Goa7-bin7 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7 hit e5 chi-phai3 e5 tiong-kan, lin2 chiu7 ti7-hia pun toe7 hou7 i choe3-giap8; che chiu7-si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2--e5.

[48]	Chi-phai3 e5 mia5 chiau3 e7-toe2 sou2 ki3--e5; tui3 kek8-pak e5 kai3 tui3 Hi-tek8-lun5 e5 lou7, kau3 Hap-ma2 chhut-jip8 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek keng2-kai3 Hap-sat-i2-lan5 ng3-pak kun7-oa2 Hap-ma2 e5 toe7, tui3-tang kau3 sai; Tan3, chit8-hun7.  2). Oa2-kun7 Tan3 e5 toe7-kai3, tui3-tang kau3 sai; A-siat, chit8-hun7.  3). Oa2-kun7 A-siat e5 toe7-kai3, tui3 tang kau3 sai; Na2-hut-tha-li7, chit8-hun7.  4). Oa2-kun7 Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 toe7-kai3, tui3-tang kau3-sai; Ma2-na2-se, chit8-hun7.  5). Oa2-kun7 Ma2-na2-se e5 toe7-kai3, tui3-tang kau3-sai; I2-hoat-lian5, chit8-hun7.  6). Oa2-kun7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 toe7-kai3, tui3-tang kau3 sai; Liu5-pian7, chit8-hun7.  7). Oa2-kun7 Liu5-pian7 e5 toe7-kai3, tui3-tang kau3 sai; Iu5-tai7, chit8-hun7.
	8). Oa2-kun7 Iu5-tai7 e5 toe7-kai3, tui3-tang kau3 sai, si7 lin2 sou2 hian3 e5 toe7, khoah nng-ban7 gou7-chheng ko-chhioh, tui3-tang kau3-sai, tng5 kap hiah e5 hun7 e5 chit8-e5 saN-tang5, seng3-sou2 ti7 hit tiong-kan.  9). Lin2 sou2 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toe7 tioh8 tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng ko-chhioh, khoah chit8-ban7.  10). Sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 tioh8 kui hou7 che3-si; pak--si3 tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, sai--si3 khoah chit8-ban7, tang--si3 khoah chit8-ban7, lam5--si3 tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 seng3-sou2 ti7 hit tiong-ng.  11). Tioh8 kui hou7 Sat-tok e5 kiaN2-sun-tiong chiaN5-choe3 seng3 e5 che3-si, chiu7-si7 kou3-siu2 Goa2 sou2 kau-tai3--e5; tng I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kiaN5 be5-lou7 e5 si5, in bo5 kiaN5 be5-lou7 chhin-chhiuN7 Li7-bi7 lang5 kiaN5 be5-lou7.  12). Chit-e5 tioh8 kui hou7 in, chiu7-si7 tui3 sou2 hian3 e5 choan5-toe7-tiong hian3 hou7 in choe3 chi3-seng3--e5, oa2-kun7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 toe7-kai3.  13). Li7-bi7 lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 toe7 tioh8 tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, khoah chit8-ban7, kap che3-si e5 toe7-kai3 saN-tang5; long2-chong2 tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, khoah chit8-ban7.  14). Chit e5 toe7 m7-thang boe7, m7-thang tui3-oaN7, khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 mih8 m7-thang kui hou7 pat8-lang5; in-ui7 si7 kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3-seng3--e5.  15). Sou2-chhun gou7-chheng khoah e5 toe7, si7 ti7 hit e5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng e5 thau5-cheng5, tioh8 choe3 peng5-siong5 e5 lou7-eng7, thang khi2 siaN5, khi2 chhu3, choe3 kau-ia2 e5 toe7; siaN5 tioh8 ti7 tiong-ng.  16). I e5 chhun3-chhioh chiu7-si7 an2-ni; pak-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah, lam5-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah, tang-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah, sai-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah.  17). SiaN5 tioh8 kau-ia2; ng3-pak nng7-pah gou7-chap8, ng3-lam5 nng7-pah gou7-chap8, ng3-tang nng7-pah gou7-chap8, ng3-sai nng7-pah gou7-chap8.  18). I2-goa7 sou2 chhun e5 tng5 kap sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 saN-tang5, ng3-tang chit8-ban7, ng3-sai chit8-ban7; koh kap sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 saN-tang5; ki5-tiong sou2 chhut-san2 beh hou7 siaN5-lai7 choe3-kang e5 lang5 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  19). Tui3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 chi-phai3 e5 tiong-kan ti7 siaN5-lai7 choe3-kang--e5 beh ti7-hia cheng3-choh.  20). Lin2 sou2 hian3 e5 choan5-toe7, tng5 nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng, khoah nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng; lin2 sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 kap siok8 ti7 siaN5 e5 toe7 si7 su3-hong--e5.
	21). Sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 i2-kip8 siok8 ti7 siaN5 e5 toe7, siang-peng5 chhun e5 toe7 tioh8 kui ti7 jun5-kun, sou2 hian3 e5 toe7 ti7 hit nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng e5 thau5-cheng5 kau3 tang--si3 e5 kai3, koh ng3-sai ti7 hit nng7-ban7 gou7-chheng e5 thau5-cheng5 kau3 sai--si3 e5 kai3, kap hiah e5 hun7 e5 toe7 saN-tang5, long2 kui ti7 jin5-kun; sou2 hian3 e5 seng3-toe7 kap tian7 e5 seng3-toe7 long2 ti7 hit lai7-bin7.  22). Koh tui3 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 giap8, tui3 siok8 ti7 siaN5 e5 giap8, si7 siok8 jin5-kun-e5 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 Iu5-tai7 e5 kai3 kap Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 kai3 e5 tiong-kan, long2 kui jin5-kun e5.
	23). Lun7-kau3 ki5-u5 e5 chi-phai3; tui3-tang kau3-sai; Pian7-nga2-bin2, chit8-hun7.  24). Oa2-kun7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 toe7-kai3 tui3-tang kau3-sai; Se-bian7 chit8-hun7.  25). Oa2-kun7 Se-bian7 e5 toe7-kai3 tui3-tang kau3-sai; I2-sat-ka, chit8-hun7.  26). Oa2-kun7 I2-sat-ka e5 toe7-kai3 tui3-tang kau3-sai; Se-pou3-lun5, chit8-hun7.  27). Oa2-kun7 Se-pou3-lun5 e5 toe7-kai3 tui3-tang kau3-sai; Ka-tek, chit8-hun7.  28). Oa2-kun7 Ka-tek e5 toe7-kai3, lam5-peng5 ng3-lam5, hit e5 toe7-kai3 tui3 Tha-ma2 kau3 Bi2-li7-pa Ka-te7-su e5 chui2, kau3 Ai-kip8 e5 khoe thang3-kau3 toa7-hai2.  29). Che si7 lin2 tioh8 liam-khau pun hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chi-phai3 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, in tak8-e5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 giap8 chiu7-si7 an2-ni; che si7 Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5.
	30). Tui3 siaN5 chhut--khi3 e5 lou7 si7 chiau3 e7-bin7 sou2 ki3 e5; ti7 pak-bin7 chiau3 sou2 niu5--e5, si3-chheng gou7-pah ko-chhioh.  31). SiaN5 hiah e5 mng5 tioh8 chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 chi-phai3 e5 mia5; pak-bin7 u7 saN e5 mng5; Liu5-pian7 e5 mng5, chit8-e5; Iu5-tai7 e5 mng5, chit8-e5; Li7-bi7 e5 mng5, chit8-e5.  32). Tang-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah, u7 saN e5 mng5; Iok-sek e5 mng5, chit8-e5; Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 mng5, chit8-e5; Tan3 e5 mng5, chit8-e5.  33). Lam5-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah, u7 saN e5 mng5; Se-bian7 e5 mng5, chit8-e5; I2-sat-ka e5 mng5, chit8-e5; Se-pou3-lun5 e5 mng5, chit8-e5.  34). Sai-bin7 si3-chheng gou7-pah, u7 saN e5 mng5; Ka-tek e5 mng5, chit8-e5; A-siat e5 mng5, chit8-e5; Na3-hut-tha-li7 e5 mng5, chit8-e5.  35). SiaN5 si3-ui5 kiong7 chit8-ban7 poeh-chheng; tui3 hit-jit8 i2-au7 siaN5 e5 mia5 kio3-choe3, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7-hia.
